sAmAnyavibhAgena saha visheShavibhAgasya samuchchaye apishabdaH | asaN^gatirapyanekavidheti vA tridhaiva na tvekavidhaiva yenAsiddhayAdInAmantarbhAvo durghaTaH syAt.h | yadvA yAvanto.anumAnAbhAsAH paraparigaNitAstAvadbhedatAM ni(rAkartu)vataryitumevashabdaH | sarveShAmatraivAntarbhAvAt.h | 
traividhyaM darshayati- pratij~nArtheti ||
sAdhyadharmavishiShyo dharmI pratij~nArthaH | tasya pratispardhisadbhAvo viruddhatA | yatrArthe liN^gapramitiH sAdhyasiddhayupayoginI tatra tadabhAvo liN^garAhityam.h | vyApterabhAvo.avyAptiH | itishabdo.adhyAhAryaH | 
sAdhyasAdhanabhAvasambandhayogyatAviraho hi sAdhyasAdhanAbhimatayostadbhAvAsambhave bhavati | nacha sAdhanasya tadbhAve.api viruddhasya sAdhyatA sambhavati | nishitatve.api parashorAkAshasya ChedyatAbhAvAt.h | nApi sAdhyasya tathAtvasambhave.apyasamarthasya 
sAdhanatopapadyate | Chedyatve.api kAShThasya kuNThakuThArasya Chedana(ka)tvAbhAvAt.h | ataH pratij~nArthaviruddhatAdInAM yuktaM virodhitvam.h | 
astu liN^garAhityAvyAptyoryuktidoShatvam.h | pratij~nArthaviruddhatA tu kathaM taddoShaH | sAdhyasambandhitvAditi chenna | sAdhyAbhimatasya tadbhAvAsambhave sAdhanAbhimatasyAviShayavR^ittitvAt.h | nanvevaM sati siddhasAdhanatA.api virodha eva syAt.h | nahi siddhasya sAdhyatA sambhavati | nachAstviti vAchyam.h | uktaprakAratrayAnantarbhAvAt.h | siddhasAdhako.asaN^gata iti svavachanavirodhAchcheti | maivam.h | sati sAkAN^kShatve.anvayAyogyatvaM virodhaH | nacha siddhasAdhanasya sAkAN^kShatA astIti nAsau virodhe.antarbhavati | 
nanu chAnyatra trividho virodha ityAdinA liN^garAhityAvyAptyorekatAmupAdAya sAdhyasya sAdhanasya vA.anugamo dR^iShyAntavirodhastR^itIyatayA parigR^ihItaH | atrApi sAdhyasAdhanavaikalyaM dR^iShyAntasyeti vakShyati | tatkathametat.h | nachAtrApi tadadhyAhAreNa tathaiva vyAkhyAnaM yuktam.h | dR^iShyAntadoShasyAnumAnadoShatA.anupapatteH | nahi dR^iShyAnto.anumAnam.h | tathA.apyanumAnAN^gavyAptidUShakatayA.anumAnadoShatvamastu | dR^iShyAntasya sAdhyavaikalye sAdhanasya sAdhyaparityAgAt.h | sAdhanavaikalye tu vyApteranupadarshanAditi chenna | tathA satyavyAptyaiva saN^gR^ihItatvena tR^itIyatvAnupapatteriti | uchyate | svArthAnumAne hi dR^iShyavyAptikasya liN^gasya vivakShitasthale siddhimAtreNa sAdhyapramitirutpadyata iti tatparipanthinAM doShatvamabhipretya pratij~nArthaviruddhatAliN^garAhityAvyAptInAmatra grahaNam.h | parArthAnumAne(.apya)tvavyAptyaupayikasyApi dR^iShyAntadoShasya tadAshrayatayA pratItatvena tathaivodbhavanIyatAj~nApanAya tena saha trividhatvamanyatroktamiti na virodhaH | 
yadvA sAdhyasAdhanobhayAshrayahInasAdhyasAdhanobhayavyAvR^ittAshrayahInAnaShyau dR^iShyAntadoShAneke bhAShante | tannirAsAya dR^iShyAntadoShasya pR^ithagupAdAnam.h | tathAhi ubhayavikalastAvanna parisaN^khayeyaH | anyataravaikalyenaiva (dR^iShyAnta)duShyatAsiddhAvAdhikyaprasaN^gAt.h | anyathaikaikavikalaparisaN^khayAnAnupapatteH| kathaM tarhyanvayavyatirekIti chet.h | na kathaJNchidityuktameva | sAdhyAdyavyAptistu dR^iShyAntasya guNa eva na doShaH | sato hi satA vyAptiM pradarshayituM dR^iShyAnto.anveShyavyaH | vaidharmyadR^iShyAntasyAyaM doSha iti chetsa eva kimarthaH | vyatirekavyAptibodhayeti chenna | tasyAH sAkShAdanupayogAt.h | pAramparyeNopayogo tu sAdharmyadR^iShyAnta evAsAviti kiM pR^ithagupAdAnena | ubhayAvyAvR^ittashchAdhikyAnni(kyani)rastaH | AshrayahInastvAshrayAsiddhisamAnayogakShema iti dvAveva dR^iShyAntadoShau | asArvatrikashcha dR^iShyAntadoShaH | nahi sarvatra dR^iShyAnta eva vyAptirupadarshanIyetyasti niyamaH | AnumAnikAgamikavyAptestadanapekShaNAt.h | 
syAdetat.h | pratij~nArthaviruddhatayA hi kAlAtItaprakaraNasamau saN^gR^ihItau | liN^garAhityamityasiddhiH | avyAptishcha trividhA bhavati | sAdhanasya sAdhyena sambandhAbhAvaH | satyapi sambandhe tadabhAvenApi sambandhaH, sAdhyAbhAvavyA(pta)pyatA cheti | tadetattrayaM krameNAnadhyavasitA naikAntikaviruddhasaMj~nAM labhate | tathAcha paranirUpitaprastArasya samasanamevAnena kR^itaM syAt.h | nachAnena kimapi prayojanam.h | anyathA puruShamativaishvarUpyeNa prakriyAntarasyApi sAvakAshatvAt.h | nacha brahmatarkAditarkashAstramanusR^ityetthaM vyutpAdanamiti vAchyam.h | prayojanAbhAve.andhaparamparApatteriti | 
uchyate | asti prakriyAntarakaraNasya prayojanam.h | tathAhi | pratij~nArthaviruddhatayA hi svavAkyavirodhasyApi saN^grahaM vakShyati | nacha kAlAtItatvAdinA sa labhyate | api cha vyavahAro.api pratij~nArthaviruddhatayopapadyate, na kAlAtItatvAdinA, vaiyarthyaprasaN^gAt.h | asAdhakamidaM kAlAtItatvAt.h | satpratipakShatvAdityasya prabalasamabalapramANaviruddhatvAdityarthaH | nachAtra visheShaNasya kimapi prayojanamasti | hInabalasya pramANapadenaiva nirastatvAt.h | pramANatadAbhAsAviveka eva hi pramANashabdaprayogo na tvaprAmANyanishchaye | ahInabalatayA vA visheShaNe sambhavati tadavAntarabhedopAdAnaM niratharkameva | tathAchaikamevedaM dUShaNaM syAt.h | liN^garAhityagrahaNena chAdUShaNAnAmapi dUShaNatayA paraparigaNitAnAmAshrayavyadhikaraNasAdhyAnyathAsiddhInAM nirAso labhyate anyathAsiddherdUShaNatve.api prakArAntasya vakShyamANatvAt.h |   Vyasa-(13)

anadhyavasitatvAdibhedo.api kiM vyAptyabhAve sambhavatItyetAvatA parisaN^khayeyo vyavahAropayogitvAdvA | nAdyaH | vyarthavyutpAdanasyAtiprasaN^gitvAt.h | na dvitIyaH | vaiyarthyaprasakteH | nedaM sAdhakamanaikAntikatvAdityasya hi sapakShavR^ittitve sati vipakShavR^ittitvAdityarthaH | nachAtra visheShaNavyavachChedyaM kiJNchidasti | evaM viruddhatvAdityasya sapakShAvR^ittitve sati vipakShavR^ittitvAdityarthaH | tathAcha vaiyarthyameva | sAdhyaviparyayavyApyatvAdityatrApi sambandhamAtreNa kR^itArthatve vyAptigrahaNaM vyarthameva | evamavAntarabhedavyutpAdanamapi nirastam.h | shiShyamativaishadyAya vyutpAdanaM tvanumatameveti na svIyavyavahAravirodha iti | 
virodhavadasaN^gaterapi prabhedAH svayamevohanIyAH | 
evaM sAkShAdyuktidoShamabhidhAya vAchanikadoShamAha- nyUneti ||
nyUnashabdo bhAvapradhAnaH | yukterdUShaNamiti prakR^itamanuvartate | avashyavaktavyAparipUrtirnyUnatvam.h | kR^itakAryatvamAdhikyam.h | vachanadoShAttatpratipAditA yuktirapi duShyA syAdityetayorvAchanikatvam.h |
nanvayukto.ayaM vibhAgaH | virodhAsaN^gatyorapi vAchi(chani)katvAt.h | nahi kR^itakatvaM svayameva duShyam.h | anityatvasAdhane.api tathAtvApatteH | kR^ishAnushaityAdau tatheti chet.h | tatkiM kR^itakatvaM kR^ishAnushaityaM vA shabdanityatvaM vA sAdhayituM svayameva pravR^ittam.h | yena tatra duShyaM syAt.h | kinnAma tatsAdhanatayA shabdena pratipAdi(darshi)tam.h | evamasaN^gatAvapi siddhasAdhanatAdilakShaNAyAM vAchyamityAshaN^kAnirAsArthaM tushabdaH | nyUnAdhikye eva vAchanike, na virodhAsaN^gatI | svArthAnumAne.api darshanAditi bhAvaH | santu tarhi pratipattR^ipratipAdakayorevaite doShAH | yathA nishAtam.h kR^ishAnushaityAdau vyApArayanpuruSha evAparAdhI syAt.h natu kR^itakatvAdikamiti | 
maivam.h | kR^itakatvAderaduShyatve tadvayApArayato.apyaparAdhAnupapatteH | anyathA shabdanityatvasAdhane prayuJNjAno.apyaparAdhyeta | tataH kR^ishAnushaityAdeH sAdhyatAnarhatvaM nityatvAdisAdhane kR^itakatvAderasamarthatvamityAdirarthashabdagata eva doSho.aN^gIkaraNIyaH | na hyupAdhimantarbhAvya bhavan.h doSho na doSho bhavati | tathA sati bahuviplavApatteriti | 
nanu kathameta evAnumAnadoShAH | sopAdhikatvasyApyatiriktasya sattvAdityatastatsvarUpAnuvAdenoktAntarbhAvamAha- sAdhyeti ||
sAdhanasya yatsAdhyavyApakavailomyaM sA.avyAptiH | chashabdAtsatpratipakShatA cha | sAdhyasyAdharmasAdhanatvAdervyApako yo niShiddhatvAdidharmaH | yatrAdharmasAdhanatvaM tatra niShiddhatvamiti niyamAt.h | tena sAdhanasya hiMsAtvAdervailomyaM sAdhyApekShayA vaiparItyamavyAptatvamiti yAvat.h | yatra hiMsAtvaM tatra niShiddhatvamiti niyamAbhAvAt.h | vaidhahiMsAyAM satyapi hiMsAtve niShiddhatvAbhAvAt.h | tadanena sopAdhikatvasya svarUpamuktam.h | sAdhyavyApakatve sati sAdhanAvyApako hi dharma upAdhiH, tadvattvaM cha sAdhanasya sAdhyavyApakAvyApyatvameva | etatprAganumAnAdvayAptigrahaNavelAyAmavyAptireva | sAdhyavyApakaM parityajataH sAdhyaparityAgAvashyambhAvAt.h | nahi sAdhyamaparityajan.h tadvayApakaM parityajatIti yujyate | sAdhyaparityAgashchAvyAptireva | 
apare tu nirupAdhikaH sambandho vyAptiH | sopAdhikatve tu lakShaNAbhAvAdvayAptyabhAva ityAchakShate | tadasat.h | vyAptij~nAnAdhInamupAdhij~nAnaM tadadhInaM cha nirupAdhikatvaj~nAnaM tadAyattaM vyAptij~nAnamiti chakrakaprasaN^gena tasya vyAptilakShaNatvAnupapatteH | tatkiM sApAdhikasyApyasti vyAptiH | maivam.h | vyAptatvAnupAdhikatvayoH samaniyame.api vyAptibodhAnaN^gatayopAdhyabhAvasya lakShaNatvAnupapatteruktatvAt.h | 
nanvevaM chetkathaM sAdhyasAdhanavyavahAraH | AgAmisambhAvanApekShayeti brUmaH | vastutastu yo dharmo yadvayApakAvyAptastasya tenAvyAptirityeva vaktavyam.h | anumAnapravR^ittyuttarakAlaM tu satpratipakShataiva | sAdhanasya sAdhyavyApakaparityAgo hi pakShAdanyatra vA syAtpakShe vA | na tAvadAdyaH | tathA sati sphuTavyabhichAraparityAgenopAdhyudbhAvanasyAnavasaratvAt.h | dvitIye tu sAdhyavyApakasya pakShAdvayAvR^ittiH sAdhyamapi vyAvartayatIti satpratipakShataiva |
etenopAdhyabhAvasya pratipakShatve nopAdherdUShaNatvam.h | nahi yadabhAvo yatra dUShaNaM so.api tatra dUShaNamiti yukta virodhAditi parAstam.h | pakShavyAvR^ittiprAdhAnyenaivopAdhitvAt.h | etadarthaM cha sAdhyavyApakasya vailomyaM pakShAdvayAvR^ittiH sAdhanasya satpratipakShateti yojanIyam.h | bhAvapradhAnasyAdoShatvaM tviShyameva | 
nanu cha prAganumAnAdapi satpratipakShatA.anumAnottaramavyAptirvA kinna syAt.h | maivam.h | pakShe hi sAdhyasyopasaMhAre pratipakShAvasaraH | nacha vyAptigrahaNasamaye pakShAdipravibhAgo.astIti kathaM tadA pratipakShatvaM syAt.h | anumAnottaramavyAptiH kathamiti vaktavyam.h | sAdhyavyApaka upAdhiH pakShAdvayAvartamAnaH sAdhyamapi vyAvartayati | tathAcha sAdhyarahite tatra vartamAnaM sAdhanaM sAdhyaM vyabhicharatIti chenna | tathA sati bAdhitasatpratipakShayorapi vyabhichAritApAtAt.h | omiti chenna | nirasiShyamANatvAt.h | bAdhapratipakShAbhyAmevAnumAnadUShaNasambhave kiM tadupajIvinA vyabhichAreNeti chet.h, tarhi vyApakavyAvR^ittyA pratipakSheNaivAnumAne dUShite kiM tadupajIvinA vyabhichAreNeti tulyam.h |
kiJNcha pakShe vyabhichAraH kiM nishchita uta sandigdhaH | nAdyaH | vikalpAnupapatteH | tathAhi | pakShe sAdhyAbhAvo nishchito na vA | Adye kiM pramANAntareNota sAdhyavyApakopAdhivyAvR^ittyA | prathame tata evAnumAnaM duShyamiti kimupAdhinA | na dvitIyaH | parasparAshrayatvaprasaN^gAt.h | upAdheH sAdhyavyApakatvanishchaye tadvayAvR^ittyA sAdhyavyAvR^ittinishchayaH sati cha tasminnasAviti | 
neti pakShe sAdhyavyApakatvAnishchayAt.h upAdheH, kathaM tadvayAvR^ittyA pakShe sAdhanasya nishchito vyabhichAraH syAt.h | pakShe sandigdho vyabhichArastu svata eva siddho sopAdhimukhanirIkShaNApekShaH | sarvAnumAnochChedahetushcha | tasmAdanumAnottarakAlaM satpratipakShataivetyuchitam.h | etadevAbhipretya "sa evopAdhidoSho.api' ityAdivachanAt.h | 
anukUlatarkAdinA sAdhyavyApakatvanishchaye sati pakShe nishchitavyabhichAritAsiddhiriti chenna | nishchisAdhyavyApakavyAvR^itterbAdhakatvena tata evAnumAne dUShite vyabhichAravaiyarthyAt.h | tathA.api sopAdhikatvaM satpratipakShatvamiti gataH pakSha iti chenna | pratipakShasya yAvajjIvaM tadbhAvAnaN^gIkArAt.h | sAmarthyAnirdhAraNAyAmeva satpratipakShaH, nirdhArite tu sAmarthye bAdhako vA syAt.h, bAdhyo veti ko nAma nAbhyupaiti |
atra sopAdhikatvamiti vaktavye sAdhyavyApakavailomyamiti vachanamupAdhilakShaNasyApi pradarshanArtham.h | tadapi sAdhyasamavyApakatvapakShanirAsAya | nanveSha pakShaShyIkAkR^itA.aN^gIkR^itaH | maivam.h | paramatAnuvAdatvAt.h | anyathaikasAdhyAvinAbhAva ityudayanavachanodAharaNavaiyarthyAt.h | dUShaNaM tu sphuTatvAnnoktam.h | tathA hi | samapadaM kiM viShamavyAptikavyavachChedArthamuta prayojanAntarArtham.h | nAdyaH | pArthivaparamANurUpAdayo nityAH paramANuvisheShaguNatvAt.h ApyaparamANurUpAdivadityAdau pR^ithivIvisheShaguNatvAbhAvAderviShamavyAptikasyApyupAdhitvena tadvayavachChedasyAyuktatvAt.h | pratipakShonnAyakatvasambhavena dUShaNatvAchcha | viShamavyAptikasyopAdhitve pakShetaratvasyApi tatprasaN^ga iti chet.h | tatkimuktavisheShaNadvayopetaM na vA | neti pakShe tata evAnupAdhitvam.h | Adye tu tasyApyupAdhitve ko doShaH | parvatetaratvAdeH sarvatra sambhavena naivamiti chenna | anumAnavyAptyAdigrAhakapramANaprAbalye sati sAdhyavyApakatvabhaN^gAt.h | tadabhAve chAnumAnabhaN^gasyeShyatvAt.h | anyathA shabdo.abhidheyaH prameyatvAdghaTavadityAdAvashabdatvAdeH samavyAptikapakShetarasyAnirAsaprasaN^gAt.h | tadidamiShyamapi tyajati aniShyamapi gR^ihNAtIti na visheShaNam.h |
yadapyayuktam.h | "svasambandhena yaHsvIyaM dharmamanyatra yojayet.h | sa upAdhiryathA loke japAdiH sphaTikAdiShu | ihApyavyApyahetvarthavyApyatvabhramahetutA | upAdheH syAttadA tasya samavyAptiryadA bhavet.h' iti | tatra vaktavyam.h | kimanenoktaM bhavati | kiM viShamavyAptikasya vyApyatvAbhAvAttatsambandhena sAdhanAbhimate vyApyatAbhramAnupapatteradoShatvena tadvayavachChedAya samapadamiti, kiMvA.anvarthopAdhishabdasampAdanArthamiti | nAdyaH | pratipakShonnAyakatvena dUShaNatvasambhave svagatavyAptyavabhAsakatAbhAvasyAdoShatvAt.h | sAdhyasAhacharyadarshanenaiva vyApyatAbhramasambhavAchcha | na dvitIyaH | upAdhishabdasambandhasya svakapolakalpitatvAt.h | ata eva bhagavAnAchAyarvaryaH sopAdhikatvamityanabhidhAya sAdhyavyApakavailomyamityAha | vyavahArAstu parakR^itasaN^ketenApi nirvahaNIyaH | yadvA kvachitsAdhyavyApyatAsadbhAvenopAdhitve.anyatrApi gauNyA vR^ittyA upAdhivyavahAropapattiH | ata eva na dvitIyo.api | 
nanu cha viShamavyAptikasya pratipakShonnAyakatvaM na sambhavati | kvachitpakShetaraviparyayasyAsAdhAraNatvAditi | maivam.h | asAdhAraNatvasya dUShaNatvAsammateH | sammatau vA tatropAdhitvAbhAvasya vyutpAdanAt.h | yatropAdhiH pakShaikadeshAdvayAvartate tatra kathaM pratipakShaH | bhAgAsiddhiprasaN^gAt.h | nachAsau nopAdhiH | pakShaikadeshAdvayAvR^ittyApi sAdhanAvyApakatvasambhavAt.h | nachAyaM samavyAptipakShe.asti doShaH | upAdhimatyekadeshe sAdhyasadbhAvaniyamena taM vihAyaikadeshAntarasyaiva pakShIkaraNauchityAditi | uchyate | asmAbhirapyupAdhivyAvR^ittimA(nevaika)nekadeshaH pakShIkriyate | ekadeshAntare.api yadi sAdhyasammatistadA tasyApakShIkaraNameva | asammatau tu tatra doShAntarameva bhaviShyatIti kimanupapannam.h |
nanu shaN^kitopAdhau kathaM pratipakShaH sandigdhAsiddhiprasaN^genAsamabalatvAditi chenna | pAkShikasiddhayAdinA satpratipakShatAphalasya saMshayasyAnivAraNAt.h | saMshayAnaN^gatvamevAsamabalatvamabhipretam.h | 
syAdetat.h | sAdhyavyApakatve sati sAdhanAvyApakatvaM kimupAdhisAmAnyalakShaNaM kiMvA visheShalakShaNam.h | nAdyaH | samavAyaH samavetaH sambandhatvAtsaMyogavadityatra sAdhanAvachChinnasAdhyavyApakakR^itakatvopAdhyavyApanAt.h | vAyuH spArshano.anudbhUtarUpAnadhikaraNatve satyupalabhyamAnasparshAdhikaraNatvAdghaTavadityatra dravyatvAvachChinnasAdhyavyApakachAkShuShatvopAdhyavyApteshcha | nacha sAdhanAvachChinnasAdhyavyApakasya yatkiJNchidavachChinnasAdhyavyApakasya cha nopAdhitvamiti vAchyam.h | tatra tatrAchAryairaN^gIkR^itatvAt.h | vyatirekopAdhyavyApakatvAchcha | na dvitIyaH | sAmAnyalakShaNAntarasya vaktavyatApAtAt.h | na chAnvayavyatirekidharmatvaM taditi vAchyam.h | tasyAtrAyamupAdhiriti vyavahArakAraNatvAbhAvAt.h | tathAtve cha lakShaNavaiyarthyAditi |
atra brUmaH | idameva sAmAnyalakShaNam.h | sAdhyapadenAvachChinnAnavachChinnasAdhyasyAbhidhAnAt.h | nacha tatra pratipakShAsambhavaH | yadavachChinnasAdhye ya upAdhistadvayAvR^ittestadvishiShyAbhAve hetutvopapatteH | yathA samavAyaH sambandhatve sati samavetatvena hIno.akAryatvAdAkAshavat.h | vAyurdravyatve sati spArshanatvena hIno.achAkShuShatvAdAkAshavaditi | 
nachAtra sAdhyavisheShaNavaiyarthyam.h | shabdo na sparshavadvisheShaguNaH pratyakShatve satyakAraNaguNapUrvakatvAdityAdAviva vyabhichAraparihArArthatvAt.h | kvachitsAdhyAvachChedakAvachChinnasyopAdhyabhAvasya hetutvAt.h | yathA vAyuH spArshano na bhavati dravyatve satyachAkShuShatvAditi | vyatirekavyAptau tUktamevottaram.h | sAdhyasAdhanapadAbhyAM cha prakR^itayoreva vivakShitatvAnna kashchitkShudropadravaH | yo yatsAdhyavyApako yatsAdhanAvyApaka iti vA.asyArtha iti sarvaM sustham.h | 
nanu cha sopAdhikatvasya satpratipakShatve.api tenaivAnumAnadoShAdhikyamiti | maivam.h | pratij~nArthaviruddhatetyanenaiva prabalapramANaviruddhatAlakShaNakAlAtIta(tA)vatsamabalapramANaviruddhatAyAH satpratipakShatAyA api saN^gR^ihItatvAt.h | pratispardhisadbhAvamAtraM hi pratij~nArthaviruddhatetyuktam.h | evaM tarhi durbalena virodho.api pratij~nArthaviruddhatA syAt.h, uktalakShaNopetatvAdityata Aha- durbaleneti ||
ayamarthaH | prakaraNAdivashAddhi sAmAnyashabdA api visheShe vatarnta iti prasiddham.h | yathA vishiShyasamaye puruShamAnayetyukte puruShavisheSha evAnIyate na tu yaH ko.api puruShaH | prakR^ite chAnumAnasyAsAdhakatvanimittaparisaN^khayAnam.h | nacha durbalena virodhe.apyanumAnamasAdhakaM bhavati | prabalavirodhAdinA tasyaivAbhAsatvAt.h | yathA vimatashchakShuShmAnrUpAparokShaj~nAnitvAdityatra vimato.andhaH puruShatvAditi | ataH sAmAnyashabdaprasakto.api durbalena virodho (nAnumAnasAdhyakatAvachChinnapra) na prathij~nArthaviruddhatA | kintu prabalasamabalapramANaviruddhataiva (iti) | 
nanvevamAdhikyanirAse.api nAnumAnavirodhatraividhyaM sambhavati | pratij~nAvirodhasyAvyAptyaiva gatatvAt.h | virodhenaiva sAdhyavirahiNi pakShe vartamAnasya hetorarvyAptibharvati | nahi viredhasyAvyAptyasaN^kIrNamudAharaNamasti | yatra tu virodhasambhavastatrAvyApterevAnyatrAvadhR^itasAmarthyAyA dUShaNatvAt.h | virodhasyAvyAptyutthApanena charitArthatvAdityAshaN^kAM bhikShu(ka)pAdapra(sAraNanyAyena)sAraNena pariharati- svavAkyeneti ||
pramANamityanuvartate | na kevalaM pramANavirodhe, kintu svavAkyena virodhe.api pramANaM naiva sAdhakatAM vrajet.h | evashabdena pareShAmapi siddho.ayamartha iti darshayati | yathoktam.h | avirodhigrahaNAtpratyakShAnumAnagamasvashAstrasvavachanavirodhino nirastA iti (bhavanti iti) | 
etaduktaM bhavati | pratij~nArthavirodho dvedhA bhavati | pramANavirodhaH svavAkyavirodhashcheti | tatrAdyaH prabalasamabalapramANavirodhAtmA dvividho bhavati | dvitIyo.apyapasiddhAntajAtibhedena dvedhA | jAtishcha svavachanavirodhasvanyAyavirodhasvakriyAvirodhabhedena tredhA | tatrAstAM tAvatpramANavirodhaH | svavAkyavirodhagrahaNaM tAvatpR^ithakkaraNIyam.h | tasyApyavyAptyutthApane vyApArAyogAt.h | svavAkyavirodhe hi kiM sAdhanasyobhayAbhimatyA (pakShe) vyabhichAro bhavet.h, kiMvA.anyarAbhimatyA | nAdyaH | svavAkyaprAmANyasyobhayAsammateH | na dvitIyaH | tasya svataHsiddhatvena svavAkyavirodhAnapekShatvAt.h | adoShatvAchcha | tasmAdaviShayavR^ivi(tAhetu)tvena pratij~nArthaviruddhatA pR^ithageva patisaN^khayAtavyeti |
kiJNchAyaM na kevalaM vyAptyapekShapravR^itteranumAnasyaiva doShaH | kinnAma tadanapekShasya pratyakShAderapi tathA chAnyatropalabdhasAmarthyasyAnumAne.api svAtantyasiddhirityAshayavatA prastAvAdanumAnamiti vaktavye pramANamityevAdhikR^itam.h | 
etenaitadapi (parA)nirastam.h | astu svavAkyavirodhasya pR^ithagdoShatvamavyAptyutthApakatvAyogAt.h | bAdhapratirodharUpaH pramANavirodhastu na svatantradoShaH | pramANavirodhe hi heturapakShadharmo vA syAt.h anaikAntiko vA (syAt.h) | jij~nAsitadharmaNo dharmiNaH pakShatvAt.h | pramANAvagatasAdhyaviruddhadharmavatashchApakShatvena taddharmasyApakShadharmatvaniyamAt.h | sAdhyadha(rma)rmiNyeva pramANopasthApitasAdhyadharmaviruddhadharmavati darshanena vyabhichArAt.h | nacha sapakShavipakShAvevAnvayavyatirekagamyAvinAbhAvadarshanaviShayau na pakSha iti sAmpratam.h | yadi hi pakShaM vihAya bahirevAvinAbhAvo.avagamyate tadA bahivyarAptibalena pakShadharmo.api heturna pakShe sAdhyaM sAdhayet.h | asiddhA hi tatra tasya sAdhyena vyAptiH | tasmAdantarbahirvA savaropasaMhAreNAvinAbhAvo.avagantavyaH | evaJNcha siddhaH pakShe vyabhichAraH sAdhanadharmasya | 
nanu pratirodhe katham.h | tatrApi vyAptigrAhakasya pramANasya prAbalyam.h | ubhayatrApi pramANasadbhAve vyApyatvAsiddhAvantarbhAvAditi | pramANavirodhasya pramANAntare.apyaviShayavR^ittitAhetutvenAvagatasvatantradUShaNabhAvasyAnumAne.api tathaivAN^gIkartumuchitatvAt.h | 
api cha kiM vyAptigrahaNasamaye.avyApterupasthApakaH pramANavirodhaH syAt.h, utAnumAnapravR^ittyuttaramapi | AdyastviShyata eva | "mAnabAdhe na tadbhavet.h' iti vakShyamANatvAt.h | na dvitIyaH | upajIvyaparityAgenopajIvakasvIkArasyAyuktatvAt.h | pramANaviruddhasyApakShadharmatve siddhasAdhanasyApi tathAtvaM syAt.h | samAnanyAyatvAt.h | omiti chenna | svArthAnumAne.api siddhasAdhanasya doShatvApatteH | nahi pakShadharmatA.asiddhiH parArtha evAnumAne doShaH | tasmAt.h parAnAkAN^kShitatvAdasaN^gata eva siddhasAdhana iti |
|| ityanumAnadoShanirUpaNam.h || 
evamanumAnadoShAnnirUpya prasaN^gAtparanirUpitAsheShanigrahasthAnAnAmapi virodhAdiShvevAntarbhAva ityAha- saMvAdeti ||
nigR^ihyate parAjIyate ebhiriti nigrahAH nigrahasthAnAni | nanu cha pratij~nAhAnyAdInAM vaktR^idoShANAM kathamarthavachanadoSheShu virodhAsaN^gatinyUnAdhikyeShvanupravesha ityata uktam.h- saMvAdAnuktisaMyuktAM iti || tathA.apyanupapattireva | virodhAdichatuShyayasyAnumAnadoShatvenoktatvAt.h | nigrahasthAnAnAM cha niyamenAnumAnAshrayatvAbhAvAt.h | nahi punaruktiranumAna eva sambhAvinI | prashnAdAvapyupapatterityato.astyatra visheSha iti tushabdenAha | dvividhaM hi virodhAdichatuShyayam.h | samayabandhAdikathAsarvarUpasAdhAraNamasAdhAraNaM cha | tatrAnumAnasyaiva yadasAdhAraNaM virodhAdi tatrAnumAnadoShANAM sarveShAM pravesho.abhihitaH | sAdhAraNe tu sarvanigrahasthAnAnAmiti na kashchidvirodhaH | 
yadvA kathAbAhyAdInAmeShAM nigrahasthAnatAvyavachChedArthastushabdaH | 
nanu keyaM kathA nAmetyapekShAyAM tatsvarUpaM nirUpayansAmAnyalakShaNaM vibhAgamuddeshaM chAha- vAda iti ||
atra katheti lakShyapadamAvartanIyam.h | vichAragocharetyupaskartavyam.h | vijAnatAmiti jAtau bahuvachanam.h | tathA chAnekavidva(tkartR^i)dvaktR^ikavichAragocharA kathA vAkyasandR^iddhiH(ndarbhaH) katheti sAmAnyalakShaNasiddhiH | tAshcha kathA vAdAdibhedena tisraH trividhA ityarthaH | vijAnatAM matena tisra iti vA | tena nyUnAdhikasaN^khayoktistadvirodhAdayuktetyuktaM bhavati | 
vAdalakShaNamAha- svArthamiti ||
tattvanirNayasAdhanItyarthAdyarthajalpavitaNDAvyavachChedaH | tathA.api vitaNDAvisheShe.ativyAptistadarthaM kevalamityuktam.h | sAkShAdityarthaH | tushabdena tattvanirNayasAdhanAdapi jalpavisheShAt.h taduddeshena pravR^ittatvavailakShaNyaM darshayita | yadA tu viditatattvau vItarAgAvaviditatattvaiH parairabhyarthitau kathAM kurutastadA tatrAvyAptemetallakShaNam.h | nachAsau na vAdaH | anyatrAnantarbhAvena tisra ityasya vyAghAtAdityata uktam.h- svArthaM parArthamapi veti || apishabda ubhayArthatAsamuchchayArthaH | 
jalpalakShaNamAha- jalpa iti ||
Adipadena khyAtyAdergrahaNam.h | arthAdivyapekShayeti vAdavyAvR^ittyartham.h | AnuShaN^gikArthAdisAdhanatvaM vAdasyApi sambhavatIti vyapekShAgrahaNam.h | vitaNDAvyAvR^ittyarthaM satAmeveti | satAmityevokte na vitaNDAvyAvR^ittisiddhiH | vitaNDAyAmapyekasya sattvAt.h | bahuvachanasya jAtyarthatvAt.h | tena evetyuktam.h | 
vitaNDAM lakShayati- vitaNDeti ||
tushabdo vAdajalpavyavachChedArthaH | kathetyanuvartate | kartR^ibhedena kathAbhede.atiprasaN^ga ityato lakShaNAntaramAha- aprakAshyeti || sadbhiH svasiddhAntamaprakAshyAsAdhayitvA.asatAM pakShasya dUShaNameva kriyate yatsA vitaNDetyarthaH | prativAdinaH svapakShasAdhanena vinA parapakShapratikShepamAtreNa paryavasyantI kathA vitaNDetyuktaM bhavati | nanvetadeva kinnimittam.h | prAshnikAdyadhInamiti brUmaH | te.api kuta etAdR^ishaniyamaM kuryuriti chet.h(na) | tattvaj~nAnAyogyAnasataH prati sadbhiH svasiddhAntasAdhane teShAM tattvaj~nAnotpAdaprasaN^gAt.h | tasya cha niShiddhatvAdityAshayenAsatAmityuktam.h | etena prathamalakShaNasyApi samarthanaM veditavyam.h | 
nanvasambhavIdaM lakShaNam.h | parapakShadUShaNaM hi tatpratipAdakapramANadUShaNenaiva bhavet.h | nacha svapakShasAdhanahInAyAM vitaNDAyAM tatsambhavatItyata Aha- ukta iti ||
tairasadbhiH prathamaM svapakShasAdhanAya mAne ukte sati sadbhistasya mAnasya dUShaNaM vaktavyam.h | asato vAdibhUtasya svapakShasAdhanaM parapakShanirAkaraNaM cha karaNIyam.h | satastu prativAdinaH tatpramANadUShaNenaiva charitArthatvamityuktaM bhavati |
kvachitsatAmevetyAdisArdhashloko vAdajalpayorityataHparaM paThitaH | tata etAmeva saN^gatimAshritya TIkAkR^itA tatraiva vyAkhyAtaH |
kiJNcha gurushiShyAdayo.asamAnavidyA api vAde.adhikriyante | tattvanirNayArthitvAt.h | jalpavitaNDayostu sambhAvitasamAnavidyayorevAdhikAraH | "yayoreva samaM vittaM yayoreva samaM shrutam.h | tayorvivAho vAdashcha nottamAdhamayoH kvachit.h' 
iti smaraNAt.h | vAdo jalpavitaNDAlakShaNo vivAdaH | anyathA.atyantApakR^iShyo.apyutkR^iShyatamena vaiyAtyAt.h ghaTamAno yadi vA daivAyattamabhibhAvayet.h tadA vR^ithAkhyAtiM labheta | tathAcha prAshnikAdInAmasuj~nAtvaM pratyavAyashcha syAt.h | apUjyaH pUjyate yatreti vachanAt.h | evaM cha vAdAjjalpavitaNDayorbhedaH | nanvetadayuktam.h | parabuddherapratyakShatvena vidyAsAmyavaiShamyayorj~nAtumashakyatvAditi chenna | jalpavitaNDArthinorvidyAsAmyAdeH parIkShayA nishchayopapatteH | tadetadAha- vidyeti |
vidyAparIkShA pUrvA kAraNabhUtA yasyAH sA tathoktA | vidyAparIkShayA nishchitasAmyayoreva vitaNDA dAtavyA, na viShamavidyayoH | jalpashchaivam.h vidyAparIkShApUrvaM eveti vyAkhyeyam.h | dvitIyaivashabdo vAdavyAvR^ittyarthaH | samAnavidyayorevetyayaM niyamo na vAde.astIti |
nanu jalpavitaNDArthinovirdyAsAmyAdinishchayAya kartavyA parIkShA kiM kathayA, utAnyathA | nAnyathA | anyonyasaN^gharShaNena vinA tadasiddheH | Adye.api kiM vAdena jalpavitaNDAbhyAM vA | na prathamaH | khyAtyAdikAmayoH spardhAvatorvAdAnupapatteH | na dvitIyaH | anavasthApAtAditi chenna | vAdena tAvadvidyAparIkShaNasyeShyatvAdityAshayavAnvAdasya vidyAparIkShAyAM kAra(tatkAra)NatvamanvayavyatirekAbhyAM sAdhayitumupodghAtaM tAvadAha- uchcheti || 
yato vidyayochchatvena nirNItatvameva jayo nIchatvena nirNItatvaM cha parAjaya ityarthaH | iti vidyAparIkShaNaM vAdeneti vakShyamANenAnvayaH | 
evamupayuktamabhidhAya vyatirekamAha- vinaiveti ||
nirNIyate.anayeti nirNItistattvasya nirNItistattvanirNItirvAda iti yAvat.h | tattvanirNItiM vinochchanIchatvavij~nAnaM na hItyevokte vinA vAdeneti vakShyamANavirodhaH syAt.h | ato jalpAdinetyuktam.h | itishabdastasmAdityarthe | vidyAparIkShaNaM vAdeneti vakShyamANamatrApi sambaddhayate | yadyapi satsAdhanopalambhe jalpe.api bhavati vAdinoruchchanIchatvavij~nAnam.h | tathA.api taduddeshenApravR^ittestAdarthvasya prathamamanishchayAnna tadarthaM jalpo dAtuM shakyate | 
vyatirekasyAnyadIyAkAraNatvamAtranishchayahetutvAdvAdasya kAraNatAmavadhArayitumanvayaM chAha- vAdeneti || 
chashabdo.anvayasya vyatirekeNa samuchchayArthaH | anvayavyatirekAbhyAM samarthitamarthamupasaMharati- itIti ||
iti tasmAdvAdasya pUrvatvam.h | jalpavitaNDArthinorvidyAsAmyAdinishchayahetuparIkShArthaM prathamAnuShTheyatvaM siddhamityarthaH | 
etaduktaM bhavati | samAnavidyayoreva jalpavitaNDe | samAnavidyatA cha parIkShAnishcheyA | parIkShA cha vAdakathayA vidheyA | na jalpavitaNDAbhyAm.h | jayena hi vidyAdhikyaM nirNetavyam.h | parAjayena cha tannyUnatA | jayaparAjayau cha pramANatarkAbhyAM prakR^itaprameyasAdhanasAmarthyAsAmarthyalakShaNau uchchanIchatvanirNayaviShayatAshabdavAchyAveva prakR^itopayoginau | tau cha vAda eva sambhavato na jalpavitaNDayoH | tatra yatkiJNchinnigrahodbhavanamAtreNa jayaparAjayavyavasthApanAt.h | ato jalpavitaNDArthaM jalpavitaNDAbhyarthanAbhAvAnnAnavastheti | 
jalpavitaNDArthinorvidyAparIkShAyAM vAdena kR^itAyAM kiM kAryam.h | samavidyatvasambhAvanAyAM jalpavitaNDe kartavye ityuktameva | viShamavidyatAvadhAraNAyAM kiM vidheyamityapekShAyAmAha- tatsiddhAviti ||
tena vAdenaiva tasya nIchochchabhAvasya siddhau satyAmanyayorjalpavitaNDayorvyarthatA | tatashcha akartavyatetyarthaH | parIkShArthena vAdenaivoparama iti |
jalpavitaNDArthinorvidyAparIkShArthaM vAdakathA prathamaM dAtavyetyuktasyApavAdamAha- bahuvidyatveti ||
prAk.h parIkShAto lokasaMvAdAdinA.anyatarasya pratiyogyapekShayA bahuvidyatvasiddhau tu vAdo.api naiva dAtavyaH | kimu jalpavitaNDe iti |
kuta ityata Aha- kAraNamiti ||
vidyAparIkShAyA iti sheShaH | vAda ityanuvartate | vAdo hi vidyAparIkShAkAraNamityeShyavyo na tu vyasanitayA | tatphalaM tvanyata eva jAtamiti kiM parIkShayA kiM tadaN^gena vAdeneti |
yaduktaM spardhAvatoH khyAtyAdikAmayorvAdo na sambhavati, tatrAsatsAdhanottaraprayogasyAvashyamavarjanIyatvAt.h, tatashcha vidyAsAmyavaiShamyaniNaryAnupapatteriti tatrAha- sabheti ||
prashnashabdAtkarotItyarthe Ikak.hpratyayo vaktavyaH | spardhinAmiti jAtau bahuvachanam.h | evetyasya yujyata ityadhyAhR^itenAnvayaH | yataH sabhAdipUrvastataH spardhinAmapi vAdo yujyata eveti | tushabdo hetvarthaH | 
sabhAsabhApatiprAshnikairniyatayorasatsAdhanAdiprayogavarjanasambhavAditi bhAvaH | 
yaduktaM "tatsiddhau vyarthatA.anyayoH' iti tadayuktam.h | vAdena tattvanirNayasiddhAvapi arthAdyasiddheH | tathAchAbhilaShitaM na siddham.h, siddhaM chAnabhilaShitamiti tatrAha- ubhayeti ||
vAda ityanuvartate | asyaiva vivaraNaM niNarItIti || na kevalaM nirNItikArakaH kintu jayakArakashcha | jayashabdena tatsAdhyamarthyAdikamupalakShyate | vidyAparIkShArthe vAde jayino.arthAdikamapi sabhApatinA sampAdanIyamiti bhAvaH | 
evaM tarhi na kadA.api jalpavitaNDApravR^ittiH "vyartharatA.anyayoH' iti yukteH sama(mAna)tvAt.h | yathA hi vidyAvaiShamyanirNaye jitavato.arthAdilAbhaH, tathA tatsAmye dvayorapi arthAdilAbhaH sambhavatyeva | nacha phalAntaramasti yena punarjalpavitaNDArambhaH syAdityata Aha- tattvAprakAsha eveti ||
tattvAprakAsha iti paravaJNchanasAmarthyamuchyate | tena tatsAdhyo.arthAdilAbho lakShyate | idamuktaM bhavati | yadyapi vidyAsAmyavaiShamyayornirNItijayau syAtAM tathA.api tAttvikakathAphalarUpAveva | parAchChAdanachAturyaprayuktArthAdilAbhArthaM samAnavidyayoH punarjalpavitaNDApravR^ittiriti | nachaivaM viShamavidyayorapi tatpravR^ittiH, upaplavaprasaN^gasyoktatvAditi |
yadvA tattvanirNayaphalo vAdaH atharAdiphale jalpavitaNDe, iti phalabhedena kathAbheda uktaH | so.anupapannaH | tathA satyarthAdInAM bhedena kathA.a.anantyaprasaN^gAdityata Aha- tattveti || yadyapi arthAdayo.avAntarabhedabhinnAstathA.api tattvAprakAsha eka eva vitaNDAjalpayoH phalam.h | tattvanirNayetaratvarUpeNArthAdInAmekatvAnnoktadoShaH| tadavAntarabhedavivakShA tu vyarthaiveti bhAvaH | 
evaM kathayA vidyAparIkShaNamiti pakShaH samarthitaH | idAnImanyatheti pakShamapi samarthayamAna Aha- vineti ||
avigItavidvatprasiddhayAdineti sheShaH | kvApItyasya pUrvArdhenAnvayaH | tadA samavidyayoH prathamamapi jalpAdiH kathAvisheShaH kAryaH syAdityarthaH | tarhi vidyAparIkShaNaM vAdenaivetyuktivirodha ityata Aha- vA eveti ||
vAda eva prathamaM kartavyo bhavediti yaduktaM tadanyathA vAdena vinA vidyAparIkShaNasya kartumashakyatva evAto na virodha iti |
astvevamupAyAntaravirahe kathayaiva vidyAparIkShaNam.h | sA tu vAda iti kutaH | tattvanirNayArthinoradhikAritvAttatphalatvAchcheti chet.h(na | evaM) | tarhi vijigIShAvatoradhikAritvAdatharAdiphalatvAtsabhAdyaN^gopetatvAjjalpo.api syAditi |
kimatra jalpashabdavAchyatAmAtramApadyate, kiMvA vAdashabdavAchyatA.abhAvaH, athavA samAhArarUpaM kathAntaraM yadvA nimittadvayasamAveshe vAdashabdasyaiva vyavahArAnupapattiH | sarvatrApyuttaramAha- jalpa iti ||
etAdR^ishasya nimittadvayopetasyAtra jalpa iti nAma syAdityabhyupagamenAdyo nirastaH | apishabdena vAdashabdavAchyatAM pratij~nAyai tAdR^ishasyetyanena heturuktaH | tena dvitIyo.api nirAkR^itaH | nahi nimittasadbhAve vAchakApravR^ittiriti yuktam.h | jalpashabde.api sAmyAt.h | atastulAyAM pramANAdito vidhAntaravatI syAt.h | vAdasya jalpa ityapi nAma syAditi vAdasaMj~nA tu mukhyA jalpasaMj~nA tvamukhyeti sUchitam.h | tena chaturtho.api nirastaH | tatra hetuvisheShasadbhAvaM tushabdena dyotayati |
tathAhi | yadyapi kathakAvAdito vijigIShU tathA.api sabhyAdibhivirjigIShAM paribhAvyotpAditA tattvanirNayArthitaiva kathopayoginI | arthAdilAbhashchAntarA prApto na tvAdita evoddiShya ityamukhya eva | ata eva pUrva ubhayArthaH syAdityukte sAmyapratItiprasaktau nirNItijayakAraka iti tattvanirNIteH prAdhAnyapradarshanArthaM vivaraNaM kR^itam.h | anyathA kathAphaladvayasyaivobhayashabdena pratItervivaraNaM vyarthaM syAt.h | alpAchtaramiti lakShaNasya vyabhichAraM kurvANenApyetadeva sUchitam.h | anyathA jayanirNItikAraka ityavakShyat.h | sabhyAdisaMvaraNaM cha vijigIShutAparibhavArthamiti vAdatAprAdhAnyamevopodbalayatIti |
api chAdhikAribhedAdikaM bahiraN^gatayaiva kathAbhedakam.h | antaraN^gaM tu pravR^ittiprakAra eva | sa cha vAdasambandhyevAsyAM kathAyAmastItyato vAdatvameva mukhyamityAshayavAnAha- pratij~neti ||  Vyasa-(14) 

vidyAparIkShArthAyAM kathAyAM kvApi prameye pratij~nAmAtreNa pramANopanyAsarahitena vachanena sAdhyatvaM praj~nApanIyaM syAt.h | kuta etat.h | katyeva devA yAj~navalkyeti shAkalyena pR^iShye, (yAj~navalkyena) trayastriMshaditi vachanamAtreNa praj~nApanasya kR^itatvAt.h | sA cha vidyAparIkShArthA kathetyupakramaparyAlochanayA siddham.h | yAj~navalkyashabdena tatkathopalakShyate | saptamyathare vatiH | tataH kimityata Aha- saMvAda iti || 
evambhAvo hi vAdiprativAdinoH saMvAde.anyonyAptatA.a.ashvAse satyeva syAt.h tadAshvAso hi vAda eva sambhavati na jalpe | vijigIShuNA.apasiddhAntAdiparihAreNa sarvathA pramANaprashnasya kartavyatvAt.h | tenAyaM vAda eveti (prati)j~nAyata iti |
nanvevaM tarhi na vidyAparIkShA sambhavati | pramANopanyAse hi tatsamarthanopAlambhAbhyAM sA syAt.h | natu prashnapratij~nAbhyupagamamAtreNetyata Aha- vivAda iti ||
heturiti pramANamAtropalakShaNam.h | pramAheturiti vA | na hyekatrAptaH sarvatrApta eveti niyamo.astIti bhAvaH | yAj~navalkyenApi tatra tatra pramANopanyAsaH kR^ita eveti sakalamanAkulam.h | 
prakR^itAnAM sabhyasabhApatiprAshnikAnAM svarUpajij~nAsAyAmAha- sabheti ||
(dvau) chashabdau sabhA(bhyA)dInAmanyonyasamuchchaye | tR^itIyo visheShaNasamuchchaye | evashabdau tu vaiShNavA eva rAgadveShavihInA eveti sambaddhayete | anyathA kathA.anupapattisUchanaM tatprayojanam.h | syuriti vakShyamANamihApi(matrApi) sambaddhayate | 
sabhyAnAM prAshnikAnAM cha visheShaNAntaramAha- syuriti ||
sarvashabdena vAdiprativAdidarshanasya kathopayuktasya vyAkaraNAdeshcha saN^grahaH | punaH sabhyaprAshnikagrahaNaM sabhApativyavachChedArtham.h | tatsArvaj~nasya kathopayogAbhAvAt.h | sabhyAH prAshnikAshcha sarvavedinaH syurityanvayaH | 
nanu prAshnikAnAM kvopayogaH | vivadamAnayorguNadoShAvadhAraNAdAviti brUmaH | evaM tarhi tairevAlaM kiM sabhyairityata Aha- etaditi ||
anantaroktAnprAshnikAn.h etachChabdena parAmR^ishati | kvachitsUkShme prameye eteShAM prAshnikAnAM kAraNAntaradvA.aj~nAne sati vAdinorguNadoShanirNayAya sabhyAshcha pramANaM syuriti vakShyamANenAnvayaH | pramANAshrayeShu pramANatvopachAraH | 
yadyevaM prAshnikeShvaj~nAnashaN^kayA sabhyAnAM varaNam.h, tadA teShvapyaj~nAnashaN^kayA.anye.api varaNIyAH | anyathA nirNayAbhAvena kathAvaiyarthyApatteH | teShvapyevamityata Aha- eShAM cheti ||
eShAM sabhyAnAM chAj~nAne sati dUragA deshAntarasthAH | nachaivaM sabhyasaMvaraNamapyanarthakam.h | tataHparaM prAyeNAj~nAnashaN^kAnudayAt.h | laukikashchAyamartha iti | 
dUragAnnirNAyakatvasambhavAya vishinaShyi- pakSheti ||
ekadeshotkIrtanena yathoktaM sabhyAdilakShaNamatidishati |
aprakAshya svasiddhAntamiti vitaNDAlakShaNamuktam.h | tatkathaM vAdajalpAbhyAM vyAvartakamityata Aha- ubhAbhyAmiti ||
vAdajalpayorubhAbhyAmeva svapakShasAdhanaM parapakShadUShaNaM kartavyaM, natu prativAdinaH parapakShadUShaNamAtreNa kR^itArthateti |
satAmeveti sArdhashlokasyAtra sanniveshe tu, lakShitau vAdajalpau | idAnIM tu vitaNDAyA lakShaNadvayaM vivakShustAvadupayuktamAha- ubhAbhyAmiti || kathA vAdajalpalakShaNA | etena jalpo.arthAdivyapekShayetyuktasya vitaNDAyAmativyAptirapi parihR^itA | ubhayasAdhanavattvena sadekAdhikArikatvena vA.arthAdivyapekShakathAyA visheShitatvAt.h | yadarthaM satAmevetyuktaM tadvitaNDAlakShaNamAha- vitaNDA tviti || kathetyanuvartate | ubhAbhyAmiti yadarthamuktaM tallakShaNAntaramAha- aprakAshyeti || 
ukte tairiti pUrvavaditi |
ubhAbhyAM sAdhanamityAdyuktam.h | tatra sAdhanAya kiM pramANaM prayoktavyam.h | yatra yadasti tatra tadeva (kiM) vaktavyam.h | satyam.h | pramANasamplave tu katham.h | kiM sarvamevotaikameva tatrApi kimityapekShAyAmAha- sadbhiriti ||
eka eva, natu sambhavatsarvamAdhikyaprasaN^gAt.h | sa chAgama eveti yojyam.h | yadvaikashabdo mukhyArthaH | IshvarAdiprameye mukhyo vedAdirAgama eva vaktavyaH (tasya svAtanteNa sAdhyasiddhayaN^gatvAt.h) nAnumAnamiti | nanvavaidikasya vedAdyAgamopAdAne.apasiddhAntaH syAdityata uktam.h- sadbhiriti || kuto vedAdiprayoganiyama ityata Aha- abhIShyeti || yata iti sheShaH | anumAnaM khalu na svAtanteNeshvarAdisAdhanasyeShye | sarvatropAdhipratipakShayoH sambhavAt.h | tadarthamantato.apyAgamo.anusaraNIyaH | tato varaM prathamameva (Agamo) vaktavyaH | tasya svAtanteNa sAdhyasiddhayaN^gatvAt.h | nanvavaidikaM prati katham.h | AgamaM prayujya tatprAmANyaM sAdhanIyamiti | 
nanvasadbhiH kiM vaktavyam.h | na tAvatpratyakSham.h | atIndriye tadayogAt.h | na chAgamaH | svaparAgamayoranyonyaM prAmANyAsammateH | nApyanumAnam.h | prayogaparimANAsammateH | tathAhi | saugato yadi dvayavayavaprayogaM kuryAttadA naiyAyikena nyUnena nigR^ihyeta | anigrahe vA prativAdI paryanuyojyamupekSheta | paJNchAvayavaprayoge tvadhikena nigR^ihyeta | tathA svIkAre chApasiddhAntena | tathAcha niyatAvayavAdivyatirekeNa vitaNDaiva na syAdityata Aha- svasiddhAnteti ||
yathAsiddhAntaM vaktavyamiti prAN^.hniyamAtsvasiddhAntanirNItaprayogAvayavaparimANApekShayaiva nyUnAdyavatArAdanyathA(kathA).anupapatteriti 
hishabdAtharH | 
sadbhirAgamo vaktavya iti na (itya)yuktam.h | vaidikasya prativAdinastaddUShaNe.apasiddhAntAt.h | adUShaNe tu parapakShAdUShaNena kathAbhAvaprasaN^gAdityata Aha- pratyakSheti |
Agame tu vAdinA prayukte prativAdinA vaidikena tasyAnyArthataiva dasharnIyA | nAnumAnasyevAprAmANyam.h | yenApasiddhAntaH syAt.h | tata eva kR^itaparapakShadUShaNo.api bhavet.h | anyArthatAM darshitavatA.a.agamasya parAbhimatArthAtprachyAvitatvAt.h | na hyapekShitArthAsAdhakatavAdanyatpramANadUShaNamastIti | 
nanvevaM sati kathaM kathAparyavasAnam.h | svasvAbhimatArthAgrahaparityAjanopAyAbhAvAdityata uktam.h- pratyakShetyAdi || atra parAbhimate.arthe pratyakShAgamavirodhamAshritya | na kevalametAvat.h | atropakramAdiliN^gavilomatAdoSho.api darshanIyaH | atrAnyatama(ra)mAtre tAtparyam.h | anyathA.a.adhikyaprasaN^gAt.h | 
nanvetAvatA.api na kathAsamAptiH | parAbhimatArthAnupapattimAtreNa svAbhimatArthAsiddherityataH satyamityAha- liN^geti ||
darshanIyapadamanuvartate | shrutyAdInAM vedAdInAM shrutirliN^gaM samAkhyA chetyuktAnAM liN^gagrahaNenaiva gR^ihItatvAt.h | upalakShaNaM chaitat.h | parAthare pramANAnukUlyasya svArthe tatprAtikUlyasya cha nirAso darshanIya ityapi draShyavyam.h | svasiddhAntaprayogaparimANAnatikrameNa parArthAnumAnavAkyaprayogaH kartavyaH | tathAtve cha na nyUnAdyavatAraH | tadatikrama eva tadavakAsha ityuktam.h | 
apara Aha | yathAvastu prayoktavyam.h | nacha vastutattva eva vAdinAM vipratipatteravashyaM nyUnAdyavatArasambhavenAprayogaprAptiriti vAchyam.h | (ta)yasya yatra tAttvikatvAbhimAnastena tatprayogAnantaraM pareNa nyUnAdAvudbhAvite tathArUpatAyAH sAdha(nIyatvAt.h)nAt.h | nachaivamarthAntarApAtaH | hetoranyatarAsiddhayudbhAvane tatsiddhivyutpAdanavatprakR^itopayogasadbhAvAditi | tadayuktam.h | dvitripaJNchAvayavAdipakShANAM sarveShAmapi tAttvikatAyAH samarthitatvAt.h | svasvaniyamasyaiva tAtvikatvamupetya tadanatikrameNaiva prayogAN^gIkAre tu sarvathA kathochChedApatteH | tattAttvikatAyAM prativAdinA vipratipadyamAnenAvashyaM nyUnAderudbhAvanAt.h | 
nanUktamatra svasvAvayavakalpanA paraM prati samarthanIyeti | duruktaM tat.h | tatsamarthanasyAshakyatvAdityAha- tripaJNcheti ||
trayaH pratij~nAhetUdAharaNAni, udAharaNopanayanigamanAni vA, paJNcha pratij~nAhetUdAhaNopanayanigamanAni vA.avayavA yasyAH sA tripaJNchAvayavA | evashabdena pakShadvayaniyamamAha | yugmau dvAvudAharaNopanayAvayavau yasyAH sA yugmAvayavinI | niyamAditi sannihitenaiva sambaddhayate | anumeti tAdarthyAtprayoga uchyate | vaisheShikAdInAM tatraiva vyavahArAt.h | taM brUyAdyadi paro.aniyatavAdIti sheShaH | yadvA yo mImAMsakastArkikAdishcha tripaJNchAvayavAmevAnumAM brUyAt.h | taM prati yaH saugato niyamAdyugmAvayavinIM brUyAt.h | sa yadi tAdR^ishI tyavayavA paJNchAvayavA cha nAnumeti brUyAditi yojyam.h | evaM (vi)parivartenApi | tAdR^ishI nAnumetyasya pramANAbhAvAditi sheShaH | 
etaduktaM bhavati | naiyAyikena saugataM prati paJNchAvayavaprayoge vihite saugato.adhikamiti nigR^ihNIyAt.h | tato naiyAyikena paJNchAvayavaprayogasyaiva tAttvikatvAnnaivamiti vaktavyam.h | tataH saugato nedaM tattvamapramANikatvAditi vadedeva | atha naiyAyikenAprAmANikatvamasiddhamiti vadatA kathamiti saugate pR^iShyavati (sati) kena pramANena svIyA paJNchAvayavakalpanA sAdhyA | tadagocharatvAt.h | nahi kAryakAraNabhAvaH kvApi pratyakShasya viShayaH | na chAgamena | tadabhAvAt.h | "paJNchAvayavayuktasya vAkyasya guNadoShavit.h' iti bhAratAdivAkyamastIti chenna "saukShmyaM saN^khayAkramashchaiva nirNayashcha prayojanam.h' ityAdinA tatraivAnyathA vyAkhyAtatvAt.h | nApyupamAnAbhAvAbhyAm.h | niyataviShayatvAt.h | nachArthApattyA | tadabhAvAt.h | anupAnAnatirekAchcheti | 
mA bhUtpratyakShAdinA.avayavakalpanAsiddhiH | anumAnena tu bhaviShyati | vyAptipakShadharmatopetaliN^gapratIteH paJNchAvayavavAkyashravaNAnvayavyatirekAnuvidhAyitvAditi chet.h | na tAvadidamanumAnaM tvachchetasi parivartamAnaM paraM pratyAyanAN^gam.h | kinnAma prayujyamAnam.h | tatra kiM paJNchAvayavaprayogo.asya vidhAsyate, atha dvayavayavaH | nobhAvapItyAha- niyateti ||
niyatAvayavasya paJNchAvayavasya dvayavayavasya cha | yathAsaN^khayaM saugatanaiyAyikayorbodhaupayikatvAsiddhau, nAnumAnenApyavayavakalpanAsiddhiriti sheShaH | 
yadvottaravAkye niyatAvayavAsiddhAvityanuvAdo.ayam.h | tato niyatAvayavAsiddheriti siddhayati | paJNchAvayavaprayoge pareNAdhikyodbhAvanAt.h | dvayavayavaprayoge.anyataranyUnatvApasiddhAntayorudbhAvanAdityarthaH | tataH kimityata Aha- vyAptIti ||
yata evaM nopAyAntaraM tena kAraNena | tena naiyAyikena vyAptimAtreNa yadyasyAnyavavyatirekAnuvidhatte 
tattatkAryamityAdivyAptivachanamAtreNaiva | upalakShaNametat.h | "liN^goktau' ityAdiprAgvyutpAditaprakAreShvanyatamenetyapi draShyavyam.h | sAdhanaM paJNchAvayavaniyamasya, kartavyaM syAt.h | saugatenApi tadanusaraNIyam.h | itarathA tasyApi prayogAnupapattiprasaN^gAditi | 
tato.api kimityata Aha- tasmAditi ||
yasmAtprayogeyattAsAdhanaM vAdiprativAdibhyAmanyatareNa vA svamataparityAgenAnyamatAbhyupagame kR^ita evopapadyate nAnyathA | tasmAtsaivAnumA matA | vyAptivachanAdikameva parArthaprayogatvena sarvatra mantavyam.h | 
idamuktaM bhavati | yadA naiyAyiko dvayavayavena paJNchAvayavaniyamaM sAdhayati | tadA dvayavayavasya tAttvikatvaM svayaM manyate na vA | neti pakShe pratArakaH syAt.h | Adye.anyatrApi kathaM tattatvaM na syAt.h | evaM kathAbhAvaprasaN^gabhIruH saugato.api paJNchAvayavena dvayavayavasyAvashyakatAM pratipadyamAnastattvaM manyate na vA | dvitIye kathaM tataH pratipadyeta | Adye.anyatrApi kutastanna tattvam.h | ato.atra sarvasiddhAntaprakArANAM tAttvikatvAdyuktaM svasiddhAntAnusAreNeti | asmAdeva saN^kaTAdbibhyadudayano yathAvastu vaktavyamityuktvA yathAsiddhAntaM vA vaktavyamiti samayaM bad.hdhvA pravR^ittAyAM kathAyAM na nyUnAdyavatAra iti pakShAntaramavAdIditi | avasitamanumAnam.h | 
nirdoShaM vAkyamAgamaH | sa dvividhaH | pauruSheyo.apauruSheyashcha | tatrApauruSheyo vedaH | anyastu pauruSheya iti suprasiddhatvAnnoktam.h | 
kechidvAkyaM vAkyArthe.anumAnamiti bruvate | tadanupapannam.h | vAkyavAkyArthayordeshataH kAlato vA.anvayavyatirekAbhAvAt.h | athedaM vAkyaM vAkyAtharvat.h vAkyatvAditi sAdhyate | tatra kiM vAkyArthamAtraM sAdhyate tadvisheSho vA | nAdyaH | visheShapramiternirnibandhanatvApatteH | dvitIye sa visheShaH pratIto na vA | Adye vAkyavaiyarthyam.h | dvitIye.aprasiddhavisheShaNatA | visheShasyAnyatrAbhAvAdanaikAntyaM cha | matubArthashcha kiM pratipAdyapratipAdakabhAvaH, sambandhAntaraM vA | Adye sAkShAlliN^gatayA vA | na prathamaH | anumAnavaiyarthyAt.h | apasiddhAntAchcha | dvitIye tu nedaM vAkyArthAnumAnaM kintu siddhe.arthe vAkyasya liN^gatAnumAnameva | tatra cha dR^iShyAnto.anyatarasAdhyavikalaH | na dvitIyaH | tadabhAvena bAdhAt.h | 
athaivaM prayujyate, vivAdAdhyasitAni padAni svasmAritArthAnvayapramitipUrvakANi AkAN^kShAdimatpada(kadambaka)tvAditi | tadayuktam.h | vinApyanvayapramitiM daivAtprayukteShvAkAN^kShAdimatsu padeShvanaikAntyAt.h | Aptaprayuktatvena hetuvisheShaNe sAdhyArthasya hetvarthe praveshApatteH | puruShavisheShaprayuktatvasyAdhyApakaprayukteShu vyabhichArAt.h | mUlapramAnumAne.api vedeShu anupapatteH | tadapauruSheyatvasya sAdhitatvAt.h | 
apare tvapauruSheyasyAgamatvamupagamya pauruSheyasyAnumAnatvamabhyupagachChanti | teShAM tu sphuTo vede vyabhichAraH | kiJNcha padAnAmanvitAbhidhAne shaktiH | padAnyeva cha vAkyam.h | nacha vaidikapadebhyo.anyAnyeva laukikAni padAni | vaktA tu padaj~nAna evopayujyate | tatkathaM lokavedayoH prakArabhedaH syAt.h | api cha vedAnusAreNa paThyamAneShu laukikavAkyeShu katham.h | anvayapratItirutpadyata eva | kinnAma punaH pauruSheyatvaj~nAnAdapanIyata iti | evaM tarhi vAkyAdeva vAkyAtharj~nAnam.h | tatprAmANyanishchayAya tu vaktrAdyanusaraNamityAyAtamityAstAm.h | 
tadevaM sAmAnyato visheShatashcha pramANAni lakShitAni | tatra svIyasAmAnyalakShaNasamarthanenArthAdvAdyantaroktasAmAnyalakShaNAni nirastAnyeva | tathA.api smR^itiviShaye vaktavya(vi)sheShasya vidyamAnatvAtprAbhAkaralakShaNaM visheShato nirAkaroti- anubhUtiriti ||
"tadA vaktavyaM smR^itiH pramA na vA | Adye.apasiddhAntaH' iti sheShaH | dvitIye tvAha- keneti || yadi smR^itirna pramA tadA smR^itiH lakShaNena vyAvartanIyA | anyathA.ativyApteH | (tatkena) tatkutaH smR^itirapodyate vyAvartyate | smR^itirvyAvartakaM na kimapi | lakShaNe.astIti yAvat.h | 
nanvanubhUtirityukta eva smR^itAvaprasaN^gaH | smR^itivyatiriktaM j~nAnamanubhUtirityabhidhAnAt.h | nahi smR^itiH smR^itivyatiriktA bhavatIti | maivam.h | smR^iterapi smR^ityantaravyatiriktatvasambhavenAvyavachChedakatvAt.h | smR^ititvAnadhikaraNaM j~nAnamanubhUtiriti chet.h | kimidaM smR^ititvam.h | na tAvajjAtiH | guNeShu jAteranaN^gIkR^itatvAt.h | saMskAramAtrajanyaj~nAnatvaM tu na sambhavati | adR^iShyAdijanyatvAt.h | asAdhAraNakAraNavivakShAyAmapi tathA | smR^itermAnasatvasya vakShyamANatvAt.h | etena niyamena pratyutpannAsAdhAraNakAraNakapratyagratvamanubhUtitvamityapyavachChedakaM draShyavyam.h | smR^iterapi mAnasapratyakShajanyAyAstathAtvAt.h | saMskArasya kAraNatve.api nAsau sattAmAtreNa smR^itiM janayati kinnAmodbuddha eva | tathAcha kathaM na pratyutpannAsAdhAraNakAraNajanyatvam.h | anyathendriyAdimA(yamA)tramupAdAyAnubhUterapi tannirAkuryAt.h | kiJNcha smR^itirapi 
kAchitpratyutpannasaMskArajanyA sambhavatyeva | nachAvachChedakena vinA niyamo j~nAtuM shakyata iti | 
yadvA anubhUtiH pramANaM chettadA smR^itAvavyAptiriti sheShaH | nanu smR^itiH pramANameva na bhavati | tatkathaM tatrAvyAptidoSha ityata Aha- keneti || smR^itiH kena nimittenApodyate pramANAdbahiH kriyate na kenApItyarthaH | tathAhi | kimayathArthatvAt.h | yAthArthye.apyananubhUtitvAdvA.aprAmANye bAdhakAbhAvAdvA prAmANye sAdhakAbhAvAdbAdhakasadbhAvAdvA | AdyaM dUShayati- keneti || smR^itiH kena prabalena pramANenApodyate bAdhyate | yena yathArthA na syAt.h | bAdhakAbhAvAnnAyathArthatvaM vAchyamiti | dvitIyaM nirAkaroti- keneti || kimanubhUtitvaM pramANalakShaNamiti kR^itvA.ananubhUtitvAtsmR^itirapramANamityuchyate kiM vA ghaTAdidR^iShyAntAvaShyambhena | Adye.anyonyAshrayatvam.h | tathAcha kena smR^itirapodyate | dvitIye.api smR^itireva kenApodyate | asmR^ititvenAnubhUtiH kuto nApodyate visheShAbhAvAditi | tR^itIyamapAkaroti- pUrveti || 
yadi smR^itirapramANaM syAttadA pUrvAnubhUte kiM mAnamiti prashno niruttaraH syAt.h | smR^itivyatiriktasya tatpramANasyAbhAvAt.h | tathAcha sAkShyAdilokavyavahAro lupyeta | smR^itireva pramANaM kintu liN^gatayeti chenna | tathA.anubhavAbhAvAt.h | anyathA sAkShAtkAreNa kAryeNa karmakArakatayA ghaTA(dya)numAnamityapi syAt.h | chaturthaM pratyAha- pUrveti || smR^itirityeva hi vaktavyam.h | vachanAchchAnubhavo.anumIyata iti lokavyavahAra evAtra pramANamityarthaH | 
nanu yadi smR^itiH pramA syAttadA tatkAraNasya saMskArasyAnupramANatvaM prasajyeta | tathAchAnupramANatritvaM bhajyeta | nahi saMskAraH pratyakShAdiShvantarbhavati | anindriyasannikarShatvAdaj~nAtakaraNatvAchcheti paJNchamamapAkaroti- mAnasamiti || 
hi yasmAttatsmaraNaM mAnasaM manaHpratyakShajaM na saMskArakaraNakaM tato noktadoSha iti sheShaH | asAkShAtkArarUpatvAnna pratyakShaphalatvamityata uktam.h- vij~nAnamiti || sAkShAtkAra ityarthaH | smaraNasya mAnasatvaM sAkShAtkAratvaM cha kuta ityata Aha- tachcheti || 
taditi mAnasatvam.h | chashabdAtsAkShAtkAratvaM cha | yadvA dvayamapi tachChabdena parAmR^ishyate | prakR^itAnusandhAnArthashchashabdaH | 
nanvindriyANAM prApyakAritvaniyamAdatItena cha manasaH prApterayogAtkathaM smR^itermAnasapratyakShajatvamityata Aha- atIteti || 
santi tAvadyogino.aNimAdisiddhisampannA atItAnAgatadarshinaH shrutismR^itItihAsapurANaprasiddhAH | shrutyAdeH siddhArthe prAmANyasya sAdhitatvAt.h | karmavidhisamAnayogakShematvAchcha yogavidhInAm.h | nacha tajj~nAnamasAkShAtkAraH | shrutyAdinA sAkShAtkAratvapratIteH | tathAhi shrutiH "apashyamapyaye mAyayA vishvakarmaNyado jagannihitaM shubhrachakShuH' iti | purANaM cha "nArAyaNaprasAdena' ityAdi | itihAso.api "divyaM dadAmi te chakShuH' ityAdi | tadidamuktam.h- aJNjaseti || sAkShAdityarthaH | evaJNcha yathA yoginAmindriyeNaivAtItAnAgatAtharsAkShAtkArastathA.atItamapi manasA smaryata iti ko doShaH | 
nanvindriyasyArthaprAptirnAma na saMyogaH samavAyo veti niyamaH | kintu pratyAsattimAtram.h | asti cha tadyogIndriyANAm.h | tattadupadarshakayogajadharmasahakR^itatvalakShaNamiti chet.h | evaM tarhi manaso.api pUrvAnubhavajanitasaMskArasAchivyalakShaNA.astyatItArthena pratyAsattirityAshayavatoktam.h- pUrvAnubhUtaM cheti ||
etaduktaM bhavati | yadi prAptiH saMyogAdilakShaNA vivakShitA tadA tadabhAvo.anaikAntikaH | pratyAsattimAtravivakShAyAM tvasiddhiriti | dR^iShyAntakathanaM tu pratyAsattimAtrasya sAkShAtkArahetutAM sambhAvayitum.h | kAryadarshanavashAchcheyaM kalpanA.asau nAtiprasaN^ga iti darshayituM cha | etena mAnasaM chetsmaraNaM syAnna saMskArajaM tadA.ananubhUte.apyu(vyu)tpadyeteti parAstam.h | saMskArasya sannikarShasthAnIyatayA.aN^gIkR^itatvAt.h | 
yatsmR^itermAnasatvaM sAkShisiddhamityuktaM tadabhinayena darshayati- vij~nAtamiti ||
etanmayA pUrvaM kR^itamityetanmayA manasA vij~nAtaM smR^itamapIti smaraNasya mAnasatvaM sAkShAdanubhavAtsAkShyanubhavena siddhamiti | 
yaduktaM paraiH pUrvAnubhavAvachChinnArthagocharA smR^itistadyAthArthyAdikamanuvidadhAnA na svayaM yathArtheti, tadasat.h, anubhavavachChuddhArthaviShayatvasyApi sAkShisiddhatvAditi darshayituM mayaitatkR^itamityapItyuktam.h |
nanu manaso.apratyakShatvAtkathaM smaraNasya mAnasatA sAkShipratyakShagamyeti chenna | tasya sAkShivedyatAyA vakShyamANatvAt.h | tathA.api kAryakAraNabhAvo na pratyakSha iti chedanvayavyatirekasachivasya sAkShiNastatra prAmANyAbhyupagamAt.h | j~nAnaM nityAnumeyamiti chenna | j~nAtatAyA nirAkariShyamANatvAt.h | svaprakAshamiti chenna | anAtvatvAt.h, ghaTavat.h | mAnasavedyatA tu nirasiShyata ityAshayavAnAha- kathameveti || 
yAthArthyamevetyAdinoktasya prakR^itopayogamAha- evamiti ||
yasmAnmAnatrayamevaMlakShaNakaM tasmAdbrahmAdivastuShu veda eva pramANaM na yuktyAdestatrAvakAshaH | indriyaM hi rUpAdimatyeva dravye pravatarte | nacha brahmAdikaM tathA | anumAnaM cha vyAptisApekSham.h | nacha vedanirapekShasya tasya brahmAdau saJNchAro.asti | upAdhipratipakShayostu sarvatra sambhavena vyAptyanishchayAt.h | vedAnusaraNe tu sAdhyAvyApakatvabAdhitaviShayatvayorAvashyakatvAt.h | pauruSheyAgamastu paratantra eveti | 
tataH kimityata Aha- tatprAmANyaM cheti ||
ya(ta)smAdvedaviShaye na yukteravakAshastato virodho.api sa evokta ityupapannam.h | 
tathAcha vedasya pramANavirodhAbhAvAttatprAmANyaM cha sAdhitam.h | yaduktaM prAk.h "tasmAdvedaprAmANyamiShyate' iti tatsiddhamityarthaH | 
|| iti shrImannyAyasudhAyAM na vilakShaNatvAdhikaraNam.h ||  Vyasa-(15) 

|| atha shrImannyAyasudhAyAM chaturtho bhAgaH (abhimAnyadhikaraNam.h) ||
|| OM abhimAnivyapadeshastu visheShAnugatibhyAm.h OM || yuktyantaravirodhaM vedasya parihartumidamArabhyate | syAdetat.h | yuktivirodhAH kiM pratyekaM pariharaNIyAH' utopalakShaNayA | nAdyaH | nirasanIyayuktyAbhAsAnantyena shAstrAparyavasAnaprasaN^gAt.h | sUtratvavyAghAtAchcha | dvitIye tvanArambha evAsyAdhikaraNasya | nirantarAtItAdhikaraNenaivopalakShaNayA sakalayuktivirodhAnAM parihR^itatvAditi | maivam.h | abhyadhikashaN^kAsadbhAvena tadupapatterityAshayavAnpUrvapakShaM tAvadAha- tathA.apIti || 
yadyapi phalavyabhichArAdivirodho vedasya parihR^itastathA.apItyarthaH | mR^ijjalAdInAmityAdipadena tejaHprabhR^itInAM grahaNam.h | buddhij~narAnaM, vAgvaktR^itvaj~n.h | AdigrahaNena shrotR^itvAdikam.h | veda ityanuvartate | dR^iShyA pramitA vyAptiryasyA yukteH sA tathoktA | vyAptigrahaNaM pakShadharmatAyA apyupalakShaNam.h | kvachittanniyamAnabhyupagamAtsvashabdenAsaN^kIrtanam.h | tayA viruddhatvAt.h | tatra mR^ijjalAdInAM buddhivAgAdau | kathamityAkShepe | pratipAdyAntaraM tu nAstyapratIteriti sheShaH | 
etaduktaM bhavati | "mR^idabravIt.h, Apo.abruvan.h, tatteja aikShata, tA Apa aikShanta, R^iNota grAvANo, viduSho.anuprANAH, ahaM shreyasi vyUdire, Apo vA akAmayanta' ityAdivedastAvanna pramANam.h, yuktiviruddhArthAbhidhAyitvAt.h, nIlaM nabha itivat.h | mR^ijjalAdInAM buddhivAgAdimattvaM khalvasyArthaH | sa cha, vimatA mR^inna vaktrI mR^ittvAtsampratipannamR^idvadityAdiyuktiviruddhaH | tathAcha vedavAkyAntare.apyaprAmANyamanumAsyate |

|| OM asaditi chenna pratiShedhamAtratvAt.h OM || nanu cha(chA)nArambhaNIyamevedamadhikaraNam.h "na vilakShaNatvAt.h' ityanenaiva vedasya sakalayuktivirodhAnAM parihR^itatatvAt.h, dR^iDhayuktivirodhaparihArasya chAbhimAnyadhikaraNanyAyasiddhatvAt.h, ityato gatArthatAM pariharannadhikaraNasyopAdhimA(pyA)ha- alpavAkyeti || 
yatra yadA vedasya vAkyayutA yuktirvirodhinI syAt.h, tatra tadA, vastunirNayaH kathaM syAt.h iti pUrvapakShiNerite sati tadvirodhiyuktInAM bAhulyAt.h prAbalyAt.h vastunirNayo bhavediti siddhAntaH | ityeSho.atrAdhikaraNe nyAyo vinishchitaH |

nanu shrutiyuktibhyAM pUrvapakShite kathaM prabalayuktimAtrAshrayeNa siddhAntaH | kathaJNchitpratipakShatAmAtrasambhavAdityata uktaM vivR^iNvannAha- yuktestviti ||
pUrvapakShayuktyapekShayA virodhiyukterbAhulyam.h | tathA pUrvapakShAgamApekShayA virodhyAgamasya cha bAhulyaM kathaM nirNayaM na kuryAt.h | pUrvapakShyutprekShitayuktyAgamAbhyAM prabalau virodhiyuktyAgamau tadbAdhayA vastuvyavasthAM kuruta ityarthaH | kuryAditi pratyekaM sambandhaH | na kevalaM siddhAnte prabalayuktimAtraM, kinnAma prabalAgamo.apyastIti bhAvaH | iti ataH, adhikaraNArambhaH sambhavatIti sheShaH | adhikaraNopAdhivyutpAdanasamAptidyotako vA itishabdaH | 
tadidamudAharaNaniShThaM vyutpAdayituM pUrvapakShamanuvadati sUtrakAraH- asaditi chediti || ayamasyArthaH | na brahmaNo jagatkatarR^itvaM yuktam.h | pramANAbhAvAt.h | "sadeva somyedamagra AsIttattejo.asR^ijata' ityAdishrutirastIti chenna | tasyA yuktiviruddhatvena bhavadabhimatArthe prAmANyAbhAvAt.h | tathAhi | mahApralaye tAvadutpatsyamAnakAryaprAgabhAvo.avashyamaN^gIkaraNIyaH | anyathA sargAdau 
kAryotpAdAyogAt.h | nachAsyAnyatra charitArthatopalabhyate | tatashcha sa eva sakalakAryakAraNaM bhaviShyati |
ayamatra prayogaH | mahApralayavartI kAryaprAgabhAvo mahadAdikAyarkAraNaM bhavitumarhati, anyatrAnupakShINatve sati niyamena tatpUrvabhAvitvAt.h, yo.anyatrAnupakShINatve sati niyamena ya(taH)tpUrvabhAvI, sa tasya kAraNam.h, yathA kuvindaH paTasyeti | mahadAdikaM vA prAgabhAvakAryam.h ananyathAsiddhaniyatapashchAdbhAvitvAt.h, yat.h yadananyathAsiddhaniyatapashchAdbhAvi tat.h tatkAyarm.h | yathA paTaH kuvindasyeti |
nanvatra jagatprAgabhAvasya jagatkAraNatvamAtraM vA sAdhyam.h, anyayogavyavachChedena vA | Adye.arthAntaratA, prAgabhAvasya kAraNatve.api brahmakAraNatAsambhavAt.h | dvitIye vyAptyabhAvaH | na hi "yo yadapekShayA pUrvabhAvI, sa eva tatkAraNaM, nAnyaH' iti niyamo.asti | tataH prAgabhAvasya jagatkAraNatve.api tatsamAnanyAyAnAmIshvarAdInAmapi tatkAraNatvamaN^gIkAryamiti | maivam.h | syAdetadevam.h yadIshvarAdInAM pralaye sattvameva syAt.h | nachaitadasti | siddhAntinA kAraNatvenAshAsyamAnamIshvarAdikaM pralaye.asadbhavitumarhati bhAvatvAnmahadAdikAryavaditi yuktivi(ruddhatvatAt.h)rodhaH | evaJNcha(JNchedI) IshvarAdInAM pralaye.asattvasiddhau prAgabhAvasya kAraNatvamAtrasAdhane.api tasyaiva kAraNatvamiti siddhayati | nanu cha yatkAryaM tatsakartR^ikamiti niyamAnmahadAdikartR^itveneshvaro.avashyamaN^gIkaraNIyaH | na | pralaye tatsattA(ttvA).abhAvasya pramitatvena prAgabhAvasyaiva jagatkartR^itvopapatteH | na chaitadanumAnajAtamudAhR^itashrutiviruddhatvenAprAmANyamiti sAmpratam.h | "asadevedamagra AsIt.h | tadasadeva sanmano.akuruta | asataH sadajAyata' ityAdishrutisaMvAditvena shrutimAtrataH prAbalyAt.h | prabalayuktiviruddhAyAshcha shruteH svArthaparityAgasyAtItAdhikaraNe sthitatvAt.h | prAgabhAvasyApi svarUpasattvAdinA sadevetyAdiprayogaviShayatadvopapatteH |
nanu "etena sarve' ityasadAdishabdAnAM brahmArthatvamuktam.h | tatkiM shabdAnAmanyatra shaktireva nAsti, kiM vA shrutestatra tAtparyAbhAvaH | nAdyaH | samAkarShAN^gIkArAt.h | na dvitIyaH | yuktyupatAyAstatra tAtparyopapatteH | tathA.api prAgabhAvasyaiva kAraNatvaM kartR^itvaM cha na kvApyupalabdhamiti chenna | alaukikArthasya yathAgamaM grAhyatvAt.h | santatotpattiprasaN^gastu brahmavAdino.api samAnaH | ichChAdikAraNAnAM kAdAchitkatvena tatsamAdhAnaM mamApi samAnam.h | ata eva shrutirAha "tanmano.akuruta' iti | tat.h tasmAt.h, tattatprAgabhAvasyaiva tattatkatarR^itvAduktamayuktamiti | tadidamuktam.h- asaditi || abhAvaH shrutyA jagatkartR^itvenochyate | anumIyate cha tathA | tasmAtsa eva jagatkarteti | atrAsachChabdo bhAvasAdhanaH shrutyanugamArthamabhAve prayuktaH | 
aparA.api vR^ittiH | bhAvatvahetunA kAryavadIshvarAdikamapi pralaye.asadanumIyata iti | atrAsachChabdaH kartR^isAdhanaH | iha prathamAM vR^ittimabhipretya neti siddhAntAMshaM vyAchaShye(vyAkhyAti)- asaditi ||
abhAva ityarthaH | kAraNamiti tadvisheShaH kartochyate | hItyanenedamAha | upapattiviruddhastAvanna vedAtharH sambhavati, tadaviruddhe.arthe sambhavatItyuktam.h | prakR^itashchopapattiviruddhaH | tathAcha vakShyAma iti | shrutyartho na bhavatItyupalakShaNam.h | anumAnaprameyamapIdaM na bhavatyupapattiviruddhatvAdityapi draShyavyam.h | 
kiJNcha sambhAvita eva shrutyartho vaktavyo.anumAtavyashcha | nachaivaM prakR^itaH | kvApyabhAvasya kartR^itvAnupalambhAdityAha- kvApIti || 
asatkAraNaM na hyanupalabdhamityanuvartate | 
chaturthapAdasyAdhikaraNasya vailakShaNyaM darshayitumalpetyAdyuktam.h | tadavishadam.h | vailakShaNyaj~nAnasyobhayasvarUpaj~nAnAdhInatvAt.h | atashchaturthapAdArthaM darshayati- shrutIti ||
shrutInAM prAyo bAhulyam.h | tatsahitAbhirupapattibhiH | shrutipradhAnakopapattibhiriti yAvat.h | avirodho virodhAbhAvaH | shrutInAmiti sheShaH | 
yadvA shrutiprAyashabdena shrutikalpatvamuchyate | shrutigR^ihItAbhirupapattibhirityarthaH| atra tu svatantrAbhiriti sphuTameva | athavA.atroktArthasyaiva tatra prapaJNchanAnna doShaH | yathA prathamapAdArthaprapaJNchanAt.h dvitIyapAdasya ityAshayenoktaM samyagiti | yadvA kvApIti atra sambaddhayate | tena kvApyadhyAtmalakShaNe viShaye, atra tvanyatreti bhedaH sUchito bhavati | yadyapyetatprAgeva vaktavyam.h tathA.apyasatkAryamityAdervakShyamANasya, sUtrasya vyAkhyAnAntaratvadyotanAya vyavadhAnenoktam.h | anyathA pUrvameva vyAkhyAnam.h, idaM tu tadupapAdanAyopayogIti vij~nAyeta | 
atha dvitIyAM vR^ittimabhipretya "asaditi chenna' ityetAvatsUtraM vyAchaShye- asaditi || 
kAryaM mahadAdikam.h | yathA pralaye.asat.h pramitaM tathA vastutvAdbhAvatvAtkAraNaM kAraNatvena siddhAntinA.aN^gIkR^itamIshvarAdikamapi(miti)pralaye.asadbhavitumarhatItyarthaH | 
kuto neti chet.h | na tAvadasmAdevAnumAnAdabhAvasya vishvakartR^itvasiddhiH | kintvanena pralayAvasthAyAmIshvarAdyabhAvasiddhau kAryasya sakartR^ikatvaniyame sthite prAgabhAvasya niyatapUrvabhAvitvena vishvakAraNatvaM siddhayan.h katarR^itayaiva setsyatIti vaktavyam.h | tadidaM pratyanumAnaparAhatamityAshayavAn.h pratiShedhamAtratvaditi sautraM hetuM vyAkuvarn.h sAdhyamadhyAharati- niShedheti ||
niShedhaikasvarUpasyeti hetugarbhavisheShaNam.h | ayamatra prayogaH | vipratipanno.abhAvo na kartA pratiShedhamAtratvAt.h niShedhaikasvarUpatvAt.h sampratipannaghaTAbhAvavaditi | kartR^itvamAtrasyAbhAve vishvakatarR^itvaM dUrotsAritam.h | nacha dR^iShyAntaH sAdhyavikalaH | anvayavyatirekAbhyAM kulAlAdeH kartR^itvanishchaye tu abhAvasya tatkalpakAbhAvAt.h |
nanvastu niShedhaikasvarUpatvaM, kartR^itvaM cha  ko virodhaH | tathAcha ghaTAdyabhAvasyAkartR^itve.api pralayakAlIno.abhAvaH kartA bhaviShyatItyataH kartR^itvaniShedhaikasvarUpatvayovirrodhaM sphorayituM kartR^itvasvarUpamAha- buddhIti || 
pravR^ittiH ichChAprayatnAdikA | nishchitaM sarvairapi parIkShakaiH | vR^ikSheNa sthIyata ityAdau kartR^itvaM pAribhAShikaM na tu svAbhAvikamiti hi sarve.api pratipannAH | 
atra buddhipUrvapravR^ittirityetad.hbuddhayA vivichya vyAkhyeyam.h | tathAhi | syAtkartR^iniShedhaikasvarUpatvayoravirodhaH, yadi tR^itIyAdiviShayatvameva kartR^itvaM syAt.h | na chaitadasti | api tarhi ichChAprayatnAdirUpA pravR^ittireva | sarvairapi parIkShakaistasyA eva kartR^itvena nishchitatvAt.h | prakaraNAchchaitadeva nishchitam.h | atraiva hi vipratipattirnAnyatra | sA cheyaM pravR^ittirbuddhipUrvA buddhivyAptA | kAryAyAH pravR^itterbuddhikAraNakatvAt.h | akAryAyAshcha buddhivyabhichArAdyadasharnAt.h | nacha kartR^itvAparaparyAyAyAH pravR^ittervyApikA buddhirabhAve sambhavati | tato vyApyaM kartR^itvamapi na sambhavatyeveti kathaM kartR^itvaniShedhaikasvarUpatvayorna virodha iti | 
atra kartR^itvAnuvAdena buddhipUrvapravR^ittiriti vyAkhyAnAnnishchitamiti napuMsakopapattiH | bhAve vA ktapratyaya iti |
nanu mA bhUdaprayojakatvaM hetoH | tathA.api vaiyarthyamaparihAyarm.h | abhAvaparyAyo hi pratiShedhashabdaH, kartR^itvaM cha kAryotpattyanukUlechChAdiyoga ityuktam.h | nacha pratiShedhatvaM kartari vartate, yenAkartR^ikaM vyabhicharet.h | tannirAsArthaM cha visheShaNaM sArthakaM syAt.h | ataH pratiShedhatvAdityetAvatA.akartR^itvavyabhichArAbhAvAtsUtre mAtragrahaNaM vyAkhyAne.apyekagrahaNaM vyarthamityata Aha- pratiShedheti ||
bhAvasyApi kulAlAdeH kartuH pratiShedhAtmakatvaM vidyate | ataH pratiShedhatvAdityu(tyevo)kte kulAlAdau, akartR^itvena hetoH, vyabhichAraH syAt.h | tatparihArArthaM mAtragrahaNam.h | tadvayAkhyAne (cha) ekagrahaNaM cha sArthakamiti | 
nanu kulAlAderbhAvasya kathaM pratiShedhAtmakatvamityata Aha- abhAveti ||
abhAvo.atrAnyonyAbhAvo vivakShitaH | sa dharmo.asyetyabhAvadharmA | tasya bhAvastattvam.h | tata iti bhAvapradhAno nirdeshaH | asti khalu kulAlAderbhAvasya bhedAparaparyAya(H)pratiShedhAtmakaH anyonyAbhAvo dharma iti |  Vyasa-(16)

nanvidamasaN^gatam.h | yaH kartA dharmI kulAlAdiH na tasya pratiShedhAtmakatvam.h, yashcha pratiShedhAtmako.anyonyAbhAvo na tasya kartR^itvamittaya Aha- dharmeti ||
dharmadharmiNoH kulAlAnyonyAbhAvorekatvataH | chashabdo hetusamuchchaye | abhAvadharmato dharmadharmyaikyatashcha pratiShedhAtmakatvaM bhAvasyAstItyanvayaH | evashabdo bhedavyudAsArthaH | anyonyAbhAvo hi dharmiNA.atyantAbhinno.abhyupeyate | na tvayAvad.hdravyabhAvI dharma iva bhinnAbhinnaH |
astvevaM pratiShedhatvasya kulAlAdau vyabhichArastathA.api kathaM mAtragrahaNasya sArthakyam.h | na hyavishiShyavyabhichAra eva visheShaNaM prayojayati | tathAtve visheShaNaniyamAnupapatteH | kinnAma visheShaNasya vyabhichAranirAsaupayikatve sati | tadatra kathamityata Aha- na tviti ||
kulAlAdeH karturbhAvasya pratiShedhatve.api(dhAtmakatve.api)tanmAtratA pratiShedhamAtratA na bhavet.h | ato.asti mAtragrahaNasya vyabhichAraparihAraupayikatvam.h | tushabdo.avadhAraNe sandigdhavyabhichAraparihArArthaH | 
nanvevamekaM sandhitsato.a(nyat.h)paraM prachyavate | yato vyarthavisheShaNatAparihAre svarUpAsiddhirApannA | tathAhi | pakShIkR^ite abhAve prameyatvAdidharmAH santi na vA | neti pakShe.apramitAshrayatvAdikaM hetoH | Adye na tAvatte.apyabhAvAH vidhipratyayaviShayatvAt.h, pratiyogyanirUpyatvAchcha | ShaT.hpadArthAtiriktatvamabhAvatvamiti chenna | svechChAparikalpanAyA anupAdeyatvAt.h | anyathA paJNchaiva bhAvAstadatirikto.abhAva iti kalpanAyAM samavAyAderapi bhAvatvaM na syAt.h | te cha nAbhAvAddharmiNo bhinnAH | 
anyonyAbhAvasamAnanyAyatvAt.h | tathAcha yathA kulAlAdervipakShasya vidhiniShedhAtmakatvena pratiShedhamAtratvAbhAvastathA pakShIkR^ithAbhAvasyApi (dharmadvArA vidhirUpasya) pratiShedhamAtratvAbhAvAtsvarUpAsiddho hetuH syAt.h | dR^iShyAntashcha sAdhanavikalaH | ghaTAbhAvasyApi dharmadvArA vidhirUpasya pratiShedhamAtratvAbhAvAdityata Aha- abhAvasya cheti ||
prathamApishabdAtpUrvaM yadItyadhyAhAryam.h | yadyapyabhAvasya pakShIkR^itasya dR^iShyAntIkR^itasya cha bhAvaH prameyatvAdidharmo.asti | chashabdAddharmiNA abhinnashcha | bhAvasyAbhAvadharma iveti vA | athA.api na svarUpAsiddhayAdidoSha iti sheShaH | 
kathamityata Aha- hi dharmiNa iti ||
hishabdo hetau | tAdR^iktvaM pratiShedhAtmakatvam.h | mAtratA pratiShedhamAtratA | iha sUtre | etaduktaM bhavati | syAdayaM svarUpAsiddhayAdidoSho yadyatra pratiShedhamAtrashabdena kevalapratiShedhatvaM vivakShitaM syAt.h | nachaivam.h | kintu dharmadvAramantareNa dhamirNa eva pratiShedhatvam.h | tachcha pakShadR^iShyAntayerastyeva | tayodharrmadvAreNa vidhitve.api dharmiNoH pratiShedhatvasyobhayasiddhatvAt.h | vyAvR^ittaM cha vipakShAtkulAlAdeH | tasya dharmato niShedhatve.api dharmi(No) vidhitvA)No.aniShedhatvAditi | nanu kathametallabhyate | uchyate | mAtrashabdo hi sAkalye vartate | nacha tat.h kvApi sambhavati | pratiShedhe.api vidhisadbhAvasya pareNaivoktatvAt.h | tataH pratiShedhamAtrashabdo vidheraprAdhAnyaM lakShayati, annamAtraM bhuktamiti yathA | dharmadharmiNoshcha, aprAdhAnyaM dharmasya, prAdhAnyaM dharmiNaH | tena dharmiNaH pratiShedhatvaM pratiShedhamAtratvamiti siddhayati |
ichChAprayatnAdirUpAyAH pravR^itteH kartR^itAparanAmikAyAH vyApikA buddhiH abhAvAdvayAvR^ittA tAmapi vyAvartayatItyuktam.h | tatrAbhAvAdbuddhivyAvR^ittireva kuta ityata Aha- buddhIti || 
tattasmAtpratiShedhamAtratvAdeva buddhirAhityamabhAvasya ghaTAbhAvavatsiddhayatItyarthaH | dvividhaM hi prameyam.h svatantraM paratantraM cha | paratantramapi dvividham.h bhAvo.abhAvashcha | bhAvo.api dvedhA chetano.achetanashcha | evaJNcha yadA bhAvasyApi kasyachinna chaitanyaM, kA vArtA tadA.abhAve chaitanyasya | kashchidabhAvo buddhimAn.h kinna syAditi chenna | nirupAdhikasambandhamanAdR^itya nirnimittAyAH shaN^kAyA atiprasaN^gitvAt.h | "tanmano.akuruta' iti shruteriti chenna | anyathAsiddhatvAt.h | atha pratiShedhamAtratvamapi pakShe nAbhyupeyAt.h | tadA.asaditi brahmeti cha saMj~nAbhedamAtram.h | anekatvAdeH pareNApi tyAjyatvAt.h | anekasvAtante kAryodayAyogAt.h | 
nanvidaM tatraiva vaktavyam.h | satyam.h | pratiShedha(tva)mAtratve vidite tato buddhirAhityapratIteH saulabhyAdihoktam.h | TIkAkArastu prameyatvAdibhAvadharmAN^gIkAre buddhirapi tathA kinna syAditi shaN^kAvakAshAdihoktamityAhuH | 
bhAvasyAbhAvo dharmaH, abhAvasya cha bhAvo.api dharma ityanupapannam.h (bhAvasyAbhAvadharmatA, abhAvasya cha bhAvadharmatetyanupapannam.h |) bhAvAbhAvayorabhAvabhAvadharmitve pramANAbhAvAt.h | sambandhAbhAvAchcha | sambaddhayoreva hi shauklayapaTayordharmadharmibhAvo dR^iShyo nAsambaddhayomarerumandarayoH | nacha bhAvAbhAvayoH sambandho.asti | saMyogasamavAyayorbhAvaniyatatvAt.h | viruddhasvabhAvatvAchcha | yAvaviruddhasvabhAvau guNaguNinau tAveva hi dharmadharmiNAvupalabdhau | na viruddhasvabhAvAvashvamahiShau | viruddhasvabhAvau cha bhAvAbhAvau | vidhiniShedharUpatvAt.h | abhedAchcha | nahi ghaTaH svayaM svasyaiva dharmo bhavati | uktaM cha dharmadharmyaikyamityata Aha- visheShyataiveti ||
visheShaNataiva cha dharmatvamityapi draShyavyam.h | yo hi vishiShyate vyavachChidyate sa tasya dharmI | dharmashchAparaH | prakArAntarasya nirvaktumashakyatvAt.h | pratIyate cha visheShyavisheShaNabhAvo bhAvAbhAvayoH | anyathA ghaTaH paTo na bhavatItyabhAvaH prameya iti cha vyavahArAnupapatteH | tatkathaM bhAvAbhAvayorna dharmadharmibhAvaH | paTashoklayayoshcha na sambandhaprayukto dharmidharmabhAvaH | nApi merumandarayostadabhAvaH sambandhAbhAvaprayuktaH | kintu svabhAvAdeva visheShyavisheShaNatvAtadabhAvarUpaH | sambaddhayorapi ghaTapaTayostadabhAvavat.h, bhUtalaghaTAbhAvayostadbhAvAchcha | 
evameva virodhisvabhAvAbhedAvapi parA(nira)stau | saguNanirguNatvena nityAnityatvena vA viruddhasvabhAvayorapi guNaguNinordharmyAditvasya darshanAt.h | adarshanAchcha paTatvashauklayayoH | dR^ishyate chAbhede.api tadbhAvaH | astitvAbhidheyatvAdInAM dharmANAM parairdharmyabhedasyAN^gIkR^itatvAt.h | bhinnAnAmapi tadbhAvo nopalabhyate | tadevamasambaddhayorapi vilakShaNasvabhAvayorapi bhAvAbhAvayorabhede.api visheShashaktyA visheShyavisheShaNatAlakShaNo dharmidharmabhAvo yukta eveti |
yadyevaM bhAvAbhAvayorabhAvabhAvadharmitvaM dharmadharmiNoshchAbhedaH syAt.h, tadA bhAvasyApyabhAvatvenAbhAvasya cha bhAvatvena, ghaTAdInAM bhAvatvameva prAkpradhvaMsAtyantAbhAvAnAmabhAvatvameveti niyamo nirnibandhanaH syAt.h | nachaivamastviti vAchyam.h | 
sakalalokasiddhasya tathAbhAvAnarhatvAt.h ityata Aha- prathameti ||
rUpashabdo dharmivachanaH | bhAvAbhAvatvamiti yathAyogaM sambandhaH | atraivaM satyapi | hishabdaH prasiddhau | ayamarthaH | kiM bhAvAbhAvanibandhanaM prameyarUpamanviShyate pramANaM vA | AdyasyottarArdhamuttaram.h | yadyapi bhAvAbhAvAtmakA ghaTAdayaH prAgabhAvAdayashcha | tathA.apyatra padArthasArthe yaH piNDo vidhidharmiko ghaTAdiH sa bhAvo, yastu niShedhadharmikaH prAgabhAvAdiH so.abhAva iti vyavasthopapadyate | abhede.api dhamardharmibhAvo visheShashaktyA saN^gachChata ityuktameva | dvitIyasya uttaraM prathamapratipattiShviti |
yaH prathamaM vidhitayA parapratikSheparUpatAM vinA pratIyate sa ghaTAdirbhAvaH | yastu niShedhatayA parapratikShepeNa pratIyate prAgabhAvAdiH so.abhAva ityuttarArdhenaikavAkyatayA yojyam.h | 
ghaTo hi prathamaM vidhitvena dharmirUpeNa pratIto.anantaraM paTo na bhavatIti paTaniShedhAtmatayA pratIyate | prAgabhAvAdirapi prathamaM niShedhatvena dharmisvarUpeNAvagato.anantaraM prameya iti vidhitayA pratIyata iti sakalapratipattR^isiddhamiti bahuvachanahishabdAbhyAM dyotayati | viShayiviShayayorAdhArAdheyabhAvamabhipretya saptamIprayogaH | kArakeShu gauNamukhyatvavivakShAbhAvasya sthitatvAditi | 
evaM pUrvapakShyutprekShitapramANasamudAyalabdhasyArthasya pramANavirodho darshitaH | idAnImasatkAryaM yathA dR^iShyamityanumAnaM visheShato nirAchikIrShustatprastAvanAya asUtrayatsUtrakAraH OM apItau tadvatprasaN^gAdasamaJNjasamiti | asamaJNjasametadvishvasyAbhAvakartR^ikatvamatam.h | kutaH | abhAvasya (eva) jagatkartR^itvAN^gIkAre.apItau pralaye tadvatprasaN^gAt.h abhAvavattvaprasaN^gAt.h | IshvarAdeH sarvasyA(pya)bhAvAbhyupagamaprasaN^gAditi yAvat.h | na hIshvarAdau sati tatparityAgenAbhAvasya jagatkartR^itvamavadhArayituM shakyamiti | nanu nedamaniShyamIshvarAdikaM pralaye.asadbhavitumarhati | bhAvatvAt.h ghaTavadityanumAneneshvarAdeH sarvasya pralaye.abhAvAbhyupagamAdityatroktaM sUtrakR^itA "na tu dR^iShyAntabhAvAt.h' iti | naiva pralaye sarvasyAsattvamaN^gIkartumuchitam.h | kasmAt.h dR^iShyAntabhAvAt.h | dR^iShyAnta iti tatrAvadhAritavyAptimUlamanumAnamuchyate | dR^iShyAntamAtrasya sAdhanabAdhanAnaN^gatvAt.h | tathAcha pralaye parameshvarAdisadbhAva(sya) sAdhakAnumAnasambhavAdityarthaH | 
kiM tadanumAnamityata Aha bhAShyakAraH- sarvanAsheShvapIti ||
apirabhivyAptau | sarvashabdo vartamAnamAtravivakShayA.api syAdityataH sadetyuktam.h | tadidaM vyabhichAraparihArAyAbhihitam.h | naH puruShasya | ayamityasyaiva vivaraNaM vimata iti | atra pUrvArdhena vyAptiruktA | uttarArdhena pratij~nAhetU | 
etaduktaM bhavati | mahApralayalakShaNo nAshaH puruShasheShavAnbhavitumarhati nAshatvAt.h sampratipanna(sammata)nAshavaditi | atra puruShAvasheShamAtraM sAdhyam.h | natu nAshakartuH puruShasyAvashiShyatA | ata evoktaM yasya kasyeti | nAshasya karturakatarurvetyarthaH | tathA.api kartR^isheShavAniti vadatedamabhipretam.h | pralaye puruShasadbhAvamAtrasAdhane sati bhagnaM tAvatparasyAnumAnam.h | yadapi parasyAbhAvakartR^ikatvaM jagato.abhimatam.h | tadapyata evApAstam.h | avashiShyasya puruSha(visheSha)syaiva vishvakartR^itvasambhave.abhAvasya tatkalpanA.anavakAshAt.h | dR^iShyAnusAriNI hi kalpanA | nahi loke prAgutpatteH kulAlAbhAvayoH satorabhAvo ghaTasya kartA dR^iShyaH | kinnAma kulAla eveti | abhiprAyamajAnAnaH kartR^isheShavAnityuktvA vibhrAntashchodayati "yatra sundopasundanyAyenAsheShA api puruShA naShyAstatra nAshatvahetoranaikAntikatA' iti, tatrAha- nacheti ||
chashabdo.avadhAraNe | asheShanR^inAshastu naiva kvachid.hdR^iShya ityatItaniShedho, dR^ishyo vA naivetyanAgatasya, naivAsti vA dR^ishyamAna iti vartamAnasya | idamuktaM bhavati | anaikAntikatvaM hi pramite vipakShe hetuvR^ittau satyAM(hetuvR^ittyA) vaktavyam.h | nApramite | tathA satyanaminamAtrochChedaprasaN^gAt.h | nachAsheShapuruShanAshaH kAlatraye.api pramitaH, yena nAshatvasya tatra vyabhichAraH syAt.h | pramitatvAN^gIkAre cha pramAturevorvaritatvena vyAghAtashcha syAt.h | nacha nAshakartuH puruShasyAvashiShyatA sAdhyatveneShyA | yena sundopasundAdinAshaH pratyudAhriyeta | kintu puruSha(vi)sheShavattvamAtramiti | 
anena pralayakAlaH puruShavAnkAlatvAdidAnIntanakAlavadityapyanumAnaM sUchitam.h | nacha tadA kAlAbhAvAdAshrayAsiddhiH | tathA sati tadetyeva vaktumashakyatvAt.h | parakIyAnumAne cha pralayavisheShaNAnupapatteH | 
yadyapyatra "kAlo.aN^gIkriyate na vA | Adye tatraiva bhAvatvahetorvyabhichAraH | dvitIye pralayavisheShaNAnupapattiH | sakalakAryavinAshavishiShyakAlasya pralayatvAt.h | atha kAryavinAsha eva pralayastathApIshvarAbhAvasya tena sambandhAbhAvAdIshvarAdikaM pralaye.asaditi pratij~nArthAnupapattiH | deshAdidvArA sambandhAbhyupagame tatraiva bhAvatvasya vyabhichAraH | pralayavisheShaNaparityAge tachChiShyairevohyatAmiti na sUtrabhAShyakArAbhyAmabhihitam.h | sUchitaM chApItAviti sUtrakR^itA | "laye mAnaM 
cha kiM bhavet.h' iti bhAShyakR^itA.api |
tadidaM jIveshvarasAdhAraNamanumAnamuktam.h | idAnIM pralaye jIvasadbhAvasAdhakamanumAnamAha- dharmeti ||
na kevalamuktAnumAnena | kinnAma dharmAdharmashrayatvenApIti sambandhaH | naro jIvAtmA | ayamatra prayogaH | pralayakAlavartI dharmaH sAshrayaH dharmatvAdidAnIntadharmavat.h | evamadharmamapi pakShIkR^itya prayoktavyam.h | nacha dharmAdharmAshrayo jIvAtmano.anyaH sambhavati | evaJNcha pralaye jIvAtmasadbhAvAdbhAvamAtrAsattvasAdhanamanupapannamiti | yatreshvarasadbhAvasAdhanamidam.h | AshrayashabdasyAdhiShThAtR^iparatvAt.h | tatraivaM prayogaH | pralayakAlavartinau dharmAdharmau kenachidadhiShThitau | kAraNatve satyachetanatvAt.h | vAshyAdivaditi | nachAtIndriyayordharmAdharmayoradhiShThAtR^itvamIshvarAdanyasyopapadyate | ato dharmAdharmAdhiShThAtR^itvenApi naraH paramapuruSho laye svIkArya iti | 
nanu pralaye bhAvamAtrasyAsattvamabhyupagachChato mama tadA dhamarAdharmAvapi na sta evetyAshrayAsiddhiriti | idamiha vaktavyam.h | kiM dharmAdharmasaMj~nitamadR^iShyamasti kAryamAtrasya kAraNaM cha bhavatItyabhyupagamya pralaye tadabhAvo.abhIdhIyate, uta sadapi tadakAraNamityabhyupetya, atha tadeva nAstItyaN^gIkR^itya | AdyaM dUShayati- anAditvamiti ||
anAditvamivAnAditvaM pralaye sattvamityarthaH | kvachiditi sR^iShyikAle | yadyadR^iShyaM pralaye na syAttadA.a.adikAlInasya kAryasya kAraNaM na syAt.h | asataH kAraNatvAyogAt.h | tathAcha sarvotpattimatAM nimittamityabhyupagamo bhagna ityatharH | 
syAdetat.h | adhunAtanakAryamadR^iShyakAraNakaM na tvAdikAlInamiti mamAbhyupagamaH | tatkimadR^iShyasya pralaye sadbhAvenetyata Aha- anAditvamiti || anAditvaM vinA tata evAdikAlInakAyarkAraNatvaM cha vinA.adR^iShyaM kvachidadhunAtane.api kArye kAraNaM kathaM syAt.h | na kathaJNchit.h | adhunAtanaM kAryam.h adR^iShyakAraNakaM na, kAryatvAdAdikAlInakAryavadityanumAnasambhavAt.h | na chedidamiva tadapyadR^iShyakAryamevAN^gIkAryamiti |
yadvA mA bhUdAdikAlInasya kAryasyAdR^iShyaM kAraNam.h | tathA.api pralaye tadbhAvo.aN^gIkaraNIyaH | kutaH | anAditvaM pralaye sattvaM, vinA.adR^iShyaM kvachididAnIntane.api kArye kAraNaM kathaM syAt.h | antarAla evAdR^iShyotpattyayogAditi yojyam.h | 
nanvadR^iShyasya sarvotpattimannimittatve.api na pralaye sadbhAvo.abhyupagantavyaH | AdikAla evotpannasyApi mahadAdikAraNatvopapatteriti | idamatra vaktavyam.h | tadAdikAle janimadadR^iShyaM tataH pUrvAdR^iShyAdutpadyate na veti | AdyamupAdatte- pUrveti ||
jAyata iti sheShaH | pariharati- naiveti || evaM tarhi taduttaramAdikAle janimadadR^iShyaM naivAsmAbhiH pakShIkriyate | kintu tatkAraNaM pralayakAlInaM pUrvAdR^iShyameveti kuta AshrayAsiddhiriti | 
dvitIyamupAdatte- pUrveti || naivotpadyata iti sheShaH | dUShayati- uttaramiti || tarhi taduttaramAdikAlInamadR^iShyaM kuto jAyate | na kutashchit.h | sarvotpattimannimittasyAdR^iShyasyAbhAvAdAdikAlInAdR^iShyotpattireva na syAdityarthaH | 
na brUmo vayaM sarvaM kAryamadR^iShyajanyamiti | kiM tarhyAdikAle janimato mahadAdikAraNAdadR^iShyAdanyadevAto noktadoSha ityAshaN^kAmutthApya dUShayati- pUrveti || yadi parAdR^iShyaM sR^iShyayupakrame janimatpUrvAdR^iShyAnnaivotpadyate | api tvadR^iShyanirapekShameva | tarhyuttaramahadAdikAyarmapi kuto.adR^iShyAdutpadyata ityaN^gIkaraNIyam.h | adR^iShyavattasyApyadR^iShyinirapekShatvasambhavAt.h | anyathA kAryatvAdadR^iShyasyApyadR^iShyApekShA.aN^gIkAyareti |
astu tarhyadR^iShyaM kAraNameva na bhavatIti dvitIyaH pakShaH, adR^iShyameva nAstIti tR^itIyo vA, ubhayasyApyanupalambhAt.h | tathAchAshrayAsiddhiraparihAryetyAshaN^kayAha- adR^iShyamiti ||
yadi pratyakSheNAnupalambhAdadR^iShyaM na syAt.h | sadapi vA kAraNaM na syAt.h | tadA laye cha kiM mAnaM bhavet.h | pralayo.apyaprAmANikatvAnna syAt.h | na hyasAvapi pratyakSheNopalabhyate | tathAcheshvarAdikaM pralaye.asadbhavitumarhatItyaprasiddhavisheShaNaH pakShaH parasyApi syAt.h | 
atha matam.h | kAlaviprakarShAdanupalabha(bhya)mAno.api pralayo.anumAnasiddhatvAdaN^gIkaraNIyaH | tathAhi | vishvasantAno.ayaM dR^ishyasantAnashUnyaiH samavAyi(ntAni)bhirArabdhaH santAnatvAt.h AraNeyasantAnavat.h | vartamAnabrahmANDaparamANavaH pUrvamutpAditasajAtIyasantAnAntarAH nityatve sati tadArambhakatvAt.h pradIpaparamANuvat.h | sarve santAnAH kadAchitsahochChidyante santAnatvAt.h pradIpasantAnavat.h | sarva eva paramANavaH kadAchitsamagropAdeyaprabandhashUnyAH ArambhakatvAt.h naShyapavanArambhakaparamANuvat.h | bhUgolakasantAnaH kadAchitsAkalyenochChidyate santAnatvAt.h dIpasantAnavat.h | iyaM kriyA 
svAnyAvayayikAlInatvAnadhikaraNakiJNchitkAlInakriyA.anyA kriyAtvAdanyakriyAvaditi |
evaM tarhi dharmAdharmAvapi svarUpato viprakR^iShyatvAdanupalabhyamAnAvapi devadattasharIrAdikaM devadattavisheShaguNajanyaM kAryatve sati devadattabhogahetutvAt.h devadattaprayatnajanyasragAdivadityAdyanumAnena vichitrakAryAnyathA.anupapattyA, "jyotiShyomena svargakAmo yajeta',"yo brAhmaNAyAvagurettaM shatena yAtayA(ye)t.h' ityAdishrutasAdhyasAdhanabhAvAnyathA.anupapattyA vA siddhatvAdabhyupagantavyAviti samaM samAdhAnam.h | 
atha manyase | nAnumAnAdinA dharmAdisiddhiH | tasyAbhAsatvAt.h | tathAhi | devadattasharIrAderdevadattavisheShaguNajanyatvaM kiM sAkShAtsAdhyamuta paramparayA | nAdyaH | dharmAdharmayorapyArambhakapreraNAdirUpeNaivopayogAN^gIkArAt.h | devadattasharIraM na sAkShAddevadattavisheShaguNajanyaM sharIratvAdyaj~nadattasharIravaditi satpratipakShatvAchcha | dvitIye tu janmAntarIyaprayatnArAdhitadevatAdvAreNopapatterarthAntaratA | devadattavisheShaguNajanyatayA vinA.api AkAshAderiveshvarechChayA devadattasya bhogahetutA sambhavatItyaprayojakatA cha | kAryavaichityaM cha dR^iShyakAraNavaichityAdevopapadyate | AdikAlInaM cha tattatprAgabhAva eva vaichityAN^gIkAreNa | svagaryAgAdeH sAdhyasAdhanabhAvashravaNaM tvasiddhameva yogyatAvirahAt.h | anyathAkhyAtimAshrityAbhyupagame.apanyathAsiddham.h | yAgAdyArAdhitAvaj~nAtadevatAdvAreNa svargAdyupapatteriti |
evaM tarhi pralayasAdhakAnumAnAnAma(pya)bhAsatvAnna taistatsiddhiriti tulyamuttaram.h | tathA hi | vimataH kAlo.avayaviyuktaH kAlatvAdidAnIntanakAlavat.h | vimato brAhmaNo brAhmaNapUrvako brAhmaNatvAtsammatavadityAdinA satpratipakShaM tAvaduktAnumAnajAtam.h | nanu pralayakAlapakShIkR^itAvAshrayAsiddhiH | anyathA siddhasAdhanam.h | evamAdyabrAhmaNapakShIkAre.anyathA cha doSha iti chenna | parvato.agnimAnityAdAvapyagnimadanagnimatpakShadUShaNasambhavena sarvAnumAnochChedaprasaN^gAt.h | nanvagnimattvadivyarirekeNApyasti parvatAdeH svarUpaM, shakyaM cha visheShAntareNAvadhArayitum.h | tatkathaM doShAvakAsha iti chet.h | tatkimavayavisambandhAsambandhau vihAya kAlavisheShasya svarUpameva nAsti, brAhmaNavyaktervA.a.adyatvAnAdyatve vihAya | avadhAraNaM cha kAlAderhiraNyagabharApavargottara(rgAnantara)bhAvitvAdinA bhaviShyati |
