kiJNcha prathamaprayoge vishvashabdena kiM brahmANDamabhipreyate sakalakAyarANi vA | nAdyaH | ashrayAsiddheH | pralayamanabhyupagachChatA brahmANDasyAnaN^gIkR^itatvAt.h | brahmANDAbhAve.api kAryAntarAvasthitisambhavena pralayAsiddheshcha | kapikapolAntargataudumbarodaravartimashakasharIrAdivatkAryAntarAvasthAnamasambhAvitamiti chenna | kuNDabadaravadupapatteH | kAlAgnirudrAdiprakriyAyA asiddhatvAt.h | dvitIye.api na pralayasiddhiH | yathA hIdAnIntanAnAM dahanapavanasantAnAnAM krameNAstamaye.api na pralayastathA tarugirisharIrAdisantAnAnAmapi kramArambhasiddhAvapyavayavishUnyasamayA siddheH | athaikadaiveti visheShaNamupAdIyeta tadA kramArabdhadahanapavanAdisantAnairvyabhichAraH syAt.h | ekadarambhakahetusAkalye satIti hetuvisheShaNe visheShaNAsiddhiH | dvayaNukAdikrameNArambhasvIkAreNa bAdhAdiprasaN^gashcha |
etena dvitIyAnumAnamapi nirastam.h | brahmANDAnabhyupagamAt.h | abhyupagame.apyavayavAnAmAvApoddhArAbhyAmevotpAdavinAshayorupapatteH | kAryAntarAvasthAnopapatteshcha | tR^itIye.apyapasiddhAntaH | krameNochChedasyAbhyupagamA(tatvA)t.h | chaturthe.api paTAdibhyaH pUrvavinaShyaistantvAdibhivyarbhichAraH | paramANutvena hetuvisheShaNe.api dvayaNukAdyavasthAnasambhavena dR^iShyAntasya sandigdhasAdhyatA | paJNchame.api kiM bhUgolakA eva santAnashabdenochyante tadatirikto vA kashchit.h | Adye siddhasAdhanam.h | avayavAnAmAvApoddhArAbhyAM santatotpattivinAshasiddheH | dvitIye tvAshrayAsiddhiH | ShaShThaM tvAbhAsasamAnayogakShematvAdupekShaNIyamiti |
atha mA bhUdanumAnaiH pralayasiddhiH, tathA.apyAgamairbhaviShyati, teShAM siddhArthe.api prAmANyasya sAdhitatvAt.h, tato nAprasiddhavisheShaNateti brUShe, tarhyasmAkamapi dharmAdisiddhirAgamAdbhaviShyatIti kathamAshrayAsiddhiriti | evaM pralaye jIveshvarasadbhAvaM sAdhayatA dharmAdisattvamapi sAdhitamiti na pralaye bhAvamAtrAsattvasAdhanaM yuktam.h | evam.h AdikAyarM pakShIkR^itya sopAdAnatvasAdhane prakR^ityAdisiddhirapi draShyavyeti |
prathamasUtre.abhAvasya kartR^itvanirAsAyAnumAnamuktam.h | idAnImito.api nAbhAvakartR^ikaM jagat.h, chetanakartR^ikatve "dR^iShyAntabhAvAt.h' iti sUtrasya vR^ittyantaramabhipretya chetanakartR^ikatve anumAnamAha- utpattIti ||
buddhimAnutpattinAshakArIti buddhipUrvaM tatkartetyarthaH | kvachitpaTAdau | sarvatra vipratipanne kArye | mahadAdikArya ityevokte.aN^kurAdau vyabhichAraH shaN^kayeta, tadarthaM tasyApi pakShanikShepArthaM sarvatretyuktam.h | katarA buddhimAniti sheShaH | anyathA.abhAvakartR^itvavAdinaM 
prati siddhasAdhanatAprasaN^gAt.h | kimAkShepe | ananumAne na kimapi kAraNam.h | dR^iShyAntAbhAvena pratipakShAsambhavAdityarthaH | 
etena "svapakShadoShAchcha' iti sUtramapi vyAkhyAtaM bhavati | ayamatra prayogakramaH | vimataM kAryaM chetanotpAdyaM kAryatvAdghaTavat.h | chetanavinAshyaM cha tata eva tadvadeva | vimatotpattishchetanakartR^ikA utpattitvAtpaTotpattivat.h | vimato vinAshashchetanakartR^iko vinAshatvAtsammatavaditi | atra vinAshasya chetanakartR^ikatvasAdhanaM prAsaN^gikam.h | yadvA kechitkAraNasya bIjAdeH pradhvaMsenAN^kurAdeH janmadarshanAttantvAdinAshena paTAdinAshadasharnAchcha pradhvaMsAbhAvasyaiva jagajjanmavinAshakartR^itvamAsthitAH | yathoktam.h | nAnupamR^idya prAdurbhAvAditi | tanmataM vA.atrAsadityAdisUtrairnirAkR^itamiti j~nApanArtham.h | dR^iShyAntAbhAvastu svayamUhanIyaH | 
nanvidamanumAneneshvarasya jagatkartR^itvasAdhanaM sUtrakArasya uktaviruddham.h | shAstrayonitvAditIshvare.anumAnaprAmANyasya svayameva nirAkR^itatvAdityata Aha- Agameti ||
anumeti vakShyamANamatrApi sambaddhayate | na sarvathA.apIshvare.anumAnasya prAmANyaM sUtrakR^itA nirAkR^itam.h | kinnAmAgamAnanugR^ihItasya | AgamAnugR^ihItA tvanumA Ishvare mAnamevAbhimatA | anyathA vedavAkyArthe yuktyanusandhAnarUpajij~nAsA nArabheteti |
kimato yadyevamityata Aha- eSheti ||
AgamAnugR^ihItetyanuvartate | mAnamiti cha | eShA sampratyupanyastA.apyanumA "yato vA imAni bhUtAni' ityAgamAnugR^ihItA | tato bhavatIshvare mAnamiti na kashchidvirodha iti | 
evamanumAnenAbhAvakartR^ikatvaM vishvasyAshaN^kayAnumAnenaiveshvarakartR^ikatvaM samarthitam.h | tadetanmatAntareNAkShipya samAdadhatsUtram.h OM tarkApratiShThAnAdapyanyathA.anumeyamiti chedevamapyanirmokShaprasaN^gaH OM iti || tatrAkShepasyAyamarthaH | nAyamanumAnAvaShyambhena pUvarpakShaH pramANena cha siddhAnto bhavati | na chAnumAnaM nAma pramANamasti | (kutaH|) anyathA.apyanumeyam.h | asatpratipakShatvaM hyanumAnaprAmANyavAdibhiranumAnAN^gamaN^gIkaraNIyam.h | pratiruddhasya karaNasya kvApi kriyAniShpAdakatvAdarshanAt.h | anumAnapratipannaM chAnyathA.apyanumeyam.h anumAtuM shakyam.h | kasmAt.h | tarkApratiShThAnAm.h | "evamevAnumAtavyam.h, na punaranyathA' iti tarkasya vyavasthA.abhAvAt.h | tathA choktam.h | "upAdhipratipakShau tu kva nAmAtIva durvachau' iti |
nanvidaM vyadhikaraNaM, tarkasyApratiShThitatvAdanyathA.anumeyamiti | maivam.h | etadanena j~nApayati sUtrakAraH, "na tarko.anumAnAdbhidyate' iti | athavA tarkasyAnumAnasyApratiShThAnAdapramANatvAnnAnumAnena pUrvottarapakShau yuktau | kathamapramANatvAt.h | yato.anyathA.anumeyamiti yojanA | 
tatra samAdhAnasUtraM saN^gamayitumutsUtrameva bhAShyakArastAvaduttaramAha- Agameti ||
AgamagrahaNaM pramANamAtropalakShaNam.h | ata evottarArdhe.akShajamapi saN^gR^ihItam.h | pramANAnugrahapramANamUlatvashabdAbhyAM pratiShThitaprAmANyapramANAntarAvadhR^itapakShaliN^gavyAptimattvaM tatsaMvAditvaM chochyate | 
tatrAdyayojanAyAmasyAyamarthaH | yaduktamanumAnasyAvyavasthitatvena sarvatra pratyanumAnasambhava iti tadanupapannam.h | yataH pramANAnugrahAbhAve tarko na pratiShThitaH syAt.h | kintu pramANamUlasyaivAsya pratiShThitiH syAt.h | etaduktaM bhavati | pratyanumAnaM bhavatkiM pramANAnugraharahitaM syAt.h, uta tanmUlam.h | AdyaM tu kathaM svayamadR^iDhabhUmikaM paraM pratirundhyAt.h | nahi bhavati tarakShoH pratipakSho hariNashAvaH | kintvAdyenaiva pramANamUlena bAdhyate | dvitIyaM tu syAdeva pramANam.h | AdyaM chApabAdheta | ubhayathA.api na sarvAnumAnAprAmANyam.h | yada tUbhayoH api pramANamUlatvasandehaH tadA.astu pratirodhaH | kintu naivaM sarvatra | avadhAraNAyAM tu pUrvaiva gatiriti |
dvitIyayojanAyAM tu praShyavyam.h | kiM pramANAnugraharahitamanumAnaM pratyanumAnaparAhatatvAdapramANam.h, uta tanmUlam.h | Adye sampratipattimuttaramAha- Agameti || (tathA.api) naivaM sarvatreti bhAvaH | pratiShThitaH pramANabhUtaH | dvitIye tvAha- akShajeti || 
pratiShThitaH prAmANyam.h | tenaiva pratiprayogasya bAdhitatvAt.h | ubhayorvAstavapramANamUlatvAsambhavAditi bhAvaH | 
yastvetAM vyavasthAmanabhyupagamya sarvatrApi pratipakShasyAstyavakAsha iti sarvamanumAnamapramANamiti cha manyate tasya sUtrArUDhamuttaramAha- anyatheti ||
etenaivamupapAdite.api yo naivaM manyate tasya svavachanavyAghAtAdanirmokShaprasaN^ga iti sUtrayojanA sUchitA | tathAhi | sarvamanumAnapramANaM pratipakShapratihatatvAditi tvadIyamanumAnaM pratipakShaparAhataM chApramANaM cha bhavati na vA | Adye nAnena sarvasyAprAmANyasiddhiH | dvitIye tvatraiva bAdhAditi | anyathA uktavyavasthAM vihAya, asya sarvasyApyanumAnasya apratiShThA 
apramANatA, svavAchaiva vyAhatA hIti | 
apare tu "na vilakShaNatvAt.h' ityAdIni sUtrANi brahmaNo jagadupAdAnatvAkShepasamAdhAnArthatayA vyAchakShate | tatprakR^ityadhikaraNa eva nirAkR^itam.h | 
yachchAtra sUtre tarkApratiShThAnAditi vAkyaM bhittvA siddhAntatayaiva varNayanti, tadvA anena sArdhena shlokena nirAchaShye | tathAhi tarkasyApratiShThAM vadanvaktavyaH | kiM pramANAnugraharahitasyota tanmUlasya | 
Adye gUDhAbhisandhiruttaramAha- Agameti || ayamAshayaH | satyametat.h | tathApi na sAN^khayaH svatarkasyAgamAdyanugrahAbhAvaM manyate | svamatenedamuchyate chetpaunaruktyam.h | shAstrayonitvAt.h, IkShaternAshabdam.h, AnumAnikamityadinA.asyArthasyoktatvAditi | 
dvitIyaM dUShayati- akShajeti || nahi j~nAnakaraNasya pramANagR^ihItavyAptyAdimattvenAprAmANyakAraNavyabhichArAdishaN^kAkalaN^kavikalasya prAmANyaM nAstIti yuktamiti bhAvaH | vipakShe bAdhakaM chAha- anyatheti || anyathoktAnabhyupagamenAsya pramANamUlasyApyanumAnasyApratiShThA svavAchA vyAhataiva sUtrakR^itaH syAt.h | svayameva hi yuktyanusandhAnarUpAM brahmamImAMsAmArabhya pramANamUlasyApi tarkasyAprAmANyamabhidadhAnaH sUtrakAro na vyAhatabhAShI kathaM syAt.h | yadapi vR^ittikArairuktam.h "ekena tArkikeNotprekShitaM tarkamaparo dUShayati, tenotprekShitamapyaparaH, ityataH puruShamativaishvarUpyajanmA tarkaH syAdapratiShThitaH' iti | tachchAyuktam.h | yato.asyApi tarkasya prAmANye.aprAmANye vA asyApratiShThA cha sva(vAchA)vyAhataiveti nAyaM vAkyabhedo yukta ityukta eva sUtrArthaH |  Vyasa-(17) 

atra sUtram.h OM etena shiShyA aparigrahA api vyAkhyAtA iti | tatkechidvayAchakShate | etena "navilakShaNatvAt.h' ityAdinA prakR^itena shiShyaiH kenachidaMshena parigR^ihItasya pradhAnakAraNavAdasya nirAkaraNena shiShyairmanuvyAsaprabhR^itibhiH kenachidapyaMshenAparigR^ihItA ye.aNvAdikAraNavAdAste.api vyAkhyAtA draShyavyA iti | tadidaM dUShayati- nacheti ||
AstAM tAvadabhyadhikAshaN^kAprakAraH, parihArAtideshaprakArashcha | yattAvaduktam.h "sAN^khayAdapi vaisheShikAderatishayena shiShyAgR^ihItatvam.h' tadati(tIva)viruddham.h | sAN^khayasya nirIshvaratvAt.h | vaisheShikAdestu seshvaratvAt.h | vaiparItyasyaivochitatvAt.h | iha hi brahmaNo jagatkAraNatve vipratipattayo nirasyante | tatra sAN^khayo brahmaiva nAbhyupaiti | kutastadIyaM jagatkAraNatvamityatishayena vedAntavAdavirodhitvAchChiShyAparigR^ihItaH | vaisheShikAdistu, brahma tasya jagannimittatvaM chAN^gIkR^ityopAdAnatAmAtraM nAN^gIkuruta itIShadvirodhitvAt.h IShachChiShyAparigR^ihIta iti yuktam.h | satkAryavAditvAdikaM tu prakR^itAsaN^gatameva | anyathA yAgIyahiMsAniShedhAdinA viparivartaH syAt.h | atha vedasaMvAdabAhulyAbAhulyaprayuktamidam.h | maivam.h | (tanna | tattvAnAM) pratipAdyAnAmaparisaN^khayAtatvAditi | 
kiM tarhyasya sUtrasyAbhidheyamityata Aha- ata iti ||
arthAntarasya nirAkR^itatvAdityarthaH | apavyAkhyAnanirAkaraNasya svavyAkhyAnadArDhyAthartvAnnAsaN^gatamiti sUchayitumata ityuktam.h | avashiShyA nirAkR^itAyA abhAvakartR^itAyAH, jIvAdikartR^itA, jagata iti sheShaH | anena nirAkR^itAdavashiShyA vedAparigR^ihItA jIvapradhAnAsatkAlasvabhAvAdivAdA nirAkR^itA iti vyAkhyAtaM bhavati | tatra shiShyA ityevokte brahmakAraNavAdo.api prApnoti | tadarthamaparigrahA ityuktam.h | tanmAtre tUkte abhAvakartR^itvavAdo.api gR^ihyeta | tathAcha punaruktiratideshAnupapattishcha syAt.h | ataH shiShyA ityuktam.h | abhyadhikAshaN^kAsadbhAvasUchanena sUtrArambhopapAdanArthaM cha shiShyAH shiShyatayA pratItAH, natu tata eva nirAkR^itatayeti | 
nanu jIvAdItyAsidagrahaNenAsatkartR^ikatvaM gR^ihItam.h | tasya "asaditi chet.h' ityAdinA nirastatvena paunaruktyAdiprasaN^gAdityata Aha- tanmana iti ||
ityAdeH pramANAt.h | AshaN^kiteti sheShaH | AdipadenoktayuktirgR^ihyate | asataH abhAvasya | manasa iti | j~nAnechChAprayatnebhyaH janiH | jagata iti sheShaH | pUrvatra tviti sambandhaH | tachcha pratiShedhamAtratvAdityAdinA sphuTamavagamyata iti hishabdaH | akasmAddhIdamAvirAsIdityAdishrutyA | tat.h mano, vinA | asataH shUnyAt.h | 
etaduktaM bhavati | pUvarmabhAvasya jagatkAraNatvaM nirAkR^itamidAnIM tu shUnyasya | kiJNcha pUrvaM kartR^itvenAdhunA kartR^itAM vinaiveti na paunaruktyAdIti | yadvA bhAShyadishA niShkAraNaivAtra jagajjanirAshaN^kiteti na paunaruktyAdikam.h | atra shaN^kAprApakapramANopanyAsastu asyaiva prameyabhedasyopapAdanArtham.h | 
etenAbhyadhikA shaN^kA.api sUchitA | tathAhi | mA bhUdabhAvakartR^ikaM jagat.h, tathApi jIvAdibhyo janimadbhaviShyati | "jIvAdbhavanti bhUtAni',"pradhAnAdidamutpannam.h',"akasmAddhIdamAvirAsId.h' ityAdishrutyanugR^ihItebhyo ghaTadadhikaNTataikShNAdidR^iShyAntebhyaH | nahi jIvAdInAM pratiShedhamAtratvamasti, yenoktayuktivirodhaH syAt.h | asattvAchetanatvAderupalakShaNametaditi chet.h | kimatrAsadAdeH kAraNatvamAtraM netyuchyate, kiMvA kartR^itvam.h | nAdyaH | uktadR^iShyAnteShu vyabhichArAt.h | na dvitIyaH | kartR^itvasyAsmAbhiranaN^gIkR^itatvAditi | ata evAtra sarvatra kartR^ishabdaH kAraNatvamAtraparo draShyavyaH | 
nanvatra jIvAdervishvakAraNatvamAtraM shaN^kayate, tasyaiva vA | Adye na siddhAntavirodhaH | jIvasya hyadR^iShyAdhAratayA nimittatvaM pradhAnasya chopAdAnatvamaN^gIkR^itameva | na dvitIyaH | prApakAbhAvAt.h | kAryasya sakartR^ikatvaniyamadarshanAchchetyata Aha- prApakamiti ||
dvitIya evAshaN^kayate | tasya cha prApakaM "na jIvAtkAraNaM param.h',"na hyanyatkAraNaM matam.h' ityAdivAkyam.h | nacha lokavirodhaH | vAkyamAtrasiddhe.arthe tatpratipannameva gR^ihyate natu loko.anugamyata iti pUrvapakShI manyata iti |
nanu cha pradhAnakAraNatvAdimatAni dvitIyapAde nirAkariShyate | teShAmatrApi nirAkaraNe punaruktidoShaH syAdityato vA.a.aha- prApakamiti || atra shaN^kAprApakaM vAkyamAtraM natu samaya ityarthaH | idamuktaM bhavati | atra shrutyanugR^ihItAbhiryuktibhiH prAptaM pradhAnAdikAraNatvaM nirAkriyate | uttaraM(ratra) tu tu sAN^khayAdisamayaprAptam.h | ato.api noktadoSha iti |
nanvevaM tarhyetenetyatideshaH katham.h | uktaparihArasya pUrvapakShiNA parihR^itatvAdityata Aha- parihAra iti ||
yadyapi pratiShedhamAtratvaM pradhAnAdiShvasiddham.h | achetanatvAdikaM cha kAraNatvamAtravAde anaikAntikam.h | tathA.api pUrvapakShANAM yuktiviruddhatvaM yatpratiShedhamAtratvAt.h dR^iShyAntabhAvAditi sAmAnyataH sUchitam.h, yachcha svapakShadoShAchchetyaprAmANikatvaM, sa parihAro.atrApyavisheShitaH samAnaH, ityatidesho yujyata ityarthaH | 
nanu kathaM jagato jIvakartR^itvAdivAdasya yuktiviruddhatvamityata Aha- kvachiditi || 
kvachit.h deshAdau | yadvA kvachit.h jIvAdau | akR^itamiti cha bhAvapradhAno nirdeshaH | kAraNatvamAtramatra pUrvapakSho na kartR^itvamityato.achetanAditi paJNchamIprayogaH | achetanAdakR^itaM cha dR^iShTvA | evashabdena dR^iShyAntAnAmasandigdhasAdhyatAmAha | anumA anumitiH | anyathA vastutvasyaivAnumAnatvAtpaJNchamI na syAt.h | jIvAkR^itatvAderiti sheShaH | anyatra mahadAdau | 
atraite prayogAH | mahadAdikAryaM na jIvakR^itaM vastutvAjjIvavat.h, vimataM na pradhAnakAryaM vastutvAtpradhAnavat.h, vimataM nAsatkAryaM vastutvAdghaTavaditi | yadyapi jIvasya nimittatvena pradhAnasyopAdAnatvena jagatkAraNatvamaN^gIkR^itameva tathA.api svAtantAbhAvAbhiprAyeNedaM vachanamiti na virodhaH | 
nanvevaM satyatiprasaN^gaH syAt.h | vimatamashvarakR^itaM na bhavati vastutvAdIshvaravat.h ityapi prayoktuM shakyatvAdityata Aha- shruteriti || "sa idaM sarvamasR^ijata' ityAdishrutermahadAderIshvarakR^itatvAvadhAraNAdatiprasaN^gAnumAnasya bAdhitatvenAprAmANyamiti | samaM tarhIdaM bhavadanumAneShu | jIvAdbhavanti bhUtAnItyAdishruterityata Aha- shruteriti || bhAvapradhAno nirdeshaH | jIvAdishabdAnAM brahmashrutitvAdbrahmanAmatvAnna shrutivirodha ityarthaH | tatkuta ityata Aha- shruteriti || "nAmAni sarvANi yamAvishanti' ityAdishruteH | sheShaM bhAShye |
nanu jIvAdikAraNa(ka)tve.api ghaTAdidR^iShyAntAvaShyambhenAnumAnasambhavAtkathamaprAmANikatvamityata Aha- shruteriti || "nAnyo.ato.asti kartA' ityAdishruterbAdhitaviShayatvAt.h dR^iShyAntAnAM sAdhyavaikalyAchcha nAnumAnAnAM prAmANyam.h | 
etenAsmadanumAne.akAryatvamupAdhirityapi nirastaH(m.h) | (svAtanteNa) jIvAdyakR^ite.api ghaTAdAvakAryatvAbhAvAt.h | pratipakShe bAdhAdidoShAnuShaN^gAchcheti sarvaM sustham.h | 
|| iti shrImannyAyasudhAyAM asadadhikaraNam.h ||
|| atha shrImannyAyasudhAyAM bhoktradhikaraNam.h |
|| OM bhoktrApatteravibhAgashchetsyAllokavat.h OM || atItAdhikaraNe brahmaNo jagajjanmAdikAraNatve shrutisaMvAditvena prabalayA yuktyA virodhaH parihR^itaH | idAnIM tu shrutisiddha(liN^ga)tvena prabalayA yuktyA virodhaH parihriyate | 
tathAhi | na brahmaNo jagatkAraNatvaM vAstavaM sambhavati | asarvakAraNena mukte(ktajIve)nAtyantAbhinnatvAt.h | nahi yo yenAtyantAbhinnaH sa tadviruddhasvabhAvo vastuta iti kvachidupalabdham.h | nacha muktasyAsarvakAraNatvamasiddham.h, (sarvakAraNatvasya) saMsAre.anupalambhAt.h | saMsAre pratIyamAnasya kasyachidAkArasyaivApagamo hi mokSho natu apUrvAkArotpAdaH, anityatvaprasaN^gAt.h | 
nachAnandAderiva vidyamAnasyaivAvidyayA tirohitatvAtsarvakAraNatvasyAnupalambha iti vAchyam.h | pramANAbhAvAt.h | AnandAdeH paramapremAspadatvAdinA IShadupalabdheshcha | nacha brahmaNo jagatkAraNatvashravaNAtsavarthA.anupalabhyamAnamapi jagatkAraNatvaM saMsAre kalpyamiti yuktam.h | shruteH kAlpanikajagatkAraNatvAnuvAditvenApi sAvakAshatvAt.h | nacha tathAbhUtameva lakShaNamastviti vAchyam.h | anaN^gIkArAt.h | kAlpanikasya jagatkAraNatvasya pradhAnAdiShvapi sambhavenAtiprasaN^gAchcha | syAdetat.h | muktasya brahmaNaikyamevAsiddhamiti | maivam.h | "karmANi vij~nAnamayashcha AtmA pare.avyaye sarva ekIbhavanti' ityAdishrutisiddhatvAditi | tadidamuktaM sUtrakR^itA bhokturjIvasya mokShe brahmatvApattishravaNAttayoravibhAgo bhedAbhAvaH | tatashcha na brahmaNo jagatkAraNatvaM vAstavaM yuktamiti | evaM prApte siddhAntitam.h | bhavedetadakhilaM yadi muktasya brahmaNA.abheda eva prAmANikaH syAt.h | nachaitadasti | shrautastvekIbhAvaprayogaH syAllokavat.h | yathA loke udake udakasyaikIbhAvavyavahAraH sthAnaikyanibandhanaH | yathA vA prAgvibhinnA brAhmaNAH sAmpratamekIbhUtA iti matyaikyanibandhanaH | tathA prAgvibhinnasthAnA bhinnamatayashcha jIvA muktau brahmaNA ekIbhavanti | ekasthAnA ekamatayashcha bhavantItyupapadyate | tasmAdasiddhenAsiddhasAdhanametaditi |
tadetadayuktam.h | mukhyAthare bAdhakAbhAvAt.h | vinA bAdhakena jaghanyavR^ittyAshrayaNe chAtiprasaN^gAt.h | ityato mukhyArthe bAdhakayuktivyutpAdanaparatvenApi syAllokavaditi sUtrakhaNDaM vyAchaShye- nAnyaditi ||
atra mukhyamevArthamaN^gIkurvANaH praShyavyaH | kiM prAgabhinnasyaiva jIvasya muktau brahmaNaikyamanenochyate, uta bhinnasya, atha(vA) bhinnAbhinnasya | nAdyaH, abhUtatadbhAvArthasyaikIbhavantIti chvipratyayasyaiva anupapatteH | ata eva na tR^itIyaH | aikyasya prAk.h siddhatvAt.h | bhedanivR^ittyarthatve tu gauNArthatvApatteH | dvitIyanirAkaraNena nirastatvAt.h (cha) | dvitIye tvidamupatiShThate, nAnyaditi | hishabdo hetau | yato loke anyat.h vastu, anyatvaM vastvantareNAbhedamApannam.h, kvachitkAle, kathaJNchanopAyena, na dR^iShyam.h | atastad.hdR^iShyAntena jIvasyApi kadAchana muktAvapi brahmabhAvo brahmatvaM na syAt.h | 
ayamatra prayogaH | jIvo na kAlAntare.api brahmaNaikyamApatsyate | prAk.h tato.atyantabhinnatvAt.h | yaH kadAchidyato.atyantaM bhidyate nAsau kadAchittadaikyamApadyate | yathA ghaTaH paTeneti | athavA jIvabrahmaNoH bhedaH, satorbhedinorna nivR^ittimAn.h, bhedatvAtstambhakumbhAdibhedavaditi | AgamabAdhitametaditi chenna | AgamAnAM mukhyArthatAsambhave.anumAnabAdhakatvaM, bAdhite chAnumAne teShAM mukhyArthateti parasparAshrayatvaprasaN^gAt.h | satpratipakShatvAchcha | tathAhi shrutiH | yathodakamityAdikA | pralhAdo.api "paramAtmAtmanoryogaH paramArtha itIShyate(tAm.h) | mithyaitadanyad.hdravyaM hi naiti tad.hdravyatAM yataH' iti |
atha matam.h | nAyamasti yuktivirodhaH | prAgapyabhinna eva brahmaNA jIva ityaN^gIkArAt.h | nacha chvipratyayAnupapattiH | pratItyapekShayA tadupapatteH | prAgvibhinnatayA dR^iShyo.ayaM jIvo brahmaNaH | athedAnIM muktAvabhinnatayA dR^ishyate, ityata ekIbhavantItyuchyata iti | atredaM vaktavyam.h | kiM prAktanI jIvabrahmaNorbhedadR^iShyirbhrAntiruta prameti | nAdyaH | bAdhakAbhAvAt.h | shrutayastvadyApyavyavasthitArthA na bAdhakatAmashnuvate | dvitIye tvAha- kvachiditi | 
kvachitkAle yadvastu yato bhinnatayA pramitaM tat.h kAlAntare.api kathaM tadabhinnatayA pratI(mI)yeta, na kathaJNchidityarthaH | kuta ityata Aha- no dR^iShyapUrvaM hIti || tAdR^ishaM prAgbhinnatayA pramitaM kAlAntare.abhinnatayA pramIyamANam.h | 
ayamiha prayogaH | jIvo na kadAchidbrahmAbhinnatayA pramAviShayaH | tato.atyantabhinnatayA pramitatvAt.h | yadevaM tadevaM yathA ghaTaH paTAdbhinnatayeti | yastu kvachidapi bhedapramAM na manyate, taM pratyAropitabhedamekaM vastu vyatirekodAharaNaM vAchyam.h | evaJNcha pratItimupAdAyApi na chvipratyayopapattiH | etadarthatvenApi syAllokavaditi yojyam.h | tadevaM grAvaplavanAdishrutivat.h upapattiviruddhatvena shrutermukhyArthAsambhavAdamukhyArtha eva svIkaraNIye parakIyahetorasiddhatvAnna brahmaNo jagatkAraNatve yuktivirodha iti siddham.h | 
kechididaM sUtramanyathA vyAchakShate | pUrvaM kila chetanAchetanAtmakasya prapaJNchasya brahmopAdanatvena brahmAnanyatvamuktam.h | tadAkShipya samAdhAtumidaM sUtram.h | tathAhi | yadi chetanAchetanAtmakasya jagato brahmAnanyatvaM syAttadA chetano bhoktA bhogyashchAchetanA viShayA ityayaM vibhAgo na syAt.h | kutaH | bhogyasyApi bhoktR^itvApatteH | bhokturapi bhogyatvApatteH | bhavitavyaM chAnena vibhAgena | pratyakShAdisiddhatvAditi chet.h | syAllokavat.h | yathA loke samudrAtmanAmapi phenataraN^gAdInAM netaretarabhAvApattyA vibhAgabhaN^gaH, yathA vA mahAkAshAtmanAmapi ghaTamaThAdyAkAshAnAM, tathA prakR^ite.api syAditi | tadidaM dUShayati- bhoktR^itveti ||
yat.h yadi bhoktrApatterityatra bhoktratvApatteriti vyAkhyAnaM sUtrakArasyApi(bhi)mataM syAt.h tat.h tarhi kuto hariH sUtrakR^it.h bhoktrApatteriti (pra)Aha | bhoktR^itvApatterityeva brUyAt.h | nachaivamabravIt.h | tato nAyamabhiprAyaH sUtrakArasyeti |
yadyapyatra pareShAmasmAkaM chAdhyAhArasAmyam.h | tathA.api bhAvapratyayAbhAvaH parasyAdhikaH |
ye tu vyAchakShate "chidachidvastusharIratve brahmaNo jIvavatsukhaduHkhAdibhoktR^itvApatterjIvabrahmasvabhAvavibhAgo na syAditi chenna | yathA kAntAre nipatitasya(syApi) nR^ipasya na daMshamashakAdyupadravastathA.atrApi syAt.h' iti | teShAmapyayaM shabdadoShaH samAnaH |
nanu bhAvapradhAnA nirdeshAstatra tatra bahulamupalabhyante | tatkathamayaM doSho.abhidhIyate | ayamabhisandhibharAShyakArasya | pratipAdye vyavasthite tadbalAchChAbdI gauNatA kathaJNchidanusartavyA | nachAsya sUtrasyedaM pratipAdyaM vyavasthitam.h | jagadupAdAnatvasya prAganuktatvenAnuktopAlambhaprasaN^gAt.h | jagachCharIratvasyAntaryAmyadhikaraNe prasakte.api sambhogaprAptirityanenaiva parihR^itatvAt.h | tatra jIvasharIragatatvena (prasa(ktaM)katabhoktR^itvamapAstam.h | atra tu jagachCharIratveneti chenna | pUrvottarapakShayornyAyAvisheShe sUtrArambhAnupapatteH | ato nirnimittaH shAbdadoSho.api nAnusaraNArha iti | yadvaitadarthapratipAdanAya kathaM chetyAdyuttaravAkyamatrApi saMyojya vyAkhyeyamityukta eva sUtrArtha iti | 
|| iti shrImannyAyasudhAyAM bhoktradhikaraNam.h ||
atha shrImannyAyasudhAyAM ArambhaNAdhikaraNam.h |
|| OM tadananyatvamArambhaNashabdAdibhyaH OM || prAk.h pramANamUlatvatatsaMvAditvAbhyAM prabalayA yuktyA ukte(ktA)rthe virodho nirA(staH)kR^itaH | bAhulyalakShaNabalavadyuktivirodhaparihArAya idamadhikaraNamArabhyate | 
tadidaM brahmapariNAmavAdI vyAchaShye "anantarAdhikaraNe bhogyavargasya pariNAmataHsiddhaprAtisvikarUpabhedAnapahnavena lokasiddha(ddhaM)kAraNAbhedamaN^gIkR^itya sAN^khayasiddhAntena shAstrato bhoktR^ivargasya svAbhAvikarUpabrahmAvibhAge bhogyasyApi brahmaikyavadbhoktR^itvApattimAshaN^kaya anaikAntikatvena nirAso(vi).abhihitaH | samprati vaisheShikAdimatena svarUpakAryavyapadeshAdibhedena kAryasya kAraNAtma(ka)tvAsiddhayA prapaJNchasya brahmAdvaitam.h AkShipya samAdhIyate | tathAhi | tadananyatvaM tena brahmaNA ananyatvaM, kAryasya | kutaH? ArambhaNashabdAdibhyaH "yathA somyaikena mR^itpiNDena vij~nAtena sarvaM mR^iNmayaM vij~nAtaM syAt.h | vAchArambhaNaM vikAro nAmadheyaM mR^ittiketyeva satyam.h' ityadishabdAt.h | "Adi'grahaNAt.h "aitadAtmyamidaM sarvam.h',"yadayamAtmA',"sarvaM khalvidaM brahma' ityAditAdAtmyAvedakashrutiparigrahaH' iti |
vivartavAdI tu vyAkhyAti "abhyupagamya chemaM vyAvahArikaM bhoktR^ibhogyalakShaNaM vibhAgam.h, "syAllokavat.h' iti parihAro.abhihitaH | na tvayaM vibhAgaH pAramArthiko.asti | yasmAt.h tadananyatvaM kAraNAdbrahmaNaH kAryasyAkAshAdeH paramArthato.ananyatvaM vyatirekeNAbhAvaH, avagamyate | kutaH? ArambhaNashabdAdibhyaH' iti |
tatrAdyaM vyAkhyAnaM tAvannirAkaroti- kathaM cheti ||
kathamityAkShepe | chashabdaH pUrvasUtrApavyAkhyAnAkShepeNAsya samuchchayArthaH | jagata iti vakShyamANamatrApi sambaddhayate | "atra pratipAdyA syAt.h' iti sheShaH | ayamAshayaH | yo hi brahmopAdAnatAM jagato.abhyupagamyApi tadanyatAM manyate so.atra pUrvapakShIkaraNIyaH | nacha vaisheShikAdistatheti prAptyabhAvAnna tadananyatvokteravasaro.asti | brahmopAdAnatAmanaN^gIkurvANaM prati tu saiva samarthanIyA | natu tadananyatA | tadadhInasiddhitvAdasyAH | atha brahmopAdAnatApyatra samarthyata iti chet.h | na | tathA sati prakR^ityadhikaraNavaiyarthyApatteH | prakR^ityadhikaraNanyAyeno(yo)papAdi(taM)tamabhyupetyApi tadanyatAM manyamAno.atra pUrvapakShIti chet.h | na | kimidaM brahmopAdAnatvaM brahmasamavAyitvaM vA, brahmapariNAmatvaM vA, yatpareNAN^gIkAritam.h | nAdyaH (kalpaH) tasyAnanyatvavirodhAt.h | samavAyasya nirAkariShyamANatvAchcha | dvitIye prayatnavaiyarthyameva | nahi ko.api pariNAmavAdamaN^gIkR^itya kAyarkAraNayoratyantabhedamaN^gIkurute, yaM pratIdamArabhyeta iti |
yadvA kathaM cha tadananyatA jagato vaktuM shakyate | ananyatvaM hi bhedAbhAvaH | atyantAbheda iti yAvat.h | bhedAbhedau cha pareNAN^gIkR^itau | atastAdAtmyamiti vaktavyaM syAt.h | naiSha doShaH, yAvatA kAryasya kAraNenAbheda eva, kAraNasya tu kAryAdbheda eva, ityevaM bhedAbhedAvaN^gIkR^itAviti chenna | yadi brahma jagato.anyadeva tadA kathaM cha tadananyatvaM(tA) jagataH syAt.h | nahi yadyato.atyantabhinnaM tattenAtyantAbhinnamiti sambhavati, atiprasaN^gAditi |
athavA kathaM cha tadananyatA pratij~nAtuM yuktA | pramANAbhAvAditi sheShaH | nanu chArambhaNashabdAdibhya ityuktatvAtkathaM pramANAbhAva iti chet.h | atra vaktavyam.h | ArambhaNashabdastAvatkiM sAkShAjjagato brahmAnanyatvamAchakShIta, uta vikArasya vikAryananyatvam.h | Adye kathaM cha tadananyatA jagatosyArthaH syAt.h | yathA somyeti mR^itpiNDAdeH prakR^itatvAdityuttaram.h | dvitIye bhavatu nAma vikArasya vikAryananyatvam.h, jagatastu kathaM tadananyateti |
(nanu) vikArasya vikAryananyatve tenokte.api jagato brahmAnanyatvaM siddhayatyeva | tasyApi tadvikAratvAdityata Aha- jagatastviti ||
avikAratve brahmavikAratvAbhAve | uktanyAyena "nacha prakR^itiH' ityAdineti sheShaH | sAdhite sati kathaM cha tadananyatetyanvayaH | yadvA jagata iti pUrveNaiva sambaddhayate | avikAratve brahmaNa iti sheShaH | na vidyate vikAro yasyetyavikAram.h | tasya bhAvastattvaM, tasmin.h |
nanvatrArambhaNasha(bdasha)bdena "uta tamAdeshamaprAkShya(kShaH)' ityAdyA shrutirupalakShyate, tattAtparyaparyAlochanAyAM cha jagato brahmavikAratvaM tadanantyavaM chAvagamyate iti chenna | mahAvAkyAvAntaravAkyopakramatvapradhAnavAchitvAdyabhAvenAsya shrutyupalakShaNayopAdAne nimittAbhAvAt.h | abhyupetyApyupalakShaNatvamAha- avikAratva iti || vikarAtvAdanyasminsAdR^ishyAdau shrutyarthatayoktanyAyena sAdhite sati shrutitAtparyaparyAlochanayA cha kathaM tadananyatA siddhayediti |
yadapyuktamAdipadagR^ihItAdaitadAtmyamidaM sarvamityAdivAkyAttadananyatvasiddhiriti tadapyasat.h | Adipadena vAkyAntaragrahaNasyAnupapatteH | tathA satyeteShAmapi shabdatvenArambhaNAdishabdebhya iti prayogaprasaN^gAt.h | 
astu vA kathaJNchidAdipadopAttatA(tvaM)teShAM vAkyAnAm.h | tathA.api naitebhyastadananyatA siddhayati | upapattiviruddhatvAdityAshayena pR^ichChati- kathaM cheti || yA sUtrakR^itA pratij~nAtA shrutibhishcha pratipAditA sA jagatastadananyatA kathaM kiMprakArA | "kiM pikaH kokilaH' itivadekatvalakShaNA kiMvA mR^idghaTa itivadvikAra(ri)vikAri(ra)tvalakShaNeti prashnArthaH | 
AdyamAkShipati- kathaM cheti || ekatvalakShaNA jagatastadananyatA tu kathaM sUtrakR^itA pratij~nAyeta | kathaM cha shrutibhiH pratipAdyeta na kathaJNchidityarthaH | atra hetumAha- avikAratva iti || brahmaNo.avikAratva uktanyAyena sAdhite sati jagatastu vikArAtmakatve pratyakShAdipramite sati viruddhadharmAdhikaraNatvAditi bhAvaH | dvitIyamAkShipati- kathaM cheti || vikArivikAratvarUpa iti sheShaH | AkShepe yuktimAha- jagatastviti || vyAkhyAnaM pUrvavat.h |
nanvevamupapattiviruddhA.api jagato brahmAnanyatA.aN^gIkaraNIyA | anyathaitadAtmyamidaM sarvamityAdishrutInAmaprAmANyaprasaN^gAdityata Aha- kathaM cheti || avikAritve.api vikAratvAdanyasmiMstadadhInatvAdau shrutyarthe "svAtante cha vishiShyatve' ityuktanyAyena sAdhite sati kathaM tadananyatA.aN^gIkartumuchitA | sAvakAshashrutipratIto.apyartho niravakAshopapattivirodhAttyAjya eva | yathoktamabhimAnyadhikaraNa iti bhAvaH | 
aparamapi vyAkhyAnaM dUShayati- kathaM cheti || (iti) prAhetyanuvartate | yadyatra kAryamAtraprapaJNchasyAnR^itatvaM sUtrakR^ito.abhimataM syAt.h | tadA.anR^itatvamityeva brUyAt.h | tadananyatvamiti kathaM prAha | nahi brahmAnanyatvashabdo.anR^itatvAvAchI | tathA sati brahmaNo.apyanR^itatvaprasaN^gAt.h | 
nanu cha tadananyatvaM tadvayatirekeNAbhAva iti vyAkhyAtam.h | satyam.h | na tathA.apyanR^itatvalAbhaH | tadvayatirekeNa nAstItyukte tadAtmanA.astIti labhyate | na punaH sarvathA.apyanR^itatvam.h | anyathA brahmAtirekeNAsato jIvachaitanyasyApi sarvathA.anR^itatvaM syAt.h | prasiddhaM chaitat.h | yadvishiShya(viShayaH)pratiShedho visheShaNamupasaN^krAmatIti |
satyam.h | tathA.api brahmavivartatAj~nApanAyaivamuktamiti chet.h(na) | tathA sati tatrAropita(tva)miti vaktavyatvAt.h | nahi shuktikAshakale kaladhautamAropitamiti vaktavye tatonanyaditi prayuJNja(jya)te | 
atha brahmasattayaivedaM sat.h, nAparA sattA.asyAstIti j~nApanametasya prayojanamiti chet.h | tarhi paramArthasadevedamityAyAtamiti kathamanR^itatvam.h |
atha yeyaM prapaJNche sattA.avagamyate sA.adhiShThAnabrahmagataivAropitetyanena j~nApyata iti chet.h | tatminyathAkhyAtivAdivadanirvachanIyakhyAtivAdino.apyAropitAkArasyAnyatra pAramArthyamAvashyakam.h | tathAtve chAkAshatvAdikamapi brahmaNi pAramArthikamaN^gIkAryaM(raNIyaM) syAt.h | rajatatvAdikaM cha shuktikAyAmiti |
yadvA syAllokavaditi bhoktR^ibhogyaprapaJNchasya satyatAmabhidhAyedAnIM kathaM cha tadananyateti tadviruddhamanR^itatvaM prAheti yojanA | nanu sUtrakAraH paramArthAbhiprAyeNa tadananyatvamityAha | vyavahArAbhiprAyeNa tu syAllokavaditi | tatkuto virodha sati chenna | pratArakatvaprasaN^gAt.h | anyathA pratyAchakShIta | apratyAkhyAyaiva kAryaprapaJNchaM, pariNAmaprakriyAmAshrayati, saguNeShUpAsaneShUpayokShyata i(tI)ti chet.h | kiM saguNopAsanaviShayaprayojane prakR^itaviShayaprayojanAnukUle, uta tadviruddhe, athodAsIne | nAdyaH | bhedaviShayatvAt.h, sAMsArikaphalatvAchcha | bhedavAsanA hi sudR^iDhA tAmevopodbalayet.h | ata eva na tR^itIyo.api | na dvitIyaH 
anAptatvAparihArAditi |
athavA.a.astAM tAvadiyaM granthArjavachintA | kathaM cha tadananyatA.anR^itatvalakShaNA jagato yuktA syAt.h | na kathaJNchiditi yojyam.h | atra hetumAha- jagata iti || avikAritva brahmavivartatvAbhAve | yachchAvikR^itamityAdyuktanyAyena | evaM pramANAbhAvaparatvenApi pUrvavadvayAkhyeyamiti |
evaM tarhi ko.asyArtha ityata Aha- svatantreti ||
yata evaM jagato brahmAnanyatvamanekavidhamapi nAtra pratipAdyaM, tenetyarthaH | anenApavyAkhyAnanirAkaraNaM svavyAkhyAnadR^iDhIkaraNArthatvAnnAsaN^gatamiti smArayati | kartranadhInasattAshaktyAdimatkAraNAntaratavyapekShA khalu ghaTAdisR^iShyirdR^iShyA | tato, mahadAdisR^iShyirapi kartR^ivyatiriktasvatantrakAraNasavyapekShA sR^iShyitvAdghaTasR^iShyivat.h, mahadAdikaM vA kartR^ivyatiriktasvatantrakAraNAyatto sApekShotpattikaM kAyartvAdghaTavat.h, prakR^ityAdikaM vA svatantraM kAraNatvAnmR^idAdivat.h, Ishvaro vA svatantrakAraNasavya(NAntarasA)pekShaH kartR^itvAtkulAla(lAdi)vaditi yuktiviruddhatvAjjanmAdisUtre.abhipretaM yatparasyaiva brahmaNaH svAtantyaM tannopapadyate | nacha shrutivirodhaH | shrutInAM brahmaNo jagatkAraNatvamAtraparatvAt.h | svatantrakAraNAntaranirAse shruterabhAvAt.h | bhAve.apyapauruSheyatayA shrutiprAbalyavadbAhulyena yuktiprAbalyasyApi sambhavAt.h, satpratipakShatayA shru(tya)tyA.abhipretAvadhAraNAnupapatterityevaM prAptam.h | svatantrakAraNAnyatvaM brahmaNo.anyasya svatantrakAraNatvamiti yAvat.h | atra adhikaraNe | tadananyatvamityanena niShiddhayate | mahadAdisR^iShyau yatsvatantrakAraNaM tasya tadananyatvamiti |
yadyatra svatantrakAraNAbhAva ityeva brUyAt.h, tadA brahmaNo.api svAtantyaM pratiShiddhaM syAt.h | tadananyatvaM svatantrakAraNasyetyukte hi svatantrakAraNaM tadeva nAnyaditi labhyate | tadupapAdanAya yat.h "ArambhaNashabdAdibhyaH' iti svapakShe pramANamuktam.h, yashcha "bhAve chopalabdheH' iti vipakShe pramANAbhAvastadubhayaM hishabdena sUchayati |
nanvArambhaNAdyAkShepashabdAdibhya iti vaktavyam.h | satyam.h | lakShitalakShaNayaiSha evArthaH pratipAdyata ityadoShaH | tathA.api "kiMsvidAsIdadhiShThAnam.h' iti (R^i.saM.10-81-2) shrautanirdeshAnusAreNAdhiShThAnasyopAdAnamuchitamiti chenna | shAbdAdapyarthaprAdhAnyasya balavattvAt.h | sAdhakatamaM karaNamiti vachanA(smaraNA)t.h | nanu cha svatantrakAraNasya brahmAnanyatvaM pratij~nAya kAraNAntarAbhAve pramANopanyAso.asaN^gataH | maivam.h | astyatrAbhiprAyaH | vakShyate (hi) cha brahmAtiriktaprakR^ityAdikAraNasadbhAvaH | ArambhaNashabdAdibhyastadabhAvo.avagamyate | tatorthAtsvatantrakAraNAntarabhAve cha pramANairupalabdheH prasaN^ga iti vadanpramANAbhAvamAha | evaM manyate | shuShkAbhyo bahuyuktibhyo.api shrutyanugR^ihItAnAM bahvInAM yuktInAM prAbalyAttadviruddhAnAM pUrvapakShayuktInAmaprAmANyamiti |
syAdetat.h | adbhayaH sambhUta ityAdivachanAtkathaM brahmAtiriktasya svatantrakAraNasyAnupalabdhiH | nachAtra na svAtantyaM shrUyata iti vAchyam.h | pAratantAnuktau svAtantyasya lokAnurodhAdeva siddheriti | etatparihArAya sUtram.h OM sattvAchchAvarasyeti OM || tasyA(yama)rthaH | syAdayaM doSho yadi vayaM brahmAtiriktaM kAraNameva nAstIti vadAmaH | na chaivam.h | avarasya tadadhInasya prakR^ityAdeH kAraNasya sattvAditi | tadidaM parihArAya na paryAptam.h | yAvatA pUrvapakShiNA pAratantAnuktau svAtantyameva setyasyatItyuktam.h | anyathA pUrvapakShasya nirdalatvApatteH, ityataH prakR^ityAdeH kAraNajAtasyeshvarAdhInasattAkatva pramANaM darshayansUtraM vyAchaShye- dravyamiti ||
chetanAH jIvAH | dhR^itiH chitprakR^itiH, "dhArakatvAt.h' iti shruteH | prakR^ityAdestadvashasya bhAvaH aN^gIkriyate | ato.adbhayaH sambhUta ityatrApi svAtantAsiddhernAnupalabdhiryuktetyarthaH | yadyapi ArambhaNashabdAderadbhayaH sambhUta iti shruteshcha parasparaviredhAdatharApattyaivaiSho.artho labhyate | tathA.api mandApekShayA spaShyashrutyudAharaNam.h |
yadvA svatantrakAraNAnyatvaM niShiddhayata ityanena paratantrakANAntarasadbhAvaH sUchitaH | anyathA kAraNAnyatvamityeva syA(brUyA)t.h | (sa) paratantrakAraNasadbhAvaH kR^ita ityata Aha- dravyamiti || bhAvo gamyata iti sheShaH | atra tadvashatvaM vidheyam.h | kArarasadbhAvasya pareNApyaN^gIkR^itatvAt.h |
|| OM asadvayapadeshAnneti chenna dharmAntareNa vAkyasheShAt.h OM || iti sUtram.h | tatra AkShepasyAyamarthaH | "nAsadAsInnosadAsIttadAnIm.h' iti mahApralaye mUrtAmUrtAderasheShasyAsattvavyapadeshAtkAraNopalabdhiparichodanA, tasyeshvaravashasyAN^gIkAreNa samAdhAnaM cha nopapadyate | nachAyaM pakShaH "asaditi chet.h' ityAdinaiva nirAkR^itaH | tatreshvarasyApyanaN^gIkArAt.h | iha punarIshvaramaN^gIkR^itya kAraNAntaranirAkaraNAt.h | nacha "adbhayaH sambhUtaH' ityAdivirodhaH | 
atra mahApralaye kAraNAntarasadbhAvasyAshravaNAt.h | IshvarAtiriktakartR^ikAsu sR^iShyiShvabAdikAraNasadbhAvaparatvAchcha | evaJNchArambhaNashabdAdayo.api samaJNjasA bhavantIti | (atra) neti siddhAntAMshaM vyAchaShye- dravyamiti || na mahApralaye kAraNAntarasyAbhAvo vAchyaH | kintu tadvashasya bhAva eva | tasya tadvashatvaM kuta iti chet.h | dravyamiti shruteriti | 
 Vyasa-(18) 

nanu "nAsadAsIt.h' iti sarvasyAsattvavyapadeshAtkathaM netyata uktaM "dharmAntareNa' iti | tadvayAchaShye- tadvashasyeti || sAvadhAraNaM chedam.h | tadvashasyaiva bhAvaH pralaye, na svatantrasya | tataH svAtantyalakShaNadharmavisheShAbhiprAyeNAsattvavyapadesho yujyate | upalakShaNametat.h | yathoktaM bhAShye | yatkhalu paratantramavyaktaM kAryAnabhimukhaM tadasaditi vyapadishyate | 
kutaH shruteH mukhyArthaparityAgenAmukhyArtho.aN^gIkriyate | "tama AsIt.h' ityAdivAkyasheShAt.h | nacha tamo brahma, "AnIdavAtam.h' iti tasya pR^ithagavasthAnokteH | nachAnantaprakAshasya tamastvamupapadyate | kintu prakR^itereva, AchChAdakatvAderiti | 
nanu cha pralaye.avasthitaM chetprakR^ityAdi tasya svAtantAdidharmAbhAvaH kutaH, yenaivaM vyAkhyAyata iti chet.h | vAkyopakramatachCheShayorvirodhAdarthApattyaiveti brUmaH | shrUyate cha spaShyamityAshayavAnvAkyasheShAdityetatprakArAntareNa vyAchaShye- na para iti ||
"tasmAddhAnyatra paraH kiJNcha nAsa' ityato vAkyasheShAtprakR^ityAdInAM pralaye svAtantAdyabhAvo.avagamyata ityarthaH | iha hi tasmAdbrahmaNo.anyatprakR^ityAdikaM paraH paraM svAtantAdidharmopetaM nAseti tatsadbhAvAbhyupagamena paratvaM niShiddhayate | anyathA parashabdavaiyarthyAditi | 
syAdetat.h | kAraNAntarasadbhAvamabhyupagamya tasyeshvarAdhInatAM vadatA siddhAntinedaM vaktavyam.h | kimIshvaraH prakR^ityAdibhirvinA.api kadAchitsR^iShyayAdikaM karotyuta taireveti niyamaH | Adye teShAM kathaM kAraNatvamaniyatatvAt.h | anyathA rAsabhasyApi gha(pa)TakAraNatApatteH | dvitIye tu kathaM tatparityAgena kadA.apyakurvANasyeshvarasya svAtantyam.h | kathaM cha niyamenApekShaNIyAnAM teShAM pAratantyam.h | evaM pR^ikR^ityaiva mahAntaM mahataivAhaN^kAramityAdiniyamaM kadAchidapahAya sR^ijati utAnena niyamenaiva | Adye tvaniyatatvenAkAraNatvaprasaN^gaH | dvitIye punarIshvarAdeH svAtantAdyanupapattiH | tathA prakR^ityAdikamupAdAnIkR^itya kAlAdikaM nimittIkR^itya sR^ijatIti niyame vyatyAse choktadoShAnuShaN^gaH | ato yuktibAdhitatvAdasyArthasya kAraNAntaranirapekSha eva bhagavantsR^iShyayAdikaM karAtItyeva jyAyaH | evaJNcha nirargalamaishvaryamasya samarthitaM syAt.h | nacha pramANabAdhaH | adbhayaH sambhUtaH pR^ithivyai rasAchchetyAderanIshvarakartR^ikAvAntarasR^iShyiviShayatvasyoktatvAt.h | tama AsIdityAdau tamaHprabhR^itInAM pralaye sattvashravaNe.apIshvarakartR^ikAyAM sR^iShyau kAraNatvAshravaNAdityAshaN^kApanodanArthaM sUtram.h- || OM yukteH shabdAntarAchcha OM || iti | asyAyamarthaH | noktayuktivirodhena bhagavataH kAraNAntaravidhuratvamurarIkartavyam.h | kAraNAntarasadbhAvAbhyupagame.api prakR^ityAdeH kAraNatvasyeshvarAdisvAtantAdikasya cha yukteH | nachaivaM tarhi vinigamane kAraNAbhAva iti vAchyam.h | adbhayaH sambhUto hiraNyagarbha ityAdishabdAntarAt.h | pUrvodAhR^itashabdavilakShaNashabdaH shabdAntaram.h | tenedamuktaM bhavati | yadyapi prAgudAhR^itAH shabdAH kathaJNchidanyathA netu shakyante | tathA.apyayaM na tathA | atreshvarakartR^ikAyAmeva sR^iShyau kAraNAntarasadbhAvashravaNAt.h | nahi hiraNyagarbhasR^iShyiranIshvarakartR^ikA | tasyaiva prathamajatvAditi |
anyathA, kAraNairvinA, kartuM shakto.api hariH kAraNAntarANyupAdAyaiva kariShyAmIti svechChAniyamataH kAraNairevedaM jagatsadA sR^ijati | evamanyathA, prakR^ityA.ahaN^kAramahaN^kAreNa mahAntamiti evam.h tathA prakR^itiM nimittIkR^itya kAlAdikaM chopAdAnIkR^itya kartuM shakto.apyetenaivedametadupAdAnIkR^ityaivedaM srakShyAmIti svechChAniyamato niyataiH klR^iptaireva, tathA niyataiH svaniyatasattAshaktyAdimadbhireva kAraNairidaM jagatsadA karotIti yojanA | 
idamuktaM bhavati | yaduktamIshvarasya kAraNopAdAnAdiniyamo.asti na veti | tatrAstIti brUmaH | tathAcha prakR^ityAdInAM kAraNatvaM yuktam.h | sacha niyamo na kulAlAderiva tAnyapahAya vyatyasya vA akaraNe shaktyabhAvanibandhanaH | yena tasya svAtantyam.h teShAM cha pAratantyaM na syAt.h | kinnAma svechChAyatta eva | tataH svAtantAdikamapi yuktam.h | nacha tAni svAdhInasattAshaktyAdimanti, yenaishvayarM nirargalaM na syAt.h | kintu bhagavatyeva tadIyaM sattAdikamAyatate | tatastatsAchivyamatishayenaishvaryasya dyotakameva | yathoktam.h "sAdhanAnAM sAdhanatvaM yadA.a.atmAdhInamiShyate | tadA sAdhanasampattiraishvaryadyotikA bhavet.h' iti |
nanu shaktasyApIshvarasya tanniyamAnusaraNechChA kuta iti chet.h | kiM kAraNaM pR^ichChasyuta j~nApakam.h | Adye svabhAvo.ayamiti brUmaH (vadAmaH) | dvitIye tu shrutiprasiddheriti | tadidamuktaM hishabdena | shrutiM chodAhariShyati |
anena shabdAntarAchcheti sUtraM prakArAntareNa vyAkhyAtaM j~nAtavyam.h | shabdAntaraM cha shabdavisheSho, vivakShitArthapratipAdakaH shabda iti yAvat.h | "paTavachcha',"yathA prANAdiH' iti sUtre, bhAShya eva vyakte |
anye punaranyathaitAni sUtrANi varNayanti | tathAhi | 
bhAve chopalabdheH | mR^idAdeH kAraNasya bhAva eva ghaTAdeH kAryasyopalabdheshchAnanyatvaM kAraNAtkAyarsya | nahi yadyato bhinnaM tattadbhAva evopalabhyate | na hyashvo goto.anyo gorbhAva evopalabhyate | kiJNcha, bhAve tilAdau kAraNe, tailAdyupalabhyate | kArye cha bhAve kuNDalAdau suvarNAdikam.h | atashcha tadabhedasiddhiH | 
satvAchchAvarasya | avarakAlInasya kAyarsya prAgutpatteH "sadeva somyedamagra AsIt.h' iti sattvAvadhArarAchchAnanyatvaM kAraNAtkAryasya |
asadvayapadeshAnneti chenna dharmAntareNa vAkyasheShAt.h | "asadevedamagra AsIt.h',"asadvA idamagra AsIt.h' iti prAgutpatteH kAryasyAsattvavyapadeshAnneti chenna | bhavedetadyadi kAryasvarUpAbhiprAyeNAyaM vyapadeshaH syAtkintu vyaktatvalakShaNadharmAntarAbhiprAyeNa | kutaH | vAkyasheShAt.h | asadevedamagra AsIt.h ityasachChabdenopakrame nirdiShyaM punastatsadAsIditi vAkyasheShe nirdishati | asadvetyatrApi "tadAtmAnaM svayamakuruta' iti | tena j~nAyate nAsatkAryaM dharmAntareNaivAsattvavyapadesha iti |
yukteH shabdAntarAchcha | yukteshcha kAyarsya prAgutpatteH sattvaM kAraNAdananyatvaM cha gamyate | shabdAntarAchcha | yuktistAvadasadakAraNAdityAdikA sAN^khayoktA | vR^ittivikalpAnupapattyAdikA cha saugatoktA | shabdAntaraM chAsadvayapadeshAdanyaH "sadeva somyedamagra AsIt.h' ityAdisadvayapadeshaH | 
paTavachcha | saMveShyitaprasAritapaTanyAyenedaM kAraNAtkAryasyAnanyatvaM prAgutpatteH sattvaM cha pratipattavyam.h | 
atra sUtrAkSharANAmArjavAnArjavAdichintA shiShyaireva kriyatAmityAshayavAn.h yaduktaM kAraNAtkAryasyAnanyatvaM tattAvannirAkariShyan.h kimanena prabandhena nimittakAraNAnanyatvaM kAryasyopapAditam.h, utopAdAnakAraNAnanyatvamiti vikalpaM chetasi nidhAyAdyaM nirAkaroti- nityabheda iti ||
nityashabdo niyamArthaH | bheda eveti | kAryasyeti sheShaH | hIti sarvapramANaprasiddhiM sUchayati | tathAcha sarvamidaM bAdhitaviShayamiti | na dvitIyaH | prakR^itAnupayogAt.h | 
viyadAdiprapaJNchasya brahmAnanyatvamupapAdayituM khalvasyopanyAsaH | tadyadi nAma upAdAnAnanyatvaM kAryasya tadA kimAyAtaM prakR^ite | nahi brahma prapaJNchopAdAnamityetaduktaprAyamiti manvAno dUShaNAntaramAha- upAdAneneti || 
hItyanuvartyate | upAdAnena kAryasya dvayaM bhedAbhedau pramitau | tato.asminnapi pakShe bAdhitaviShayatvamiti | 
kathaM kAryaM kAraNena bhinnAbhinnaM pramitamityata Aha- asaditi ||
yat.h ghaTAdikaM mR^idAdikAraNAtmatayA prAgutpatterastIti pramitaM pareNAN^gIkR^itaM cha tadeva pR^ithubudhnodarAkArAdinA kAryarUpera prAgutpatterasat.h hi yasmAttasmAdupAdAnena bhinnAbhinnamiti nishchIyate | 
etaduktaM bhavati | paro hi ghaTAdeH kAryasya prAgutpatteH sattvamabhyupagachChati | tatkiM pR^ithagevota mR^idAdikAraNAtmatayeti vaktavyam.h | nAdyaH | anabhyupagamAt.h | anupalabdheshcha | dvitIye tu kAryasyopAdAnAbhedastAvadaN^gIkR^itaH | na chAtyantAbhedaH | ghaTAdeH kAryAkAreNa prAgutpatterasattvAt.h | yadA hi ghaTAdikaM mR^idAdinA.atyantAbhinnaM syAt.h | tadA prAgutpatterghaTAdirUpeNa satsyAt.h | mR^idAdestadA sattvAt.h | na chaivam.h | tena jAnImo ghaTAdikaM mR^idAdinA bhinnAbhinnamiti | atyantAsatkAryavAdinaM prati bhedAbhedasamarthanaM virodhaparihArashchottaratra vidhAsyata iti | 
yachcha kAryasya prAgutpatteH sattvamuktaM tadapi nopapannamityAha- asaditi ||
yat.h ghaTAdikaM prAgutpatterastItyAvayoH sammatam.h | tadeva tadA.asachcha yasmAttasmAtsadeveti satkAryavAdo.anupapanna eva | tasyaiva tadaiva tatraiva sattvamasattvaM cha viruddhamiti chenna | rUpabhedena avirodhAt.h ityAshayenoktaM kAraNAtmatayA kAryarUpeNeti | nanvevaM sati kiJNchitsadeva kiJNchit.h asadeva sadasattu na kimapi syAt.h | na syAt.h | tayorapi rUpayoratyantabhedAbhAvAditi |
syAdetaduktaM yadyasattvaM prAgutpatteH kAryasya syAttadeva kutaH | tathA chAtyantAbhinnaM kAryamupAdAnenetyato vipakShe bAdhakapradarshanena kAryasya prAgutpatterasattvamupAdAnAdbhedaM chopapAdayati- anavastheti ||
anyathA kAryasya prAgutpatterAtyantike sattve kAraNenAtyantAbhede chAN^gIkR^ite sarvatrotpattinAshayoranavasthA avyavasthA syAt.h | yathA hi | paTastantvAtmakaH prAgapi sanneva | tathA tantavo.api svakAraNAtmakAH santa evetyanena krameNa sarvasya mUlakAraNAtmakatvenAtyantikaM sattvaM syAt.h | nacha mUlakAraNamutpadyate vinashyati cheti paTAdInAmapyutpattivinAshau na syAtAm.h | tathAcha paTAdaya utpattivinAshavanta AtmAdayastadrahitA iti lokavedaprasiddhotpavinAshavyavasthA na syAditi | upalakShaNaM chaitat.h | paTAdInAmutpattivinAshAbhAve tatkArakavyApAravaikalyaM syAdityapi draShyavyam.h | 
yadvotpattinAshashabdAbhyAM sattvamasattvaM chopalakShyate | tatashchAyamarthaH | yadi paTastantvAtmakaH prAgutpatterapi sanneva tadA(tadA).apyupalabhyeta tantuvat.h | yadi chAnupalabhyamAno.api sannabhyupeyate, tadA sarvatrotpattinAshayossadasattvayoranavasthA syAt.h | upalabhyamAnaM ghaTAdikamastyanupalabhyamAnaM kharaviShANAdikaM nAstIti sarvajanasammatA vyavasthA na syAt.h | 
athavotpattivinAshashabdAbhyAM tadupapAdanasyopalakShaNam.h | tathA chaivaM yojanA AstAM tAvadanyat.h | satkAryavAde sarvatra shiShyaM prativAdinaM vA prati utpattinAshayornAsadutpadyate na sadvinashyatItyevaMrUpopapAdanasyApyanavasthA.avasthAnAbhAvaH syAt.h | tathAhi | idamupapAdanaM kimarthamiti vAchyam.h | shiShyAdervidyotpattaye.avidyAnAshAya vAda jalpAdau tu khyAtyAdyutpAdAyeti chet.h | tadvidyAdikaM sachchennotpAdyam.h, sattvAdAtmavat.h | asachchennotpAdayituM shakyam.h, anyathA satkAryavAdabhaN^gaprasaN^gAt.h | evamavidyA satI chenna vinAshyA | anyathA.apasiddhAntApatteH | asatI chet.h(nitarAM) na tAram.h | nityanivR^ittatvAt.h | tataH sarvathA pratipAdanAsambhava eveti |
yadi votpattivinAshayoriti viruddhadharmopalakShaNam.h | tathAhi | yadi kAryamupAdAnAtmakameva sadeva cha prAgutpatteH syAt.h | tadotpattivinAshAdidharmANAmanavasthA syAt.h | tantavaH prAgeva santo nedAnImutpadyante | paTastUtpadyate | tantuShvavinaShyeShveva paTo vinashyati | tantavo bahavaH paTastvekaH | evamAkArAbhidhAnabuddhikAryabhedo.api draShyavyaH | saiShA vyavasthA na syAditi |
nanvetatsakalamapi paTavachcha, yathA prANAdiriti vyaktyavyaktyavaShyambhena parihR^itam.h | tathAhi | vyaktyapekShayotpattiH paTAdInAmavyaktyapekShayA cha vinAsho yujyate | vyaktyavyaktyarthameva cha kArakANyupayujyante | vyaktyavyaktibhyAmevopalabdhyanupalabdhI bhavataH | ata eva pratipAdanaM saN^gachChate | vyaktAvyaktarUpeNaiva viruddhadharmA vyavatiShThante | yathA hi saMveShyitaH paTo na sphuTaM paTa iti pratIyate | na prAvriyate na shItamapanudati | na bahudeshavyApI bhavati | prasAritastu sphuTapratItyAdimAn.h | na chaitAvatA bhedaH | nApi prasAritaH prAgasat.h | yathA cha prANAyAmena niruddhaH shArIro vAyurjIvanamAtraM karoti notkShepaNAdi | nirodhApagame tvAsAditavyaktistadapi karoti | na tAvanmAtreNa bhidyate | prAgasanvA | tathaivaitadapi vyaktyavyaktibhyAM samaJNjasamiti |
atra brUmaH | keyaM paTasya prAgutpatterUrdhvaM cha vinAshAdavyaktirmadhye cha vyaktiH | anupalabdhiravyaktirupalabdhirvyaktiriti chettatrAha- anavastheti ||
yadyupalabdhyanupalabdhI evotpattivinAshau | tadA sarvatrotpattinAshayoranavasthA syAt.h | yadyadopalabdhaM tattadaivotpannam.h anupalabdhaM cha vinaShyamiti syAditi yAvat.h | kiJNcha prAgutpattessattve paTasya kasmAnnopalabdhiH kathaM chordhvamupalabdhiriti prashnasya upalabdhyanupalabdhi(anupalabdhyupalabdhi)bhyAmeveti parihAraM vadandevAnAMpriyaH shlAghanIyapraj~naH syAt.h | api cha prAgUrdhvaM cha tantUpalabdhau kathaM tanmAtrasya sataH paTasyAnupalabdhiH | anyathA tantUnAmapi sA syAt.h | 
atha paTadharmAveva vyaktyavyaktI | tadA tAvapi tantUnAM vidyete na vA | na chenna kAryakAraNayeratyantAbhedaH | vidyete chettatrAha- anavastheti || utpattinAshavyavahArahetUvyaktyavyaktI yadi tantuShvapi vidyete tadA sarvatrotpattinAshayoranavasthA syAt.h | tantavo notpannA na naShyAH | kintu paTa evetyutpattivinAshavyavasthA na syAditi |
kiJNcheyamabhivyaktirutpattyAdivyavahArakAraNatayopAdIyate | sA kiM chakrachIvarAdibhiH prAgasatyevotpadyate mudgarAbhighAtAdinA cha nashyati, uta prAgapi satyevAvinAshinI cha | evamavyaktirapi kiM prAgasatI mudgarAbhighAtAdinotpadyate | kiMvA prAgapi satI | ubhayatrAdyau dUShayati- anavastheti || vyaktyavyaktyorutpattinAshavattve sarvatrotpattinAshayoranavasthA vyavasthAbhAvaH syAt.h | na kiJNchidasadutpadyate na kiJNchitsadvinashyatIti siddhAntavirodhaH(hAniH) syAdityarthaH | dvitIyau dUShayati- anavastheti || vyaktyavyaktyoH sadA sattve sarvatrotpattinAshayoranavasthA.avyavasthitiH syAt.h | tathAhi | etAvantaM kAlamanutpanno ghaTa idAnImutpanna iti tAvanna syAt.h | utpattivyavahArahetorabhivyakteH prAgapi sattvAt.h | tathA mudgarAbhighAtAdyuttarakAlamapi ghaTasattvavyavahAraH syAt.h | taddhetorabhivyakteravinaShyatvAt.h | tathedAnImeva naShyo ghaTa ityapi na syAt.h | 
vinAshavyavahArakAraNAnabhivyakteH prAgapi sattvAditi | kArakavyApAravaiphalyatAdavasthyaM sphuTameva | 
athaitaddoShaparihArAya vyaktyavyaktyorapi vyaktyavyaktI svIkriyete, tadA tayorapyuktavikalpadoShAnuShaN^gaH syAt.h | atha tatrApi vyaktyavyaktyantarAN^gIkArastadA.anavasthA syAdityAha- anavastheti || utpattinAshayoriti viShayasaptamI | santvanantA vyaktayo.avyaktayashcha | mUlakShayAbhAvAnnAnavasthA doSha ityata Aha- anavastheti || anyathA.anavachChinnavyaktyavyaktiparamparAN^gIkAre savartra ghaTAdAvutpattinAshayoranavasthA.anavaklR^iptiH syAt.h | uttarottaravyaktyavyaktisiddhau hi pUrvapUrvavyaktyavyaktInAmutpattinAshavyavahAranidAnatvam.h | tataH prayojanaparikShayahetutvAdanavasthA dUShaNameva |
nanvidaM bhavatAmapi samAnam.h | prAgasataH sattAsamavAyo hi janiriShyate | sattAsamavAyAha cha sadA santAviti prAgvinAshottaramapi janiH syAt.h | vinAshashcha na syAdityata Aha- anavastheti || iyaM sarvatrotpattivinAshayoranavasthA.avyavasthitiH anyathA samavAyasya janitvAN^gIkR^itAveva hi syAt.h | nAsmanmate | prakArAntareNa janervakShyamANatvAditi |
nanu janiH kiM prAk.h satI uta kArakavyApArajanyA | Adye prAgukta eva doShaH | dvitIye janerjanirapi tathetyanavasthA | evaM vinAshopItyata Aha- anavastheti || sarvatrotpattinAshayoriyamuktAnavasthA | anyathA ghaTajaneranyA janerjanirityaN^gIkAra eva syAt.h | na tvevamaN^gIkriyate | api tarhi ghaTajanmaiva janmano janmeti | yathA.a.ahuH "yathA janerjanirnAnyA tasyA vastujanirjaniH' iti | ghaTo jAyate ghaTajanma jAyata ityanayorekArthataiva hi laukikaparIkShakasammatA | nacha vyaktyavyaktyorapyevamaN^gIkartumuchitam.h | janmavinAshAvupalabdhyanupalabdhI vA vihAya vyaktyavyaktyorevAprAmANikatvAditi | 
nanu yadyasadutpadyeta sachcha vinashyeta tadA sarvatrotpattinAshayoranavasthaiva syAt.h | evaM sati hi (khara)shashaviShANamapyutpadyeta | AtmA cha nashyedityata Aha- anavastheti || anyathA kAraNashaktyanAdaraNe hImutpattivinAshayoranavasthA syAt.h | nachaivaM kintu yasyotpattikAraNamasti tadasadapyutpadyate | yasya cha vinAshakAraNaM vidyate tatsadapi niruddhayate | nacha kharaviShANajanmanyAtmavinAshe vA kAraNamastIti tayorjananavinAshAbhAvaH | kAraNasvabhAvAnanugame tu satkAryavAdino.apyatiprasaN^ga eveti |
athavA syAdiyamanavasthA yadyatyantAsadevotpadyate sanmAtraM vinashyatIti brUmaH | sadasadevotpadyata iti choktaM vinAshakAraNavadeva cha vinashyatIti | yachchoktaM bhAve chopalabdheriti sUtrArthatvena, tadvayApyavyApakabhAvenaivopapannaM nAtyantAbhedasAdhakam.h | atha kAraNoparaktabuddhiH sAmAnAdhikaraNyabuddhirvA.atrAbhimateti matam.h | sA.api abhedamAtreNa charitArthA nAtyantAbhedasAdhanAyAlam.h | kiJNchaitadyukteshchetyanenaiva shakyasaN^grahaM na punarabhidhAtavyam.h | athAnena pratyakShamupanyasyate tadapi nAtyantAbhedasAdhakam.h | ata eva bhAvAchchopalabdheriti sUtravipariNAmo.api nirastaH | sattvAchchAvasyeti yuktishchedyukteshchetyetenaiva gatArthatA | shrutishchechChabdAntarAchchetyanena | asadvayapadeshAditi tu parichodanaivAsaN^gatA | paramArthato brahmakAraNatAparatvenApAtatastu shUnyasyAbhAvasya vA kAraNabhAvapratipAdakatApratibhAsena kAryAsattvasya shrutAvapratIteH | yukterityuktayuktiM tUttaratrApAkariShyAmaH | shabdAntaraM tvAchAryeNaivAnyatrAnyathaiva vyAkhyAtam.h | paTe prANAdau cha nAtyantAnupasaJNjAtavisheShatvamityanudAharaNamevetyalaM prapaJNchena | 
yaduktaM shakto.api hIti yachcha nityabheda itrata tadubhayaM shrutyA.api sAdhayati- shakto.apIti ||
akartuM shakto.api karoti | anyathA vinA kAraNaistadvayatyAsena cha kartuM shakto.api niyataiH kAraNaiH karotIchChayeti yojyam.h | svasmAnnimittakAraNAdbhinnam.h | upAdAnakAraNenAbhinnaM bhinnaM cha | saMsAriNo hi viShyigR^ihItA iveshvarapreritA aniShyamapi dhArakaprayatnenAkR^itvA na sthAtumIshate | nacha bhagavAMstathetyakartuM shakto.apItyuktam.h | asheShataH prAgidAnIM chokto na tu sannihita evetyarthaH | 
|| iti shrImannyAyasudhAyAM ArambhaNAdhikaraNam.h ||
|| atha shrImannyAyasudhAyAM itaravyapadeshAdhikaraNam.h ||
|| OM itaravyapadeshAddhitAkaraNAdidoShaprasaktiH OM || asminnadhikaraNe jIvakartR^itvapakShaH shrutiprApto vistarAnnirAkriyata iti bhAShyam.h | atra vaktavyam.h | kimatra jIvasya sarvathA kartR^itvaM nirAkriyate | uteshvarAdhInaM tadaN^gIkR^itya svAtantyamAtram.h | nAdyaH | tathA sati kartA shAstrAtharvattvAdityAdivakShyamANavirodhApatteH | svataHkartR^itvAnupapattirityAdivisheShaNavaiyarthyaprasaN^gAchcha | na dvitIyaH | hitakaraNAdidoShaprasaktirityAdisUtrANAM svAtantyanirAkaraNaparatvena shakyayojanatve.api 
kR^itsnaprasaktirniravayavatvashabdakoSho vetyasya sUtrasyAshakyavyAkhyAnatvAt.h | idaM hi sUtraM sarvathA kartR^itvaM nirAkurvadupalabhyate | 
tathAhi | kartR^itvaM kR^itsnaikadeshAbhyAM vyAptam.h | tatra kR^itsnaprasaktAvanubhavavirodhaH | ekadeshAN^gIkAre cha "atha yaH sa jIvaH sa nityo niravayavaH' ityanaMshatvashrutivyAkopaH syAt.h H nahi sAmarthyAparaparyAyaM prayatnAdirUpaM kartR^itvamasmAkaM jIvAdbhinnam.h | yena tasya vichitratve.api jIvasya niraMshatvaM na vyAhanyeta | tato vyApakanivR^ittyA vyApyaM kartR^itvamapi vichitratve.api jIvasya niraMshatvaM na vyAhanyeta | tato vyApakanivR^ittyA vyApyaM kartR^itvamapi nivartata iti khalvasya(tra) tAtparyaM pratIyate | prasaN^gasya viparyaye paryavasAnAvashyambhAvAt.h | atha jIvakartR^itvasyeshvarAdhInatAnaN^gIkAra evaito prasaN^gAvuktau na kartR^itvamAtre | tathA cheshvarAdhInatvameva viparyayavaryavasAnalabhyaM bhaviShyatIti chenna | syAdapyevaM yadi jIvakartR^itvasyeshvarAdhInatvAN^gIkAreNemau prasaN^gau shakyasamAdhAnau syAtAm.h | nachaivaM parAdhInenApi khalvanena kR^itsnena vA kartavyamekadeshena vA | tR^itIyaprakArAbhAvAt.h | bhAve vA tenaivAparAdhInatve.api kartR^itvopapatteH | ato viparyayAparyavasAnAnnaivaM vyAkhyAnaM yuktamiti kartR^itvAbhAva eva tAtparyam.h | tathAcha vakShyamANavirodhaH | atha vastuto nAstyeva jIvasya kartR^itvam.h, AbhimAnikaM tu tadityavirodhaH | maivam.h | vihAropadeshAdityAdinA vAstavasyaiva tasya sAdhayiShyamANatvAt.h | 
ato durghaTametadadhikaraNamityato dvitIyapakShamaN^gIkR^itya prasaN^gau jIvakartR^itvasyeshvarAdhInatAnaN^gIkAraviShayau vyAkariShyannAdau tAvadIshvarAdhInatAN^gIkAre prasaN^ganivR^ittiprakAramAgamavAkyodAharaNena darshayati- anaMshasyApIti || 
kiJNchitsAmarthyayojanAM kAryAnurUpasAmarthyaprayogAt.h | svayambhuve svatantrAya | iti vachanAdavasito.ayamabhipretaH artha ityanuvartate | tatashchaitaduktaM bhavati | yadi jIvaH parameshvarAdhInatayA kartAN^gIkriyate | tadopapadyate eva tasya kartR^itvam.h | prasaN^gayoH samAdhAtuM shakyatvAt.h | anaMshatvasyAbhyupagamena hi na niravayavatvashabdakoShaH | anaMshasyApi parameshvarAchintyashaktivashena kAryAnurUpasAmarthyaprayogasambhavAnna kR^itsnaprasaktiriti | etachachAnupadaM sphuTIbhaviShyati | 
evamupodghAtaprakriyayA viparyayaparyavasAnopapattimuktvedAnIM vivakShitArthe sUtraM yojayati- yadIti || 
bhAgena kAryAnuguNAMshena | atra yadIshvarAdhInatayA kartA na syAditi vaktavye yadi bhAgenetyAdivachanaM prasaN^gasphuTIkaraNArtham.h | IshvarAdhInatvaprakAraprapaJNchanArthaM cha | sarvatra tR^iNAdAnAdAvapi kR^itsnayatnoM.ashitApi vA prasajyeta | tathA chAnubhavashrutivirodhaH | tasmAtparameshvarAdhIna eva jIvaH karteti sheShaH | na chopAdhikR^itAMshakalpanayA kartR^itvasyAvidyakatvena (vo)chopapattiH | anaMshasyApItyAdipramANasiddhopapannopapAdakaparityAgenAprAmANikAnupapannasvIkArasyAyuktatvAt.h | 
nanu jIvashaktyaivedaM ghaTatAm.h | maivam.h | tasyAghaTitaghaTakAchintyashaktyabhAvAt.h | bhAve vA hitAkaraNAdidoShaprasaktiH | na hyatrAdhikaraNe pUrvapakShiNA mahadAdisakalakAryakartR^itvaM jIvasyAshaN^kitam.h | kintu ghaTAdikartR^itvam.h | tattAvadanubhavasiddhatvAtkulAlAdInAM na tyaktuM shakyam.h | tatreshvarasyApi kartR^itvAN^gIkAre kalpAgauravaM syAdityato neshvarasya sarvakartR^itvamiti | tathAcha kathamachintyashaktiprasaktiH | 
nanu cha vyatireko gandhavaditi jIvAnAmanekarUpatAM sUtrakAra eva vakShyati | utkrAntigatyAgatInAmityaNutvaM cha | na chANoryugapadanekarUpatvaM vinA sAMshatayopapadyata iti sAMshatA.api tata eva siddhA | tatkathamatra niravayavatvashabdakopo vetyavAdIditi gUDhAbhisandherAshaN^kAmaviditAbhiprAyaiva pariharati- aMshino hItyAdinA || sAdharena shlokadvayena |
tatra bahusvarUpatAkhyetyanena vakShyamANamabhyupaiti | bahvityanekatvopalakShaNam.h | bahusvarUpatayA khyAyata iti bahusvarUpatAkhyA | tushabdaH shrutiniShedhyAyA vaishiShyayadyotakaH | teShu chetaneShu | hishabdaH pramANaprasiddhiM dyotayati | ata evAstyevetyavadhAraNam.h | 
tatashchAyamarthaH | astyeva vakShyamANAnekasvarUpatA.aNutvaM cha tadanyathAnupapattisiddhA sAMshatA cha | prAmANikasya tyaktumashakyatvAditi | tarhi kathamatra tadviruddhamuktamityata uktam.h- aMshina ityAdi || Adyo hishabdaH pramANaprasiddhau dvitIyo yasmAdityarthe | ye paTAdyA aMshinaH prasiddhAste parasparaM bhinnairevAMshairaMshinA cha vakShyamANaprakAreNa bhinnAbhinnaireva na tvatyantAbhinnaiH tantvAdibhiraMshairaMshina uchyante | chetanAstvevameva paTAdivaduktarUpairaMshairaMshino na bhavanti | kintu parasparamaMshinA chAtyantAbhinnaiH | yasmAdevamataH prasiddhAMshivaidharmyAdevAnekasvarUpeShu tata eva sAMsheShvapyeteShu chetaneShvanaMshina iti shrutirvartate | natu sarvathAMsharAhityAbhiprAyeNa | ato na virodha iti | 
nanu yadi bhedo nAsti kathaM tarhyanekatvaM tasyAbhedavyAptatvAt.h | kathaM chAMshitvam.h | matvarthasya bhedena vinA.anupapatterityata uktaM visheShAdeveti | bhedAbhAve.api kevalaM tatpratinidhervisheShAdevAnekasvarUpeShviti yojanA | yadvA "apyanekasvarUpeShu' ityanenaiva vakShyamANamaN^gIkR^ityAMshina ityAdinA virodhaH parihR^itaH | tatra bhedAbhAve kathamanekatvamaMshitvaM chetyAshaN^kAM 
visheShAdevetyAdipAdatrayeNa pariharati | kevalameva bhedena vinaiva teShu bahusvarUpatA tayA khyAyamAnA sAMshatA chAsti | katham.h | visheShAdeveti | kuta etatkalpyate | shrutidvayavirodhAdeveti hishabdenAha | atra jIvasyeti prakR^ite.api yachchetanA iti sAmAnyenoktam.h | tena chetanamAtre.apyayaM nyAya iti sUchayati | athavA yadyaMshino jIvAstarhi paTAdivadeva syurityasyAchetanatvamupAdhimanena dyotayati |
nanvevaM tarhi kiM jIvakartR^itvasyeshvarAdhInatvakalpanayA | tadabhAve.api svato bahurUpatvasadbhAvenaikadeshataH kriyopapattau kR^itsnaprasakterabhAvAt.h | vibhinnAMshAbhAvena niravayavatvashabdakopasyApi parihArAt.h | etadatiriktasya cheshvarakR^ityasyAdarshanAditi pUrvapakShiNA svAbhisandhAvudghATite satyAha- bahutveneti || 
yadi bhagavAnpuruShottama evaM na niyamakR^idbahutve.api bhedo jIveShu mA bhUditi vyavasthAyAH kartA na syAt.h | tadA bahutvena hetunA jIveShvapi bhinnatA bhavet.h | bahutvasaN^khayAyA bhinnatvenAvinAbhAvalakShaNAnniyamAt.h | yathoktam.h- tadanuvidhAnAtpR^ithaktvam.h' iti | 
etaduktaM bhavati | parameshvarAnapekShasya jIvasya kartR^itvAN^gIkAre na sarvathoktaprasaN^gadvayaparihAraH | tathAhi | kR^itsnaprasaktistAvatkathaM pariharaNIyA | bahutvasadbhAveneti chet.h | tarhi bahutvasya loke bhedAvinAbhUtatvena jIvasya bahutve bhinnatvamapyApadyeta | tathAcha durAtmA niravayavatvashabdakopo duShparihAraH | atha tatparihArArthaM bhedo neShyate | tadA vyApakanivR^ittyA vyApyanivR^itterAvashyakatvAdbahutvasaN^khayA.api tyAjyA syAt.h | tathA cha punaH saiva kR^ityA kR^itsnaprasaktirAskandeta | atha jaDeShveva yatra bahutvaM tatra bheda iti niyamo na chetaneShviti chet.h | kuta etat.h | tatha darshanAditi chenna | yataH kArakaprashno.ayaM na pramANaprashnaH | svabhAvo.ayaM padArthAnAmiti chenna | anIshvaravAdapAdaprasArikApAtAt.h | kiJNcha viruddhashcha svabhAvashcheti katham.h | nahi svayameva svena sadvitIya iti yuktam.h | pramitatvAnna virodha iti tu pratyuktam.h | chaitanyasAmarthyAdidaM ghaTata iti chet.h | dhUmavAnapi kashchinniragniko ghaTatAm.h | atha visheShashaktyedamupapadyata iti chet.h | ghaTe.apyupapadyatAm.h | nahi tatra visheSho nAsti | visheShavaichityAnneti chet.h | tadeva kutaH | tasmAdbhagavAneva svarUpasvabhAvavisheShANAM niyAmakashchaitanyamavachChedakaM vidhAya visheShaM nimittIkR^itya viruddhe apyabhedabahutve samAveshyAbhedena niravayavatvashabdakopamapAsya bahutvena kR^itsnaprasaktiM nyakkR^itya kAryAnurUpaM sAmarthyAvisheShaM (ni)yojayaJNjIvena kArayatItyaN^gIkartavyamiti | 
nanvetatsarvaM jIvasAmarthyAdinA.ashakyasampAdanaM kathaM bhagavAnapi sampAdayedityata Aha- tasya tviti || 
tadevamasya sUtrasyaivaM tAtparyavyAkhyAne na kashchidvirodha iti sthitam.h ||
|| iti shrImannyAyasudhAyAM itaravyapadeshAdhikaraNam.h ||  Vyasa-(19) 

|| atha shrImannyAyasudhAyAM shabdamUlatvAdhikaraNam.h ||
|| OM shrutestu shabdamUlatvAt.h OM || nanvIshvarasyApi kartR^itvaM na yujyate | jIvavatkR^itsnaprasakteH | nahi brahmANDapipIlikA(NDa)nimarANe samaM sAmarthyaM prayuJNjAnaH prekShAvAnbhavati | gatyantarAbhAvAnna doSha iti chenna | IshvaratvavyAghAtAt.h | athaitatparihArAtharmekadeshena pravR^ittiraN^gIkriyate tadA "neha nAnA' ityAdiniravayavatvashabdakAShaH syAt.h | sharIrendriyAdivikalatvAchcha na katarR^itvam.h | nahi kashchichCharIrAdivikalaH kartopalabdhaH | bhUmyAdyAdhAravidhuratvAchcha | evaM daurghaTye.api yadi kartR^itvamIshvarasya syAttadA jIvasyApi kinna syAt.h | visheShAdarshanAt.h | evaJNcha sarvakartR^itvaM dUranirastamityayaM pUrvapakSho.atrAdhikaraNe nirasyate | tasya tAtparyamAha- tasya tviti || 
tushabdo jIvAdvisheShaM dyotayati | chashabdo hetusamuchchaye | IshvarasyalaukikatvashruterAgamaikAgamyatvena yuktivirodhAnavakAshAt.h | vichitrashaktiH puruShaH',"sarvairyuktA shaktibhirdevatA sA' ityAdishrutibhirvichitrAsheShashaktitvAvagamAchcha | sarvaM bhinnAMsharahitasyApi kAryeShu kR^itsnaprasaktyabhAvaH, svarUpAMshabAhulye.api bhedAbhAvaH, aMshataH kAryakaraNe.api niravayavatvashabdakopAbhAvaH, dehAdirahitasyApi kartR^itvanirvAha ityAdi yujyata iti |
nanu durghaTamapi jIvakartR^itvamIshvarashaktyA ghaTata ityatItAdhikaraNe.abhihitam.h | tathAcha kathamatra pUrvapakShAvakAshaH | yo hi paratra pramitaM ghaTayitumIShye saH svasminna IShye ityasambhAvitam.h | uchyate | naiShorthaH sUtrakR^itA.atItAdhikaraNe.abhihitaH | kintvAgAminamarthaM manasi nidhAya jIvakartR^itvavAdanirAsa eva vihitaH | bhAShyakAreNa tu shiShyahitaiShiNA vakShyamANamapyarthamAkR^iShya pUrvottaravirodhaH parihR^ita iti |
pariNAmavAdino vivartavAdinashcha brahmaNo jagadupAdAnatvaM kR^itsnaprasaktirityanenAkShipya shrutestvityAdinA samAdhIyata iti vyAchakShate | tathAhi | na brahma jagadupAdAnam.h | yatastathAtve kR^itsnasyApi brahmaNaH kAyarAkAratAprasaktiH syAt.h | sthitau cha brahmAbhAve taddarshanopadeshAnarthakyAdi syAt.h | athaitaddoShaparijihIrShayA brahma ekadeshena pariNamate ekadeshena chAvatiShThata ityuchyate tadA "niShkalaM shAntam.h' ityAdiniravayavatvashabdakopaH syAditi | atrochyate | nAyaM doShaH | "tadAtmAnaM svayamakuruta' ityAdishruterbrahmaNo jagadupAdAnatvasya kR^itsnapariNAmAbhAvasya chAvagamAt.h | shabdamUlatvena yuktivirodhAnavakAshAchcha | api cha sarvashaktyupetA cha paradevatA shrUyate | "sarvakarmA sarvakAmaH' ityAdi | tato niravayavasyApi brahmaNaH kR^itsnaprasaktyabhAvenaiva jagadupAdAnatvamupapannamityAdi | tadetadvayAkhyAnamanupapannam.h | evaM sati eShAM sUtrANAmetadadhyAyAntarbhAvalakShaNasaN^gatyabhAvaprasaN^gAt.h | tatkathamityata Aha- virodha iti || 
tushabdo.avadhAraNe | parabrahmaNA nArAyaNasya sarvasmAchchetanAdachetanAchcha vaishiShyaye vailakShaNye paramotkR^iShyatve.atyantavyAvR^ittatve cha yo yuktyAdivirodhaH sa evAtra dvitIye.adhyAye nirasyate | sakalajagadupAdanatvena sarvAtmakatvaM tu na sarvavaishiShyayam.h | nApi tadupayuktam.h | pratyuta viruddhameva | tatkathaM tatra virodhaparihAro.atrAntarbhAvamAsAdayet.h | nanu jagadupAdAnatvAdeva sarvavaishiShyayaM brahmaNaH | nahi jagajjagadupAdAnamiti chet.h | tatkimupAdAnopAdeyayorbhedaM manyase | tathAcha tadananyatvamityuktavirodhaH | jagat.h brahmaNo na bhidyate brahma tu jagato bhidyata iti chet.h | na | uktottaratvAt.h | 
prAgbrahmopAdAnatvasyAnuktatvAtkR^itsnaprasaktyAdiparichodanaivAnavakAshA | pariNAmapratipAdakashruterabhAvena gaganAdiprapaJNchAtmakasya tadasambhavishabdamUlatvasarvashaktitvAdyasambhavena cha samAdhAnamapyayuktam.h | vivartavAde tu sarvathA.api naiShA shaN^kA.avakAshamashnute | shuktyAdikamiva rajatAdyAropasya brahmAvidyakaprapaJNchAropasyAdhiShThAnamiti spaShyamArambhaNAdhikaraNe.abhihitam.h | tatra kathaM kR^itsnaikadeshavichAraH | uktAnavaChAnAchChaN^geti chet.h | tarhyuktaM smareti vaktavyam.h | spaShyaM chAropitatvaM prapaJNchasya brahmaNyupapAdanIyam.h | shrutestvityAdestu kA saN^gatiH | 
kashchitparihArAdarshanasambhrAntachitta Aha | avidyAsaMvalitaM khalu brahma jagadupAdAnam.h | tatrAvidyopAdAnatvasyAyamAkShepaH parihArashcheti | tadatIva mandam.h | na hyavidyAyA upAdAnatvamapi vAstavam.h | tasyAvichAritaramaNIyatayaiva shaN^kA.aviShayatvAt.h | kiJNcha kR^itsnaprasaktiH sAvayavatvaM chAvidyAyAM kiM kariShyati | samAdhAnaM tu sarvathA.apyasaN^gatameva | etena vikaraNatvAdityAkShepaparihArAvapyasaN^gatau veditavyau | nahi bhramAdhiShThAnatA sharIrAdikamapekShate | IshvaraviShayaM taditi chenna | tasya kiraNatvAbhAvenAkShepAnudayAdityAdikaM svayameva shiShyairavagantavyamityasaN^gatirevAchAryeNoktA | 
syAdevamasaN^gatiryadi brahmaNaH sarvavaishiShyaye virodhaparihAro.adhyAhAyarH syAttadeva kuta ityata Aha- tadanya iti |
tasmAtsarvavaishiShyayaviShayAdanye virodhAstatra tatraivAdhikaraNeShu gatAH parihR^itAH | etaduktaM bhavati | avirodhalakShaNo dvitIyo.adhyAya iti tAvatsammatam.h | na chAnukte.arthe virodhaparihAraH saN^gata iti prathamAdhyAyArthe.avirodho dvitIyasyArthaH | prathame chAdisUtreNa shAstrIyaviShayaprayojanapradarshanamukhena brahmajij~nAsAyAH katarvyatvamuktam.h | tachchaturadhyAyIparisamApyaM naikatra paryavasyati | tataH kiM tadbrahma | kiM jIvo.atha jaDamiti svarUpajij~nAsAyAM shR^iN^gagrAhikayA pradarshayitumashakyatvAt.h | dvitIyasUtre sarvato vailakShaNyapradarshanena sarvotkR^iShyaM sarvasmAdvayAvR^ittaM cheti pratipAditam.h | sajAtIyavijAtIyAsambhAvitadharmasya lakShaNatvAt.h | sakaletaravyAvR^itteshcha tatprayojanatvAt.h | tR^itIyasUtre shAstraM tatra pramANamabhidhAya tasyottaraprabandhena sAmAnyato visheShatashcha sakalajIvajaDavyAvR^ittavastuviShayatA samarthitA | evaMcha dvaye virodhaH pariharaNIyA bhavanti | dvitIyasUtrasiddhasarvavaishiShyayaviShayAH shAstrasamanvayaviShayAshcha | tatra dvitIyA vikArashabdAdityAdinA tatra tatraivAdhikaraNe parihR^itA iti parisheShAtsarvavaishiShyayaviShayavirodhaparihAra eva dvitIyArtha iti j~nAyata iti |
nanu cha shrutInAM parasparavirodho.api dvitIye.adhyAye na viyadashruterityAdinA parihR^itaH | tatkathamuchyate brahmaNaH sarvavaishiShyaye virodho dvitIye nirasyata iti tatrAha- sR^iShyIti ||
jIvarUpAbhidhAyinAM vAkyAnAm.h | upalakShaNametat.h | prANAdiviShayANAM chetyapi draShyavyam.h | sR^iShyayAdivisheShaNamupapattisUchanArtham.h | tushabdo visheShArthaH | yo dvitIyAdhyAyagocharo vAkyAnAmanyonyavirodhaH so.api pArameshvarasarvavaishiShyayavirodhaparihAra eva | kintu prathamadvitIyapAdayoH sAkShattR^itIyachaturthayostu vyavadhAneneti visheShaH | tathAhi | shrutInAM parasparavirodhaparihAraH kiM tatprAmANyanirNayamAtraphalaH kiM vA prameyanirNayaphalaH | nAdyaH | mImAMsAyA nyAyashAstratvApatteH | kiJNchaivaM sati viyadAdisR^iShyayAdiviShayavAkyavirodhaparihAra eva kasmAtkriyate | uditahomAdivAkyAnAmapi nyAyadarshana ivopAdAnopapatteH | 
AkAshavAyvAdikramashchAtra nAtyantamupayujyate | dvitIye.api kiM sR^iShyayAdikameva prameyamuta tadaN^gibhUtamanyat.h | nAdyaH | tasya svarUpato.aprayojanatvAt.h | prathamApratipAdyatvam.h | anyathA punaruditahomAdivAkyavirodhaparihAro.api kAryaH syAt.h | sR^iShyayAdiviShayaniShkarSho.api nirhetukaH | ato dvitIya eva parishiShyate | nachAnyadasti sR^iShyayAdiprameyasyAN^gi prathamoktaM dvitIyasUtrAbhihitAdbrahmaNaH sarvavaishiShyayAt.h | ato yuktamuktam.h | tadevaM paroktasUtrArthasya dvitIyAdhyAyAntarbhAvalakShaNasaN^gatyabhAvAdvirodhAchchokta eva sUtrArtha iti siddham.h | 
atreshvarasya sharIrendriyAdikaraNarahitatvAtkartR^itvaM nopapadyate ityAkShepasamAdhAnArthaM sUtram.h || OM vikaraNatvAnneti chettaduktam.h OM || iti | etadanArambhaNIyam.h | punaruktatvAt.h | shrutestu shabdamUlatvAt.h, tAtmani chaivaM vichitrAshcha hi, savaropetA cha taddarshanAditi sUtrairevAlaukikatvashabdaikasamadhigamyatvavichitrAnantashaktitvAdiyuktibhiH sarvasyApi daurghaTyasya parihR^itatvAt.h | yo hi sAkShAtkArakAdhiShThAnasya neShye sa sharIravyavadhAnamapekShate | yasya chAgantukaM j~nAnaM sa tadarthamindriyANi | yashcha gurusharIro nAvasthAtuM shaknoti sa kShityAdikamAdhAram.h | bhagavAMstu sarvashaktiH sarvaj~naH kimarthapapekShateti | nacha kAchidabhyadhikA shaN^kA.asti yena punarArambhaH syAdityata Aha- mAneti ||
yatA ata eva prANa ityAdau mAnaikye.api meyavisheShaNa na punaruktidoShastathA.atra meyaikye.api mAnavisheShaNa na punaruktidoShaH | etaduktaM bhavati | kimuktArthoktimAtraM doShaH | kiM voktAnatiriktoktiH | nAdyaH | uktaparihArAtideshokterapi doShatvAnuShaN^gAt.h | dvitIyastu prakR^ite na siddhaH | prameyaikye.api pramANabhedasya sattvAt.h | iha hi chidAnandAdyAtmakadivyamaN^galavigrahavato mahApuruShasya prAkR^itasharIrAdyabhAve.api sakalakAryakartR^itvamapANipAda ityAdishrutimAshrityoktamiti | yadvA mAnameyayorvisheSheNeti yojyam.h | tathA chAyamatharH | pUrvasUtraiH sAmAnyaviShayapramANAnyAshritya sAmAnyata eva sarvAnupapattiparihAro vihitaH | iha tu visheShaviShayeNaiva pramANena visheShAnupapattiparihAraH kriyata iti kathaM punaruktidoShAvakAsha iti | tathA.apyAkShepo nopapadyata iti chenna | visheShajij~nAsayopapatteriti |
|| iti shrImannyAyasudhAyAM shabdamUlatvAdhikaraNam.h || 
|| atha shrImannyAyasudhAyAM na prayojanAdhikaraNam.h ||
|| OM na prayojanavattvAt.h OM || OM lokavattu lIlAkaivalyam.h OM | yatprayojanArthaM sR^iShyayAdistadUnatvAdapUrNatetyAkShepaparihArAyedamadhikaraNamArabhyate | tadetadanupapannamityAbhAti | tathAhi | yadyatra kartR^itvena prayojanavattvaM prasAdhyApUrNatvasAdhanaM pUrvapakShiNo vivakShitaM syAttadA prathamasUtramayuktaM syAt.h | apUrNatAsAdhakaM prati prayojanavattvahetorasiddhatvAt.h | atha kartA chetprayojanavAnsyAt.h tathA chApUrNaH syAdityApAdanaM vivakShitam.h | tadA vyarthamevedaM sUtram.h | na chApUrNastato na prayojanavAniti pareNaivAN^gIkR^itatvAt.h | anyathA viparyayAparyavasAnAt.h | lokavattu lIlAkaivalyamiti dvitIyasUtraM tu pakShadvaye.apyayuktam.h | sAdhanApAdanadUShaNasyAnudbhAvanAditi | maivam.h | Ishvarasya sR^iShyayAdinA prayojanamasti na vA | Adye.apUrNatvaM prasajyeta | dvitIye tu kartR^itvAnupapattiH tasya prayojanavyAptatvAdityubhayathA.apIshvarasya jagatsR^iShyayAdikartR^itvAnupapattirityatra pUrvapakShiNo vivakShitam.h | tatra prathamasUtreNa prayojanAbhAvapakShaM sayuktikamupAdatte | tatroktadoShaparihArArthaM dvitIyaM sUtram.h | yadvA kartR^itvena prayojanasya tena chApUrNatvasya idaM sa dhanaM vivakShitamutApAdanamiti siddhAntI vikalpyAdyamAdyena nirAchaShye | na kartR^itvena prayojanavattvaM sAdhyam.h | kR^itakR^ityatvena prayojanAbhAvasyaiva nishchitatvAt.h | nachAsiddho hetuH | athaiSha eva parama Anando niraniShyo niravadya iti shruteH | prayojanavattvenApUrNatAnumAnaM tu garbhasrAveNaiva ga(li)tamiti | Adyasya dUShaNAntaraM vadandvitIyaM dvitIyena nirAkarotIti |
nanUktamatra lokavaditi sUtreNa sAdhanasyApAdanasya vA na kiJNchiddUShaNamudbhAvyata iti | maivam.h | bAdhAderudbhAvanAdityAshayavAndvitIyasUtrasya tAtparyamAha- sadeti || 
yathA loke jvalanapavanAdInAM tatheshasyApi sadA sR^iShyayAdau kevalaM prayojanena vinA svabhAvAdeva pravR^ittiH pramiteti sheShaH | tadaneneshvarasya pravR^ittyA prayojanasAdhanamanaikAntikaM bAdhitaviShayaM cha | prasaN^gastu vyaptivikalo viparyayAparyavasAyI chetyuktaM bhavati | atha manyeta | chetanapravR^ittiH na prayojanena vinA dR^iShyA | ato nAnaikAntyAdIti | tadapi nAsti | mattasya sukhodrekAdeva nR^ittagAnAdipravR^ittidarshanAt.h |
nanu cha prekShAvatpravR^ittirna prayojanoddeshena vinopalabdhA iyaM cha prekShAvatpravR^ittiH | ataH prayojanoddeshavatI syAditi sAdhyamApAdyaM chetyata Aha- aN^geti ||
kAshchidvayAkhyAnAdAvaN^gulichAlanAdikAH | uddeshavarjitAH prayojanoddeshavarjitAH | tathA IshasyApi pravR^ittiriti pUrveNAnvayaH | tathA.apyanaikAntyAdyanistAra iti bhAvaH | 
yaduktamIshvarasya pravR^ittiH prayojanena vinA svabhAvAdeva pramiteti | tatpramANamidAnImAha- devasyeti ||
"devasyaiSha svabhAvo.ayamAptakAmasya kA spR^ihA' iti shrutiraJNjasA sphuTamuktamarthamAha | devasyAyaM sR^iShyayAdiviShaya eShaH ichChA | tatpUrvikA pravR^ittiriti yAvat.h | svabhAva eva | na prayojanAya | kutaH AptakAmasya prayojanaspR^ihA.asambhavAdityarthaH | 
kechididaM sUtramanyathA vyAchakShate | yathA loke saptadvIpAM medinImadhitiShThataH sampUNarshauryavIryaparAkramasyApi mahArAjasya kevalalIlaikaprayojanAH kandukAdyArambhA dR^ishyante | tathaiva parasyApi brahmaNaH svasaN^kalpamAtrAvaklR^iptajagajjanmasthitidhvaMsAderlIlaiva prayojanamiti tadetannirAkaroti- krIDAmiti ||
"bhogArthaM sR^iShyirityanye krIDAtharmiti chApare' iti krIDAprayojanAM bhagavataH sR^iShyayAdipravR^ittiM vadataH pUrvapakShIkR^itya devasyaiva svabhAvo.ayamiti sayuktikaM prayojanaleshAbhAvaH shrutyA siddhAntitaH | ataH shrutiviruddhatvAdapavyAkhyAnamevaitat.h | 
sUtrAkSharA.ananuguNaM chaitadvayAkhyAnamityAha- itIti ||
yata evaM "krIDAM prayojanaM kR^itvA sR^iShyiH shrutivirodhinI' iti tasmAt.h shrutyanusAriNA prabhuNA svayaM sAkShAtsR^iShyaM kevalalIlaiva sR^iShyayAdipravR^ittirnirNItA lIlAkaivalyamiti | natu lIlArtheti tato.apyayuktamidaM vyAkhyAnamiti | yadvA pUrvavAkyokto hetuH, ayaM sAdhyanirdeshaH | yasmAllIlAM prayojanaM kR^itvA sR^iShyiH shrutivirodhinI tasmAdetatsUtre kevalalIlaiva sUtrakR^itA nirNItA vyAkhyAtA na punarlIlArtheti | 
kiJNcha kartR^itvena prayojanavattAM sAdhayannApAdayanvA praShyavyaH | kiM prayojanaM svasambandhi vivakShitam.h, uta parasambandhi, atha sAdhAraNam.h | Adye sAdhane.anaikAntyam.h | ApAdane vyAptyabhAvaH | viparyayaparyavasAne vyabhichAra eva | dR^ishyante hi kR^ipAlavaH svaprayojanamanuddishya paraprayojanArthameva pravartamAnAH | nachAdR^iShyArthamiti vAchyam.h | pashUnAM pashuprAyANAM chApatyapAlanAdau pravR^ittidarshanAt.h | nacha prayojanoddeshitA kR^ipAlutA cheti sambhavati | dvitIye.apyanaikAntyAdikameva | svaprayojanArthaM pravR^itterbahulamupalambhAt.h | bhagavato.api svaprayojanAbhAve.api paraprayojanoddeshitAN^gIkAreNa krameNa siddhasAdhaneShyApAdanAsiddhatvaprasaN^ga(N^gA)shcha | ata eva na tR^itIyo.api | ata eva (yena) kenachitkartR^itva(tve)visheShaNaM, pravR^ittisvabhAvatve sadA pravartetetyatiprasaJNjanaM cha pratyuktam.h | 
syAdetadevam.h | yadIshvarapravR^ittau paraprayojanoddeshaH syAnna chAsAvaN^gIkartumuchitaH | kA spR^ihA na kA.apIti shrutyA neti sUtrakAreNa cha sarvathA prayojanoddeshasya nivAritatvAdityata Aha- Atmeti ||
shrutiriti sUtrakR^ito.apyupalakShaNam.h | paraprayojanArthatAM tvaN^gIkuruta eveti sheShaH | 
kuta etadavagamyata ityata Aha- neti ||
yataH paraprayojanamaN^gIkR^ityAtmaprayojanArthatAmeva neti nyavArayat.h | ata eva hi prayojanavattvAditi tatra hetumAha- anyathA naitaM brUyAt.h | 
etaduktaM bhavati | yadi neti sautrIpratij~nA svaparaprayojanaviShayA syAt.h tadA prayojanavattvAditi heturanaikAntikaH syAt.h | svayaM vyApArasAdhyaprayojanavato.api paraprayojanoddeshena vyApAradarshanAt.h | svaprayojanamAtraviShayatve tu nAyaM doShaH | yo.avAptayatprayojanaH sa svArthaM na taduddishatIti vyApteranavadyatvAt.h | ataH prayojanavattvAditi hetuM brahmaNaH sUtrakR^idAtmaprayojanoddeshameva neti nivAritavAn.h | na paraprayojanoddeshamapi | tathAtve tadvayAptameva kamapi hetuM brUyAt.h | svaprayojananiShedhaM kurvANo visheShaniShedhasya sheShAbhyanuj~nAj~nApakatvAtparaprayojanaspR^ihAmabhyupaitIti (manujAnAtItyapi) j~nAyata iti | upalakShaNametat.h | shrutirapyAptakAmasyeti hetugarbhavisheShaNaM prayuJNjAnA.a.atmaprayojanaspR^ihAmevAkShipati paraprayojanaspR^ihAmabhyupaitIti j~nAyata ityapi draShyavyam.h | 
iha hi buddhireveshvarasyAvyAhatA kriyAshaktiH, tathaiva sarvasyopapattau kimichChAprayatnakalpanayA | yadvA prayatnaH kartatvam.h | tasyaivAkhyAtArthatayA nirNItatvAt.h | sa cha dvedhA buddhimapekShate | utpattyarthaM viShayaniyamArthaM cha | tatreshvaraprayatno yadyapi nityatvAnnotpattAvapekShate buddhim.h | tathA.api viShayaniyamArthaM tAmapekShata eva | na hi nirviShaya evAsau | vyarthatvaprasaN^gAt.h | nacha svabhAvata evArthapravaNaH | buddhitvaprasaN^gAt.h | buddhireva hi svabhAvato.arthapravaNA | ato j~nAnaprayatnAbhyAmeva sarvanirvAhAnneshvarasyechChA.asti | na chechChayA prayatnasya viShayaniyamaH | tasyA api svato viShayapravaNatAbhAvAt.h | tadarthaM buddhayaN^gIkAre tayaiva prayatnasya viShayaniyamopapatteH kimantargaDunechChayeti manvA(nyamA)nAH kechit.h, "kA spR^ihA' itrata 
shrutirneshvarasya prayojanechChAmAtraniShedhaparA, kintvichChAlakShaNaM guNameva niShedhatIti vyAchakShate | tannirAkaroti- ichChAmAtramiti ||
kA spR^iheti shrutyA neshvarasyechChAmAtraM niShi(She)dhyate | kutaH | ichChAvattvasya pramANataH siddhatvAt.h | tathAhi | "vibhUtiM prasavaM tvanye manyante sR^iShyichintakAH | svapnamAyAsarUpeti sR^iShyiranyairvikalpitA | kAlAtprasUtiM bhUtAnAM manyante kAlachintakAH' iti pariNAmavAdaM vivartavAdaM kAlAdinimittavAdaM chAnyamatatvenoktvechChAmAtramiti shrutyA svamatamuchyate | ye sR^iShyiviShaye vishiShyanishchayavantaste, prabhorichChAmAtrAdhInA sR^iShyirna brahmapariNAmo nacha tadvivarto nApi kAlAdinimitteti manyanta iti | anayA prabhorichChAmAtrAyattatAM sR^iShyermanyamAnAnAM vinishchitA iti prashaMsayA tasyechChAvattvamavagamyate | yadIshvarasyechChA na syAt.h tadA tadAyattatAM sR^iShyermanyamAnA vipayarstAH syuH | vishiShyanishchayavanta ityeShA prashaMsA.anupapannA syAt.h | nacha prashaMsAtvAdevArthAsiddhiH | pUrvottarapakShAvadhAraNaprasaN^ge prashaMsA.anupapannA syAt.h | nacha prashaMsAtvAdevArthAsiddhiH | pUrvottarapakShAvadhAraNaprasaN^ge prashaMsAyA api yAthArthyAvashyambhAvAt.h | anyathA pariNAmAdivAdA api prashaMsyeran.h | 
na kevalaM shrutArthAnupapattyA | api tarhi "kAmastadagre samarvatAdhi',"so.akAmayata' ityAdibhyo bhagavataH kAmapratipAdakashrutibhyashchechChA.avagamyate | evashabdaH shrutInAmarthApattitaH prAbalyasUchakaH | ichChAkAmashabdayorj~nAnaprayatnopalakShaNatvasya sambhavAnnArthApattishrutibhyAmichChAsiddhiriti chenna | mukhye bAdhakAbhAvAt.h | 
mA vA saitsIdichChA.arthApattishrutibhyAM yuktitastAvatsetsyati | tathAhi | Ishvara ichChAvAn.h AtmatvAt.h yaj~nadattavat.h | nacha muktAdau vyabhichAraH | tatrApi tasyAH sAdhayiShyamANatvAt.h | j~nAnavattvAt.h, prayatnavattvAt.h, kartR^itvAdvA | Ishvaraj~nAnaM vechChAsamAnAshrayaM j~nAnatvAdasmadAdij~nAnavat.h | evaM tatprayatnamapi pakShIkR^itya prayoktavyam.h | yadvA kShityAdikamichChAvajjanyaM kAryatvAdghaTavat.h | nanvevaM duHkhAdikamapi sAdhayituM shakyamiti chettatkimatiprasaN^gabhIruNA kShityAderbuddhimatkAraNakatvAnumAnamapi tyakShyate | duHkhAdisAdhane bAdho.asti na buddhisAdhana iti chet.h | samaM prakR^ite.api | 
nanvIshvarasya ichChAbhAve bAdhakAbhAvAdaprayojakatvamanumAnAnAmiti | maivam.h | mahAtAtparyayukteshcha | yadIshvarasya ichChA na syAt.h tadA tasminsarvavedAnAM (vedAntAnAM) mahAtAtparyaM na syAditi bAdhakasadbhAvAt.h | ichChA niShprayojaneti chet.h | syAdevaM yadi prayojanamanurudhya kalpyate | anyataH siddhe.arthe kiM prayojanagaveShaNayA | 
kiJNchaivaM sati buddhirapi nAN^gIkaraNIyA | svarUpasAmarthyenaiveshvarasya kartR^itvopapatteH | lokavairUpyamiti chet.h | tatkimudAsInasya boddhuH kartR^itvamupalabdhaM loke, yenAnichChato.api tadIshvarasyAN^gIkriyate | prayatnavata eva vA kartR^itvaM bhaviShyati | tasya viShayaniyamArthaM buddhireShyavyeti chenna | buddhivatsvato viShayapravaNatopapatteH | tathAtve buddhito bhedo na syAditi chenna buddhitvAdinaiva tadupapatteH | anyathA paropAdhikaviShayapravaNatvayorichChAprayatnayorapi bhedA na syAt.h | viShayaniyamArthamiti cha ko.arthaH | kiM viShayavisheShasambaddhatayotpAdA(nA)rtham.h, utotpannasya sthitasyaiva vA tatsambandhArtham.h, atha tajj~nAnArtham.h | nAdyaH | anAditvAt.h | sAditve.api ka(kA)raNasApekSha(ta)yA buddherapi parato viShayapravaNatApatteH | na dvitIyaH | paurvAparyobhAvAt.h | nahi prayatnaH utpAdya sthitvA vA pashchAdviShayeNa sambaddhayate | na tR^itIyaH | svarUpagrAhakapramANenaikatadgrahaNAt.h | buddherapi parApekShAprasaN^gAchcheti |
mahAtAtparyayukteshcheti yaduktaM tadasat.h | yadIshvaro nechChAvAnsyAttadA shrutimahAtAtparyaviShayo na syAdityatra vyAptyabhAvAt.h | ichChArahitasyApi dharmAdestattachChAstramahAtAtparyaviShayatvadarshanAt.h | ApAdyasyAniShyatvAbhAvAchchetyata uktaM vivR^iNoti- mokShArthA iti ||
