yasmAtkAraNAtsarvA api shrutayo mokShArthAH mokShaprayojanAstasmAttadabhAve parameshvarasyechChA.abhAve tata eva mokShArthatA.abhAve shrutistatra mahAtAtparyarahitA syAt.h | tathAcha kathaM pramANatvaM gamiShyatIti yojanA | mokShArthatve kimIshvarasyechChayetyata uktam.h- sa cheti || sa cha mokShastasya Ishvarasya prasAdato yasmAttasmAttadabhAva iti sambandhaH | tathA.apIshvarasya prasAdena bhAvyaM kimichChayetyata prasAdata ityetadvayAkhyAtam.h- ichChAnimittaka iti || Ishvaraj~nAnAdeva mokShasiddheH kiM tatprasAdenetyata uktam.h- loketi || vimato bandhamokShaH prabhuprasAdasAdhyo mokShatvAt.h shR^iN^khalAmokShavat.h ityAdilokadR^iShyavyAptyupetAnumAnAnusArataH ityatharH | na kevalamanumAnAtkintvAgamAdapItyuktaM- unninIShatIti || "eSha hyeSha sAdhukarma kArayati taM, yamebhyo lokebhya unninIShate' iti vAkyAchcha | atra karmetyupalakShaNam.h | unninIShate UrdhvaM netumichChati | yadvA prasAdashabdenechChochyate ityata idaM vAkyaM (vAkyametat.h) j~nApakam.h | lokadR^iShyA(dR^iShya)nusArata ityetadapyasyaiva arthasya j~nApakamuktam.h | shrutaya ityupakramya 
shrutirityekavachanaM kaimutyArtham.h | ekamapi vAkyaM na tatra mahAtAtparyavatsyAt.h | kimuta sarvAH shrutaya iti | 
etaduktaM bhavati | shAstraM hi sAdhyasAdhanabhAvavadviShayaprayojanavattayA vyAptam.h | tatra shrutInAM mokSha eva prayojanam.h | "teShAM duHkhaprahANAya shrutireShA pravartate' iti vachanAt.h | mokShAdanyatrAtyantikaduHkhaprahANAyogAt.h | svargAdiprayojanaM bhavadapyavAntarameva na pradhAnam.h | viShayastu parameshvara eva | "sarve vedA yatpadamAmananti' ityAdivachanAt.h | dharmAdikaM tvavAntarapratipAdyam.h | abhipretaprayojanasAdhanaM cha viShayatAmashnute | nacha dharmAdikaM mokShasAdhanam.h | "puNyachito lokaH kShIyate' iti shruteH | ato bhagavatyeva mokShasAdhanatvAtsavarshrutInAM mahAtAtparyam.h | nachAvyApR^itAtsAdhanAtphalasiddhiH | vyApArashcha prasAda eva | natu shrutijanitaM tajj~nAna sAkShAtkAro vA | "yasya prasAdAt.h' ityAdivAkyAduktAnumAnAchcha | j~nAnaM tu prasAdasAdhanamiti na sambandhAnupapattiH | prasAdo nAmechChAvisheShaH | tathA sati "unninIShate' "tadichChayA yato hyasya bandhamokShau pratiShThitau' ityAdishrutibhiH "yasya prasAdAt.h' iti shruteraikArthyalAbhAt.h | prasanno.asmIti pratItau paropachikIrShAyA eva sphuraNAt.h | tathAcha yadIshvaro nechChAvAMstadA na prasidedghaTavat.h | sAmAnyAbhAve visheShAbhAvaniyamAt.h | prasAdarahitashcha na mokShasAdhanaM syAt.h | yadyatra vivakShitAvAntaravyApArarahitaM na tattatra sAdhanamiti vyApteH | mokShaM pratyasAdhanaM cha na mokShashAstramahAtAtparyaviShayaH syAt.h | tathAcha mokShaprayojanatA shrutInAM hIyeta | nacha viShayAntaraM prayojanAntaraM chAstIti viShayaprayojanashUnyatvAdaprAmANyamevApadyeta | nacha tadapauruSheyatAyA.anAshaN^kitadoShasya vAkyasyopapadyate | ato.avashyamuktena krameNechChAvattvaM bhagavato.aN^gIkaraNIyamiti |
nanu viShayAbhAve syAdaprAmANyam.h | phalAbhAve tu kathamaprAmANyApAdanam.h | nahi phalavattvaM prAmANyam.h | kintu yAthArthyamevetyuktam.h | nApi prAmANyasya vyApakam.h | tR^iNAdidarshanasya prayojanAbhAve.api prAmANyAbhyupagamAdityata Aha- yAthArthyameveti ||
yadyapi yAthArthyameva mAnatvaM na phalavattvam.h | nApi tena vyAptam.h | tathA.api vAkyaM prayojakameva mAnatvametIti yuktamApAdanam.h | etaduktaM bhavati | prAmANyamAtrasya prayojanavattvena vyAptyabhAve.api tadvisheShasya vAkyaprAmANyasyAstyeva | padAnAmiShyasAdhana eva gR^ihItasaN^gatikatvAt.h | padasaN^gatigrahaNasavyapekShasyaiva vAkyasya bodhakatvAt.h | phalasya viShayavisheShe vAkyaprAmANyanirNayahetutvAchcha | ato vyApakAbhAve vyApyavAkyaprAmANyAbhAvApAdanamupapannameveti |
nanu cha mahAtAtparyagocharasya viShayasya paramaprayojanasya chAbhAve.apyavAntaraviShayeNa dharmAdinA.apradhAnaprayojanena cha svargAdinA viShayaprayojanavatI shrutiH pramANaM bhaviShyati ityata Aha- tatrApIti ||
vAkye.api nirdhAraNe saptamI | prayojanavattve.apIti vA | yat.h vAkyaM sampUrNaprayojanaM mahAprayojanam.h | upalakShaNaM chaitat.h | pradhAnaviShayaM chetyapi draShyavyam.h | yaditi shravaNAttaditi labhyate | sampUrNaprayojanamiti chAvartanIyam.h | mAnatvametItyanuvartanIyam.h | tathA chAyamarthaH | nAvAntaraviShayaprayojanAbhyAM vAkyasya prAmANyaM sambhavati | kinnAma yadvAkyaM yanma(hA)hatprayojanamuddishya yaM pradhAnaM viShayaM pratipAdayituM pravR^ittaM tattAbhyAM(eva) prayojanaviShaTAbhyAmupetaM prAmANyamashnute | tadabhAve.avAntaraprayojanAderapyasiddheH | siddhau vA vA tasyaiva prAdhAnyaprApteH | vedavAkyaM cha mokShoddeshena mahAtatparyopetamityuktam.h | tattayoreva viShayaprayojanayorupapattau pramANaM syAnnAnyatheti | 
|| iti shrImannyAyasudhAyAM na prayojanAdhikaraNam.h ||   Vyasa-(20)

|| atha shrImannyAyasudhAyAM vaiShamyanairghR^iNyAdhikaraNam.h ||
|| OM vaiShamyanairghR^iNye na sApekShatvAttathA hi darshayati OM || prANinAM vividhAndehendriya(yAdi)viShayAMstatphalaM cha sukhaduHkhalakShaNamutpAdayannIshvaraH kiM tadIyaM dharmAdharmarUpaM karmApekShate na vA | Adye tasya svAtantyaprachyutiH | dvitIye nirnimittaM kAMshchitsukhayanviShamaH syAt.h | kAMshchid.hduHkhayannirghR^iNaH syAt.h | ityubhayathA na tasya sarvakartR^itvamityeSha(va) pUrvapakSho.atrAdhikaraNe nirAkriyate | tatra tAvadAdyena sUtreNa kamarAdisApekShasya kartR^itvamabhyupetya vaiShamyanairghaNye parihR^ite | apekShaNIyaM karmAdi IshvarAyattaM na vA | neti pakShe sarvakAraNatvahAniH | Adye nirnimittaM viShamANAM karmaNAM kArayituvaraiShamyanairghR^iNye syAtAmityAkShipya karmAdInAmanAditA(tvA)bhyupagamena samAdhAnamuktaM "na karmAvibhAgAditi chennAnAditvAt.h' iti sUtreNa | evaM tarhi karmAdisApekShasya svAtantyaM na syAdityAshaN^kayoktamupapadyate cheti | karmAdyapekShasyApi tasya svAtantyamupapadyate | karmAdisattAderapi tadadhInatvasyArambhaNAdhikaraNe samarthitatvAt.h | nahi svAdhInasattAdikamapekShamANasya svAtantyaprachyutiryukteti | evaM(cha) tarhi tadapekShA nAmAnapekShaiva | tathAcha 
punarvaiShamyAdyApattirityAshaN^kayoktam.h- upalabhyate cheti || upalabhyate hI(che)shvarasyedR^ishaM vaiShamyaM nirghR^iNatvaM cha pramANaiH | ato nedamaniShyamiti |
tadidamayuktam.h | vaiShamyanairghR^iNye hi vastuto dUShaNe na vA | Adye kathamantato.apyaN^gIkriyete | dvitIye prathamamevAN^gIkArye | kiM sApekShatApakShaM kakShIkR^itya tatra dUShaNaparihArakleshena | tathAcha bakabandha(ka)rItirityato.abhiprAyamAha- vaiShamyamiti |
dvividhaM khalvidaM vaiShamyaM nirghR^iNatvaM cha | ekaM (dha)karmAdyanapekShatAprayuktam.h | aparaM tu sApekShatve.api karmAdisattAderapIshvarAdhInatvaprayuktam.h | tatrAdyaM vedAprAmANyakAraNatvena dUShaNatvAt.h neshvarasyAN^gIkartumuchitam.h | vedo hi dharmaM sukhasAdhanamadharmaM cha duHkhasAdhanamAha | tatra yadIshvaro dharmAdharmAnapekShya viShamo nirghR^iNashcha syAt.h tadA vedoditaM dharmAdharmayoH sukhaduHkhasAdhanatvamasatsyAt.h | tathAcha tasya kathaM prAmANyaM syAt.h | ataH sUtrakAreNa karmAdisApekShatApakShamurarIkR^itya tatparihR^itam.h | ato.anyattu dvitIyaM vaiShamyaM nairghR^iNyaM cha na vaiShamyAdinAmakaM dUShaNarUpaM na bhavatIti yAvat.h | tathAhi vaiShamyAdikaM tAvanna svarUpeNa doShaH kintu doShahetutayA | na chedaM vedAprAmANyakAraNam.h | karmAdisApekShatvAN^gIkArAt.h | nApi jIvAnAmiveshvarasya pratyavAyahetuH | tadabhAvAt.h | ato.adUShaNatvAdaN^gIkR^itaM sUtrakR^iteti na kashchiddoShaH | tathAcha bhAgyam.h | "nacha punarvaiShamyAdyApAtena doShaH' iti | 
|| iti shrImannyAyasudhAyAM vaiShamyanairghR^iNyAdhikaraNam.h ||
|| atha shrImannyAyasudhAyAM sarvadharmopapattyadhikaraNam.h ||
|| OM sarvadhamaropapatteshcha OM || sarve chetanA apUrNaguNA doShiNashcha dR^iShyAstad.hdR^iShyAntena chetanatvAdIshvarasyApi samAsavyAsAbhyAmaparipUNarguNatvaM doShitvaM cha syAditi pUrvapakSho.atrAdhikaraNe nirasyate | tadidamaspaShyaM bhAShye | chashabdasamuchchitAyAH shruterevodAhR^itatvAt.h | yukteravyutpAdanAt.h | tataH spaShyaM yadadhInA iti ||
chApishabdAvanyonyasamuchchaye | evashabdasya yadadhInA evetyanvayaH | hishabdaH sarvasya bhagavadadhInatAyAM shrutyAdiprasiddhiM dyotayati | kathamityAkShepe | dvedhA hi vastu na prApyate | tatra svAtantAbhAvAdvA prepsA.abhAvAdvA | dvedhA cha na hIyate | svAtantAbhAvAdvA jihAsA.abhAvAdvA | asti tAvadIshvarasya sarvatra svAtantyam.h | asti cha mayA sarvadA.a.anandAdiguNavatA duHkhAdidoShavarjitena bhAvyamitIchChA, prekShAvattvAt.h | ataH kathaM tasyAnandAdiguNapUrNatvaM duHkhAdisarvadoShadUratvaM na bhavati | 
atraite prayogAH | IshvaraH sakalaguNapUrNaH sarvadoShadUrashcha, svatantratvAt.h | vyatirekeNa yaj~nadattavat.h | Ishvaro vipratipannaguNavAn.h, tatra prepsAvattve sati svatantratvAt.h | yo yatra prepsAvatve sati svatantraH sa tadvAn.h yathA sampratipannaH | Ishvaro na vimatadoShavAn.h, tajjihAsutve sati svatantratvAt.h | yo yatra jihAsAvattve sati svatantraH sa tadabhAvavAn.h | yathA sammata iti |
tat.h evamuktaprakAreNa sarveShAM dharmANAM guNAnAM doShAbhAvAnAM cha sambandhinyAstatpratipAdikayA upapatteH tAdR^ishaiH sarvaguNapUrtyAderupapAdakaiH | hishabdasteShAM "guNAH shrutAH' ityAdInAM prasiddhAnAM sUchayati |
tadanena svapakShe pramANamabhidadhataiva parakIyayuktInAM kAlAtyayApadiShyatvaM svAtantAbhAvopAdhiduShyatvaM choktaM bhavatIti |
|| iti shrImatpUrNapramatibhagavatpAdasukR^iteranuvyAkhyAnasya praguNajayatIrthAkhyayatinA | kR^itAyAM TIkAyAM viShamapadavAkyAtharvivR^itau dvitIyAdhyAyasya prathamacharaNaH paryavasitaH ||
|| iti shrImannyAyasudhAyAM dvitIyAdhyAyasya prathamacharaNaH samAptaH ||
|| atha shrImannyAyasudhAyAM rachanAnupapattyadhikaraNam.h ||
sakalajagajjanmAdikAraNe sakalaguNaparipUrNe samastAvadyagandhavidhure pare brahmaNi viShNau samastashrutisamanvayo yaH prathamAdhyAye.abhihitaH, tasya sAN^khayAdisamayavirodhenAnyathAtvasha(N^kAyAM tannirAkaraNArthamayaM)N^kAM nivArayituM dvitIyapAda Arabhyate | 
nanvanArambhaNIya evAyaM pAdaH | tathAhi sAN^khayAdimatAni kiM smR^ititvenoktArthamanyathamantIti shaN^kayate, kiMvA yuktyupetatayA, athavA shrutyupetatayA, yadvA pratyakShopetatayA | nAdyaH, pratismR^itiparAhatatvenAptinishchAyakAbhAvena cha teShAmapasmR^ititvasya prathamapAde samarthitatvAt.h | ata eva na chaturthaH | na dvitIyaH | uktArthaviruddhAnAM sakalayuktInAmAbhAsatvasya tatraiva vyutpAditatvAt.h | prabalayuktivirodho.atra nirasyata iti chenna | prAbalyaM hi yuktInAM shrutyAdipramANamUlatvena, tatsaMvAditvena (vA), bahutvena vA syAt.h | sarvathA.api nAdhikAshaN^kAvakAshaH | shrutyAdisaMvAdinInAM tanmUlAnAM bahvInAM cha yuktInAM tatraiva 
nirAkR^itatvAt.h | kAshchideva tatra nirastA na samastA iti chenna | sUtrANAmupalakShaNArthatvAt.h | anyathA yuktyAbhAsAnAmanantatvena aparyavasAnaM syAt.h | pAdabhedashchaivaM sati na syAt.h | na tR^itIyaH, samastashrutInAM brahmaNi samanvayasyoktatvAt.h | 
atra kashchidAha | svapakShasAdanaparapakShapratikShepAbhyAmeva nirNayo bhavati | tatra prathamAdhyAye svapakShe pramANamuktam.h | tasya yuktivirodho dvitIyasya AdyapAdena nirastaH | evaM svapakShasthApane jAte parapakShapratikShepAtharmayaM vAda Arabhyata iti | tadayuktam.h | parapakShapratikShepo hi tadIyasAdhananirAsAdanyo nAsti | sAdhanAni cha smR^ityAdInyeva | nirastAni cha samastAni tAni prathamapAda iti kimasya kR^ityam.h | kiJNchaivaM sati virodhaparihAro.adhyAyArtho na syAditi | 
apara Aha | uktArthe smR^itinyAyavirodho nAstIti sthApite.apyasti brahmaNi samanvayAbhAvashaN^kA | katham.h | yadyapyanumAnaM brahmaNo jagatkAraNatvamapabAdhituM nAlam.h, tathA.api kAraNAntaraM jagato.avagamayitumalam.h | tatashcha vastuvikalpAnupapatteranyataraparigrahe hetvabhAvAt.h brahmaiva jagatkAraNamiti na nishchetuM shakyate, pratyuta sarvaj~napraNetR^ikatvenAnumAnasyopabR^iMhitatvAt.h pradhAnAdyeva jagatkAraNaM na brahmeti buddhiH syAt.h | ato na kevalaM brahmaNo jagatkAraNatvamapabAdhitumanumAnaM notsahate | kintu kAraNAntaramapyavagamayituM nAlamiti pradarshanArthaM dvitIyaH pAda Arabhyata iti | etadapyuktam.h | tathAhi | kimanenoktaM syAt.h | yadi, prAk.h svAbhimatArthe yuktivirodhaparihAreNa svapakShasthapAnA vihitA, idAnIM parapakShapratikShepo vidhIyata iti | tadoktamevottaram.h | atha yuktivirodhaparihAra eva pAdadvayArthaH, kintu svapakShavirodhiyuktinirAkaraNaM prathame, dvitIye tu parapakShasAdhakayuktinirAkaraNamiti, tanna | nyAyasAmyena tAsAmapi shakyanirAkaraNatvAt.h (sArvaj~naM) sarvaj~natvaM cha praNetR^INAM prAgeva nirastam.h | 
ato nAyaM pAda ArambhaNIya ityata Aha- smR^itIti || 
shrutayo gurA upasarjanA(ni) yAsAM tAstathoktAH | chaturvidhA virodhipratItayaH | anvayaM prati na viruddhayante iti shrutisamanvayasiddhamarthaM nAnyathayituM shaknuvantItyarthaH | abhiyoga AgrahaH | dR^ishyate prameyamebhiriti darshanAni sAN^khayAdishAstrANi | etaduktaM bhavati | yadyapi paramatasAdhakAnAmasmanmatabAdhakAnAM cha smR^ityAdInAmAbhAsatvavyutpAdanena spaparapakShasAdhanopAlambhau kR^itAveveti paramArthaH | tathA.apyukte.arthe punaH puruShasya AshaN^kA bhavatyeva, kimetadevamanyathA veti | kasmAt.h | abhiyogato (darshanAnAM) matAnAM pravR^ittatvAt.h tadupalambhAditi | 
nanu cha shrutayastAvadapauruSheyatayA.anAshaN^kitadoShAH bahula(prabala)yuktibhishchAnusaMhitArthA nirastasamastapratipakShAshcha | tatkathaM tatsamanvayasiddhe.arthe.abhiyogapravR^ittadarshanopalambhamAtreNAnyathAtvashaN^kA syAt.h | atiprasaN^gAt.h | nanvata evoktaM manda iti | maivam.h | prAptimanAlochya shaN^kamAnasyAvichikitsitashaN^kasya shAstre.anadhikArAdityato.abhiyogato darshanAnAM pravR^ittatvAdityuktashaN^kAkAraNaM vivR^iNoti- anAdIti ||
kapilakaNAdAdInAM praNetR^INAM smaraNAtkathamanAditvamityata uktam.h- pravAhata iti || kapilAdayo hi pUrvaiH praNItAnyeva shAstrANi kAlabalAdutsannAni sva(tapaH)prabhAvAdinA.avagamya prabandhAntararachanayA pravartayanti | evaM pUrve.api pUrvatarairityevaM pravAhato.anAditvAdadoShaH | tathaiva cha smaraNAnIti | iti hetorAshaN^kita iti pUrveNa sambandhaH |
idamuktaM bhavati | karaNadoShabAdhakapratyayavashAdeva hyaprAmANyaM kalpanIyam.h | anyathA atiprasaN^gAt.h | tatra yatA shrutInAmanAditvAtkaraNadoShAbhAvaH, tathA samayAnAmapi | svarUpAnAditvaM pravAhAnAditvamiti tu vaiShamyamAtram.h | puruShadoShasaJNchArAbhAvasyobhayatrApi sAmyAt.h | yathA chAnuchChedenAnuvR^itteH shrutInAM bAdhakAbhAvaH, evaM samayAnAmapi | yadi karaNadoShabAdakapratyayopetAH syuH tadonmattavAkyavadidaMprathamAH samuchChedavantashcha syuH | nachaivam.h | ataH kathamaprAmANyamashnuvate | yathA cha shrutayo balavadyuktyanusaMhitArthA evaM samayA api | nacha tAsAmAbhAsatvamuktamiti vAchyam.h | sarveShAM tadanuvartinAmasmAbhiranavagatatvena tatparihArasambhAvanAt.h | evamevApratipakShatvaM shrutInAmiva samayAnAM sambhAvitam.h | kathamanyathA sUtrakR^idekadhurINAH shauddhodaniprabhR^itayo.abhiyogatastAnpravartayeyuH, kathaM cha prekShAvanto.aneke.abhiyogenaivopAdadIran.h | tadevaM shrutitulya(samAna)yogakShematAM samayAnAM manyamAnasya syAdevoktArthe sandeha iti |
nanvevaM sati parasparaviruddhAnAmanekeShAM prAmANyaM tAvanna sambhavati, vastuvikalpApatteH | tathAchAvashyAshrayaNIye kasyachideva prAmANye anAdikAlato.anuvR^ittatvAdeH anyeShvanyathAsiddhau sarvathA kalpanIyAyAm.h "itareShAM chAnupalabdheH' ityuktadishA sAN^khayAdisamayAnAm.h aprAmANyaM kalpayituM shakyata eva, tatkathaM shrutisamanvayasiddhe.arthe punaH shaN^keti | uchyate | yo hi 
itareShAM chAnupalabdheH' iti saN^kShepeNoditaM nyAyaM para(pari)kalpiteShu prameyavisheSheShUtprekShituM kShamate, taM pratyevametat.h | yastvevaM na kShamaH sa yAvadayaM saN^kShepo na prapaJNchyate tAvadanyaparityAgenaikagrahaNasyAnIshAnaH shaN^ketaiva | nachaivaM shAstre nAdhikriyeta | saN^grahaprapaJNchochChedaprasaN^gAt.h | tadidamuktaM manda AshaN^kata iti | kimato yadyevamityata Aha- ata iti ||
bhrAntipadaM vipralambhasyApyupalakShaNam.h | pR^ithak.h vistareNa | sphuTam.h subodham.h | tattatsamayoktArthAnAmaprAmANikatvaM pramANaviruddhatvaM (cha) prAk.h saN^kShepeNAsphuTaM choktaM, atra vistareNa sphuTaM darshayaMsteShAM bhrAntyAdimUlatvaM j~nApayatItyarthaH | etena pUrvapAdenAsya pAdasya prapaJNchyaprapaJNchakabhAvalakShaNA saN^gatiH, prapaJNchane prayojanaM choktaM bhavati | tadidamuktamitareShAmityAdi bhAShyeNa | 
nanvetadashakyaM taiH svaprameyANAM dR^iDhatarkAgamasAdhitatvAt.h parakIyatarkAdenirastatvAdityata Aha- tarkairiti || 
tarkashabdaH sopaska(skA)rAnumAnArthaH | dR^iDhatamaiH parakIyatarkabAdhakaiH tadabAdhyaiH (cha) vAkyaishcha dR^iDhatarai(mai)riti sambaddhayate | pUrveNa sambandhaH (anvayaH) | vedAdivAkyAnAM prAmANyamanabhyupagachChantaM prati kathaM tadupanyAsa ityata uktam.h- AgamavAdinAmiti || Agamasya vedAdeH prAmANyamabhyupagachChatAM puMsAM samayAnAmiti sambandhaH | yadvA svAgamaprAmANyavAdinAmityarthaH | tatashcha svAgamaprAmANyAbhyupagamanyAyena vedAderapi prAmANyaM tairaN^gIkAryamiti(rayitveti (ryeti) bhAvaH | athavA.a.agamasya vedAdeH prAmANyavAdinAM shiShyANAM vyapekShayeti sheShaH | tathAcha bauddhAdhikaraNAntena na virodhaH | yadyapyetadanupadameva pradarshayiShyate, tathA.api shrotR^imanaHsamAdhAnArthamuktamiti |
nanu chAnAdyanantakAle.anuchChedena pravartamAnAnAM samayAnAM na bhrAntyAdimUlatvamuchitam.h | nahi tathAvidhasyonmattavAkyAderanAdyantakAle.anuvR^ittirasti | tadayaM prayogaH | sAN^khayAdisamayAH pramANabhUtA, na bhrAntyAdi(nti)mUlA vA, sarvadA.anuvartamAnatvAt.h, mahAjanaparigR^ihItatvAt.h(vA), vedavaditi | tathAcha vakShyamANasya tarkAderbAdhitaviShayatvamiti | maivam.h | kimatra sarveShAmapi samayAnAM prAmANyAdikaM sAdhyamutaikasya | nAdyaH | parasparaviruddhAnAM prAmANyAdisAdhane vastuvikalpApattyA bAdhitaviShayatvAt.h | parasparapratikSheparUpatvena satpratipakShatvAchcha | na dvitIyaH | pakShIkR^itAdanyasya prAmANyAdyabhyupagame praguktadoShAnuShaN^gAt.h | anabhyupagame tatraiva vyabhichArAt.h | vedaprAmANyAdyabhyupagame pratij~nAtArthAnupapattiH | anabhyupagame cha dR^iShyAntadoShaH | bhavedevam.h | bhrAntyAdimUlatve samAne satyunmattavAkye.avidyamAnAM anAdyanantakAlAnuvR^ittireteShAmeva tarhi kinnimitteti suhR^idbhAvena pR^ichChantaM pratyAha- daurlabhyAditi || 
samayapravartakAnAM puMsAM durAgrahagR^ihItatvAdvartante samayAH sadA | naikyamunmattavAkye vidyate | nanvAgrahe.api kiM kAraNamityata uktam.h- vidveShAditi || 
tarhi dveShotpattyanantaraM pravartatAm.h | kathaM sadA ityata uktam.h- anishamiti || nanu puruShArthakAmAH kathaM (vi)dveShanimittAdAgrahAdanyAyaM pravartayantItyata uktam.h- anAdIti || 
vAsanAvashAttebhyastadeva rochayata iti bhAvaH | nanvanAdivAsanA.api balavatprayatnena kuto na nivartata ityata uktam.h- asurANAmiti || viparItaprayatnAdiprerakANAM buddhayAdyabhimAninAmiti sheShaH | 
nanu sAdhUnAM viduShAM nivAraNAtkuto na nivartanta ityata uktam.h- daurlabhyAditi || alpavedinAM bhramAdhiShThAnasvarUpamAtravidAM samayapravartakAnAm.h | tarhi rAjAdirloko nivArayiShyati ityata uktam.h- tAmasatvAditi || tata eva kupaNDitanimittamithyAj~nAnaprasaktishcha | na chaitAni kAraNAni svarUpato.apyanAdau vede sambhavantIti |
yadyapyetatpAdAnte vaktavyam.h, tathA.apyatra prasaN^gA(dA)gataM buddhisamAdhAnAyoktamiti |
yadyevaM tarhyeteShAM sudR^iDhanirUDhAnAM samayAnAM sarvathotsAdanasyAshakyatvAdvayartheyaM nirAkR^itirityata Aha- tathA.apIti ||
yadyapi kusumayA na sarvathA samuchChedyAH tathA.api | tamaH aj~nAnam.h | suyuktitvasya vivaraNaM sadA.a.agamAnugatA iti | pramANagR^ihItavyAptyAdiyuktAH tatsaMvAdayuktAshcha | iti ityevamartham.h | etaduktaM bhavati | na sAN^khayAdisamayasamuchChedArtho.ayaM prayatnaH, yenoktadoShaH syAt.h | kinnAma keShAJNchitpuMsAM taistaiH samayairAhitA(na)j~nAnasaMshayaviparyayAn.h AgamasahitAbhiryuktibhiH tattvaj~nAnamutpAdya apanetumiti | 
nanvetadapyayuktam.h | atinirUDhanibiDavAsanAnubaddhamanAdyaj~nAnam.h idAnImevotpannena tattvaj~nAnenApanIyata iti | kintu tattvaj~nAnaM paribhUya svavAsanAvashAtpunarudbhavati | pravartayati cha svochitaM kAryamityata uktam.h- shuddhabuddhInAmiti || yathArthaj~nAnasvabhAvAnAM mokShayogyAnAm.h | ayaM bhAvaH | vakShyate hi kechana chetanA mokShayogyAH kechana neti | tatra nAyogyAnAmaj~nAnamapanetumaya--rambhaH, 
kintu yogyAnAmeva | techa vishuddhavij~nAnasvabhAvAH | tathAcha pramANairidAnImevotpannamapIdaM manovR^ittitvaM tattvaj~nAnamantaraN^gabhUtena vishuddhasvarUpaj~nAnenopodbalitaM sat.h bahiraN^gamanAdyapi savAsanamaj~nAnaM samUlaghAtaM hanti | svabhAvasya sarvato.api balavattvAt.h | nachaivaM pramANavaiyarthyam.h | svabhAvasya bAhyaprayatnasachivasyaiva kAryakAritvAt.h | yathoktam.h "vinA yatnaM na haTho nApi karma' iti |
kiJNcha sarvato.api balIyAnIshvarAnugraha iti tAvatsuprasiddham.h | asti chAsau mokShayogyeShu (jIveShu) anAdita iti vakShyate | tathAcha tatsachivamidaM vR^ittij~nAnamaj~nAnamatinirUDhanibiDavAsanAnubaddhamanAdyapi samUlakAShaM kaShatyeva | ato na vyartheyaM samayAnAM nirAkriyeti bhAvenoktam.h- IshAnugrahayoginAmiti || nachaivaM tata evAvidyAnivR^ittirbhaviShyati kiM tattvaj~nAneneti vAchyam.h | IshvarAnugrahasya puruShaprayatnAnusAreNaiva phalajananasvAbhAvyAt.h | tathAchoktam.h "phalaprado vAsudevaH akhilasya' iti | akhilasya yogyatAkamarprayatnasAkalyasya na punarekaikasyetyarthaH | 
yadyevaM sAdhUnAM kusumayAhitamaj~nAnamapanetuM bhagavAnsamayAnAM nirAkR^itiM chakAra, tadeyaM brahmAdibhiranAdartavyA syAt.h | teShu kusumayairaj~nAnasyAnAhitatvena prayojanAbhAvAt.h | tathAcha "evaMvidhAni sUtrANi kR^itvA' ityAgamavirodha ityata Aha- nijeti ||
kusumayairanAhitAj~nAnAnAM brahmAdInAM buddhiM yuktInAM shANatvasiddhaye yuktishANena j~nAnAseH atinaishityasiddhayarthamiti yAvat.h | pUrveNaiva sambandhaH | kusumayA(hitA)j~nAnanirasanaprayojanAbhAve.api j~nAnavaishadyaprayojanasya vidyamAnatvAttairidamAdaraNIyamiti bhAvaH | 
|| OM rachanAnupapatteshcha nAnumAnam.h OM || tadevaM samarthitaH pAdArambhaH | tatrAdyAdhikaraNe nirIshvarasAN^khayAnAM nirAkriyate | nacha tatsvarUpAj~nAne dUShaNaM subodhaM bhavati ityataH tanmatasthitiM tAvaddarshayati- chetaneti ||
chetanamachetanaM cheti dvandvaikavadbhAvaH | AhuH saN^khayA iti sheShaH | nanu cha vidhAntarAsambhavAtprAmANikaistattvadvayameva vaktavyam.h, tatkiM teShAM vaiShamyamuchyata ityata uktam.h- nirIshvara iti || Ishvaramanabhyupagamya jIvajaDAtmakaM tattvadvayamevAhurityarthaH | 
nanu sAN^khayA manyante | saN^kShepatastattvasya chatasro vidhAH | kashchidarthaH prakR^itireva | kashchidartho vikR^itireva | kashchitprakR^itivikR^itiH | kashchitanubhayaH | tatra sattvarajastamasAM sAmyAvasthA pradhAnaM prakR^itireva | sA hi vishvasya kAryasya mUlam.h | na tvasyA mUlAntaramasti | mahadahaN^kAratanmAtrAH sapta prakR^itivikR^itayaH | prakR^itayo vikR^itayashcheti | tathAhi | mahattattvamahaN^kArasya prakR^itiH vikR^itishcha mUlaprakR^iteH | evamahaN^kAratattvaM tanmAtrANAmindriyANAM cha prakR^itiH vikR^itishcha mahataH | evaM paJNcha tanmAtrANi (tattvAni) bhUtAnAmAkAshAdInAM prakR^itayo, vikR^itayashcha ahaN^kArasyeti | paJNcha bhUtAnyekAdashendriyANIti ShoDashako gaNo vikR^itireva | yadyapi pR^ithivyAdInAmapi goghaTavR^ikShAdayo vikArAH, evaM tadvikArabhedAH payobIjAdayaH, teShAM dadhyaN^kurAdayaH | tathA.api gavAdayo bIjAdayo vA na pR^ithivyAdibhyastattvAntaram.h | sthUlatendriyagrAhyatAsAmyAt.h | tattvopAdAnatvaM cha prakR^ititvamiha vivakShitamiti | puruShastvanubhayo na prakR^itirnApi vikR^itiH | tadevaM vistarataH paJNchaviMshati tattvAni | yathoktam.h | "mUlaprakR^itivikR^itirmahadAdyAH prakR^itivikR^itayaH sapta | ShoDashakastu vikAro na pR^ikR^itirna vikR^itiH puruShaH' iti | tatkathamuchyate tattvadvayamevAhuriti, Aha- taditi ||
paJNcha cha te paJNchatashcha (paJNchapaJNchataH) teShAM bhAvaH paJNchapaJNchatvam.h | sa chAsau vibhAgashcha | tenopalakShitaM tiShThatIti paJNchapaJNchatvavibhAgastham.h | tat.h chetanamachetanaM cha tattvadvayameva, saN^kShepataH chaturvidham.h, vistarataH paJNchaviMshatiprabhedamAhurityato na virodhaH | 
nanu chetanamachetanaM chAsaN^khayAtaM pratyakShAdipramANairupalabhamAnAH kathamevamAhurityata Aha- taditi ||
tadityubhayaparAmarshaH | upAdhikroDIkAreNa paJNchaviMshatiprabhedaM vadanto.apyavAntarabhedena tattvadvayamasaN^khayAtamAhurityarthaH | 
chetanAnAmachetanAnAM cha pratyekamasaN^khayAtatvasAmye.api nobhayorbhinnatvena sAmyam.h | kiM tarhItyata Aha- bhinnamiti ||
chetanamiti sheShaH | chetanaM parasparato bhinnamAhuH | yathoktam.h | "jananamaraNakAraNAnAM pratiniyamAdayugapatpravR^itteshcha | puruShabahutvaM siddhaM traiguNyaviparyayAchcha' iti | anyat.h chetanAt.h, achetanaM bhidojkhitamAhuH | 
nanvIshvarAnabhyupagame kasyApi pravR^ittyanupapatteH, sargAdyasambhavAdIshvarAkhyaM tR^itIyaM tattvamaN^gIkaraNIyam.h | tatkathaM nAN^gIkurvantItyata Aha- achetanasyeti ||
nigadyate sAN^khayairiti sheShaH | tathAhi | chetanaH saN^ghAtaparArthatvAdihesiddhaH | achetanaM cha vyaktaM pratyakShAdisiddham.h avyaktaM cha kAraNakAryavibhAgAdihetusiddham.h | nachaivamananyathAsiddhamIshvare pramANamasti | achetanasyaiva pradhAnasya kartR^itvena sargAdyupapatteradR^iShyeshvarakalpanAnupapatteriti manyanta iti |
nanvachetanaM chetanAnadhiShThitaM kvapi na pravR^ittimadupalabdham.h | tataH pradhAnasyAdhiShThAtreshvareNa bhAvyamityata uktam.h- svAtanteNeti || chetanAdhiShThAnena vinetyarthaH | ta(ya)thoktam.h | "vatsavivR^iddhinimittaM kShIrasya yathA pravR^ittiraj~nasya | puruShasya vimokShanimittaM yathA pravR^ittiH pradhAnasya' iti |
anyadbhidojkhitamityuktam.h | tadasat.h | achetanAnAmapi chetanavatparasparato bhedasya pratyakShAdisiddhatvAdityata Aha- paraspareti || 
AlayaM pralayaparyantam.h | kAryANAM parasparavibhedashcha bhavediti nigadyate taiH | 
etaduktaM bhavati | kAryaM tAvatkAraNavyApArAtprAgapi sat.h | asadakaraNAt.h | asachchet.h kAraNavyApArAtpUrvaM nAsya sattvaM kartuM shakyam.h | nahi nIlaM shilpisahasreNApi pItaM shakyaM kartum.h | kiJNcha kAryeNa sambaddhaM kAraNaM kAryasya janakam.h, asambaddhaM vA | Adye tvasatA sambandhAnupapatteH sattvamaN^gIkAryam.h | na dvitIyaH | asambaddhatvAvisheSheNa sarvasmAtsarvasambhavApatteH | asambaddhatve.api kAraNaM tadevaM karoti yatra shaktamato nAtiprasaN^ga iti chet.h | sA shaktiH shakyaviShayA vA syAtsavartra vA | sarvatra chetsaivAvyavasthA | Adye tvasati shakye kathaM tadviShayA syAditi sadeva kAryam.h | nacha kAraNAdanyatkAryaM sadupalabhyata iti kAryakAraNayorabhedo.aN^gIkaraNIyaH | kiJNcha na paTastantubhyo bhidyate tantudharmatvAt.h, yadyato bhidyate tattasya dharmo na bhavati, yathA gaurashvasya | upAdAnopAdeyabhAvAchcha | yayorarthAntaratvaM na tayorupAdAnopAdeyabhAvo, yathA ghaTapaTayoH | saMyogAprAptyabhAvAchcha | arthAntaratve hi saMyogo dR^iShyo yathA kuNDabadarayoH | aprAptirvA yathA himavadvindhyayoH | nacheha saMyogAprAptI | tasmAnnArthAntatvam.h | gurutvAntarakAryasyAvanatibhedasyAgrahaNAchcha |
evaJNcha kAryANAM parasparaM bhede.api svasvakAraNairabhedAtkrameNa mahApralaye mUlakAraNabhAvaM gatAnAmabheda eva, ityenenAbhiprAyeNAnyadbhidojkhitamityuktamiti | tachchoktam.h "asadakaraNAdupAdAnagrahaNAtsarvasambhavAbhAvAt.h | shaktasya shakyakaraNAtkAraNAbhAvAchcha satkAryam.h' iti |
teShvapi matabhedamAha- bhoktR^itAmiti || 
sarve.api sAN^khayAH puruShasya kartR^itvaM nAnumanyante | kriyAvesho hi kartR^itvam.h | na chAtmanaH parispandalakShaNA kriyopapadyate | sarvagatatvAt.h | nApi prayatnalakShaNA | tasyAH antaHkaraNavR^ittitvAt.h | nacha vikriyAlakShaNA | nirvikAratvAt.h | yathoktam.h | "tasmAchcha viparyAsAtsiddhaM sAkShitvamasya puruShasya | kaivalyaM mAdhyasthyaM draShyR^itvamakartR^ibhAvashcha' iti | tatra kechichchetanasya bhoktR^itAmAhuH | yathA bhoktR^ibhAvAditi | apare tAmapi nAhuH | yathA "tasmAnna badhyate na muchyate nApi saMsarati kashchit.h | badhyate saMsarati muchyate cha nAnAshrayA prakR^itiH' iti | 
nanu kartR^itAbhAve bhoktR^itvamapi katham.h | tasyApi kriyAveshAtmakatvAdityata Aha- svarUpeti ||
sukhaduHkhAdyanubhavitR^itvaM hi bhoktR^itvamAhurityata uktam.h- svaprakAshAditi || sukhAdyanubhavitR^itvasya svapratItisiddhatvAdityarthaH | yathA.a.aha | bhoktR^itvayogyatA cha puruShasya chaitanyamiti | nachaivaM katarR^itvamapyaN^gIkartumuchitam.h | upapattibAdhitatvena kartR^itvapratIteradhyAsarUpatvAt.h | 
nanvevaM tarhi pratItisiddhaM bhoktR^itvamapare kathaM nAbhyupayantItyata Aha- prakR^iteshcheti ||
bhogaM bhogavyavahArakAraNam.h | ayaM teShAmAshayaH | bhoktR^itvaM hi na puruShasya svabhAvaH | apavargAbhAvaprasaN^gAt.h | AgantukaM tu nopapadyate | apariNAmitvAt.h | ataH kartR^itvamiva bhoktR^itvamapyAtmano na shakyamaN^gIkartum.h | nacha pratItivirodhaH | pratIterabhAvAt.h | vyavahAra eva hi kevalaM bhoktA.a.atmeti | sa cha kartR^itvavyavahAravatprakR^itipuruShavivekAgrahamAtranibandhana iti |
syAdetat.h | yeShAM puruSho bhoktA teShAM mokShAbhAvaH syAt.h | prakR^itisaMyoganimitto hi puruShasya bhogastairaN^gIkriyate | "puruShasya darshanArthaM kaivalyArthaM tathA pradhAnasya | paN^.hgvandhavadubhayorapi saMyogastatkR^itaH sargaH' iti vachanAt.h | nacha prakR^itipuruShasaMyogaH kadApyapaiti yena puruShasya mokShaH syAdityata Aha- bhedagrahAditi ||
tayoH prakR^itipuruShayoH bhoginAM puruShasya bhogamabhyupagachChatAM mate | ayamabhisandhisteShAm.h | prakR^itisaMyogo hi puruShasya na kevalaM bhogArthaH | kinnAmApavargArthashcha | tatra vivekAgrahasachivo bhogAya bhavati | vivekagrahe chApavargAya | karotu nAma paunaHpunyena shabdAdyupabhogaM prakR^itiH | anayA vivekakhyAtirakR^iteti | kR^itavivekakhyAtistu na shabdAdyupabhojayati | avivekakhyAtinibandhano hi tadupabhogo, nibandhanAbhAve na bhavitumarhati | tachchoktam.h "dR^iShyA mayetyupekShaka eko, dR^iShyAhamityuparamatyantA | sati saMyogo.api tayoH prayojanaM nAsti sargasya iti | tathA "raN^gasya darshayitvA nivartate nartakI 
yathA nR^ittAt.h | puruShasya tathA.a.atmAnaM prakAshya vinivartate prakR^itiH' iti | nacha nivR^ittA.api punaH pravatsyartIti shaN^kanIyam.h | prayojanAbhAvAt.h | uktaM cha "prakR^iteH sukumArataraM na kiJNchidastIti me matirbhavati | tasyApi svenaiva nivR^itteH | 
nanu cha yeShAM mate puruShasya bhoga eva nAsti teShAM kathaM mokShaH | bandhAbhAvAt.h | tathAcha yogAnushAsanavaiyarthyamityata Aha- sa eveti ||
sa bhedagraha eva muktiruddhiShyA | bhedAgrahanibandhano bhrama eva hi bandhaH | sa cha bhedagrahe sati nivartate saiva muktiH | na tvaparA.astItyataH sa evetyuktam.h | na punarbhedagraha eva muktiH | tasyApi nivartanIyatvAt.h | nApi vivekakhyAtimityuktatvAditi |
evamupanyastaM matamadhunA nirasanIyam.h | tatra sUtrakR^itA kramavivakShitvA "rachanAnupapatteshcha nAnumAnam.h' iti prathamaM parapakShopAlambhaM vidhAyAnantaraM "pravR^itteshcha' iti svapakShasAdhanaM vihitam.h | bhAShyakArastu sAdhakapramANasya tattvapratipattyantaraN^gatvena tadupanyAsasya prAthamyaM parapakShanirAsAya tasthaiyarhetorbahiraN^gatvena tadupanyAsyAnantaryamiti kramamapi grAhayiShyan.h vyatyayena vyAchakShANaH pravR^itteshcheti sUtrasya pAtanikArthamAha- Ishasyeti || 
asaN^grahAt.h anabhyupagamAt.h | evetyasya doShasyolbaNatvaM sUchayati | tAvubhApi puruShasya bhoktR^itvAbhoktR^itvapakShau | 
nanvaprAmANikasyeshvarasyAnabhyupagame kathamayuktatvamityataH pravR^itteshcheti sUtrArthatayeshvare pramANamAha- chetaneti || 
yadA yasmAt.h | tasmAditi labhyate | etAdR^ishatvaM paTavachchetanechChAnusAreNodbhUtatvam.h | anyasya mahadAdeH, vastutvAt.h kAryatvAdanumIyamAnamiti sheShaH | kena ityAkShepe |
ayamatra prayogaH | mahadAdikaM chetanechChAdhInotpattikaM kAryatvAtpaTavaditi | yadvA mahadAdyudbhavaH chetanechChAdhIna udbhavatvAtpaTodbhavavaditi prayoktavyam.h | prayogadvayasUchanAya paTodbhava dR^iShyAntamuktvA vastutvAditi hetumAha | evamuktAvupalakShaNatvaM hi ubhayatra j~nAyeta | upalakShaNaM chaitat.h | mahadAdyupAdAnaM chetanamadhiShThitaM upAdAnatvAttantuvadityAdyapi draShyavyam.h | nachAnyashchetanastathA bhavitumarhatIti sarvAtishayI puruSha Ishvara eva siddhayatIti |   Vyasa-(21) 

syAdetat.h | mahadAdikaM na tAvatpratyakShasiddham.h | avyaktatvAt.h | ataH sAN^khayAchAryavachanAt.h tatprayuktAnumAnAdvA tadavagamo.abhyupagantavyaH | taishchAnevaMvidhameva taduktamanumitaM cheti bAdhaH | anyathA.a.ashrayAsiddhiriti | maivam.h | vedatastadavagamAt.h | uktaM hIdam.h "ajAmekAm.h' ityAdishrutiH pradhAnamapi pratipAdayatIti |
nanu puruShashchetano nAntaHkaraNam.h | ichChA chAntaHkaraNadharmo na chetanasyAvikArasya | ataH aprasiddhavisheShaNatA bAdho vA | paTAderapyevambhAvAbhAvAd.hdR^iShyAntasya sAdhyavaikalyaM cheti chenna | Atmana evechChAvattvasya vakShyamANatvAt.h | 
tathA.apyudbhavo nAmotpattirabhivyaktirvA | nAdyaH | prathamaprayoge.aprasiddhavisheShaNatvAt.h | dR^iShyAntasya sAdhyavikalatvAchcha | dvitIye chAshrayAsiddheH | mayA satkAryavAdasya abhyupagatatvAt.h | dvitIye.apyeta eva doShAH | tvayA vyaktyanabhyupagamAditi chenna | asatkAryavAdasya sAdhitatvAt.h | satkAryavAde pramANAbhAvAchcha | asadakaraNAdityAdibhishcha kiM kAryasya prAkkaraNavyApArAtsattvamAtraM sAdhyam.h utAtyantasattvam.h | Adye siddhasAdhanam.h | sadasattvAbhyupagamAt.h | dvitIye tvasadakaraNAditivatsadakaraNAdityapi samAnam.h | nahi sannAtmA kenachitkriyate | 
nanvasataH kathaM karmatvam.h | sataH kathaM kAryatvamityapi samAnam.h | anena ghaTo jAyata ityapi pratyuktam.h | tarhi ghaTaM karotItyAdeH ko.arthaH | mR^ittikAM ghaTIkarotIti | mR^ittikA ghaTIbhavatIti | asadutpattau kharaviShANamapi kuto notpadyata iti chet.h | tadAtmakasyopAdAnasyAbhAvAditi brUmaH | anyathA sata utpattAvAtmA.api kuto notpadyata iti samAnam.h | 
ya(da)dyapi kAryeNa kAraNaM sambaddhaM tadupajanayati utAsambaddhameveti pR^iShyam.h | tatra kAraNashabdenopAdAnaM vA vivakShitaM nimittaM vA | Adye janayatItyeva neShyate | kintu nimittakAraNAni tat.h kAryatAM nayanti | dvitIye tu kAryAkAreNAsambaddhaM kAraNAkAreNa sambaddhamityuttaram.h | ata eva nAtiprasaN^gaH | shaktishcha kAraNAnAM sadasadviShayA | anyathA nirviShayatvApAtAt.h | nahi sat.h kartuM shakyaM bhavati |
yachcha tantupaTayorabhedAnumAnaM tatrAbhedamAtrasAdhane siddhasAdha(nam.h)natvam.h | bhedAbhedAN^gIkArAt.h | atyantAbhedasAdhane tantudharmatvaM tAvadasiddham.h | nahi svayameva svasya dharmo bhavati | nahi upachAro.anumAnapravR^itteraN^gam.h | atiprasaN^gAt.h | kathaM cha tantudharmatvaM paTasya | tantuvisheShaNatvamiti chenna | puruShAdivisheShaNe daNDAdau vyabhichArAt.h | tadAshritatvamiti chenna | 
abhedenAsiddhiprasaN^gAt.h | kuNDabadarAdau vyabhichArAchcha | tadAtmakatvamiti chenna | sAdhyavishiShyatvApatteH | abhedena bhedAbhAvaH sAdhyata iti chenna | bhedAbhAvAtiriktasyAbhedasya anabhyupagamAt.h | abhyupagamo.api bAdhAt.h | evamupAdAnopAdeyabhAvo.apyasiddha eva | nahi svayamevopAdanamupAdeyaM cheti yuktam.h | karaNatvakarmatvayobharedaniyatatvAt.h | saMyogAprAptyabhAvashchAtyantabhedAbhAvAdupapatsyate | gurutvAntarakAryAdarshanaM chAbhedAN^gIkAreNa bhaviShyati | 
etena kAryatvamabhUtvAbhAvitvaM chedasiddhamasmAkam.h | abhivyaktidharmakatvaM chedyuShmAkamiti cha nirastam.h | tadidamuktam.h- kena vAryata iti ||
tadevaM paTAdyutpattau chetanasya kuvindAdeH pravR^itterupalambhAttad.hdR^iShyAntena mahadAdyutpatterapi chetanechChAdhInatvamityevaM svapakShaM prasAdhya parapakShanirAsArthaM rachanAnupapatteshcha nAnumAnamiti sUtraM vyAkhyAtuM pIThamArachayati- nacheti ||
na kevalamasmanmate pramANasadbhAvaH | kintu sAN^khayoktArthe pradhAnasya svAtanteNa jagatkAraNatve kimapi pramANaM nAsti | tathAhi | kimatra pratyakShaM pramANaM syAduta Agamo.athavA.anumAnaM vA | nAdyaH | taddhayasmadAdInAM vA yoginAM vA | na prathamaH | asyArthasyAtIndriyatvAt.h | na dvitIyaH | asiddheH | nahi evaM yoginaH pashyantItyasmAkaM pramANamasti | 
nApyAgamaH | sa hyapauruSheyaH pauruSheyo vA syAt.h | nAdya ityAha- shrutireveti ||
shrutirno.asmAkameva mate pramA hi | savarA.api hi shrutirIshvarameva svAtanteNa sakalajagatkAraNaM sarvaj~naM sarvashaktiM pratipAdayati | pradhAnaM cha tadAyattasattApratItipravR^ittimattadadhiShThitaM jagadupAdAnamAtramiti | tathAhi | "yaH sarvaj~naH sarvavit.h' | "yo yonimadhitiShThatyekaH' ityAdi | tathAcha shrutiH parasya pratipakShabhUtaiva | 
pauruSheyo.api kiM smR^itItihAsapurANalakShaNaH | uta sAN^khayAchAryapraNItaH | nAdyaH | tasyApyasmanmatAnusAritvAt.h | "prakR^itiM puruShaM chaiva pravishya puruShottamaH | kShobhayAmAsa bhagavAnsR^iShyayarthaM jagato vibhuH' ityAdivachanAt.h | na dvitIyaH | tatprANyasyAsammateH | Aptoktatvena tatprAmANyasiddhiriti chettatrAha- Aptatvamiti ||
uktamArgeNa shrutireva pramA hi na ityuktarItyA shrutiviruddhabhAShitvAdityarthaH | vaktuH sAN^khayapraNetuH | yadvA itareShAM chAnupalabdherityuktamArgeNa | sAN^khayashAstre.api hyAkhyAyikAsu yogyAnupalabdhibAdhitA bahavo.arthAH pratipAdyante | athavA "avipralambhastajj~nAnam.h' ityAdyuktamArgeNAptatvanishchAyakapramANAbhAvAdityarthaH | "kapilo vAsudevAkhyastantraM sAN^khayaM jagAda ha | brahmAdibhyashcha devebhyo bhR^igvAdibhyastathaiva cha | tathaivAsuraye sarvavedArthaparibR^iMhitam.h | sarvavedaviruddhaM cha kapilo.anyo jagAda ha | sAN^khayamAsuraye.anyasmai kutarkaparibR^iMhitam.h' iti purANoktamArgeNeti vA | "R^iShiM prasUtaM kapilam.h' ityAdishrutyudAharaNamapyanenaiva nirastam.h | etenaiva "AgamAdyogipratyakShAvagame' ityapAkR^itam.h | 
na kevalamuktamArgeNAptatvAnupapattiH | kinnAmAnupapannabhAShitvAdapItyAha- aprAmANyeti ||
apishabdena prAmANyasvatastvamapi samuchchinoti | j~nAnAnAM prAmANyamaprAmANyaM j~nAnakAraNamAtrAdhInotpattikamiti svIkaroti sAN^khayaH | tachchAnupapannamityato.apyasau nAptaH | 
kathaM prAmANyAprAmANyayoH svatastvamanupapannamityata Aha- mAyivaditi ||
prAmANyAprAmANyayorj~nAnakAraNamAtrajanyatve sAN^khayasya vachanenotpannaM j~nAnaM pramANamapramANaM chetyubhayAtmakaM vA syAt.h | parasparavirAdhenobhayavikalaM vA j~nAnamAtramutpa(dyeta)dyate | niHsvabhAvasya j~nAnasyAnupapattyA notpa(dyate)dyeta vA | Adye sadasadvilakShaNaM vishvaM manyamAno mAyAvAdI yathA svoktaniShedhI sadvilakShaNamityuktyA prAptasyAsattvasya, svayameva asadvilakShaNamiti niShedhAt.h | asadvilakShaNamityuktyA cha prAptasya sattvasya svayameva sadvilakShaNamiti niShedhAt.h | tathA sAN^khayo.api svoktAkhilaniShedhI syAt.h | tadvAkyajanitaj~nAnasya yAthArthye hi prakR^itirjagatkAraNamityAdiko.artho yo labdhaH, sa evArthastasyAyAthArthye niShiddhaH syAt.h | ayAthAthyarsya viShayaviparyAsAnatirekAt.h | ubhayasvatastve vastuno viruddhAkAradvayAliN^gitatvaM prasajyeteti bhAvaH | mAyAshabdasya vrIhyAditvAnmAyIti sAdhu | 
nanvevamapi yAthArthyena prakR^itirjagatkAraNamityAdiko.arthastAvatsiddhayatItyata Aha- nacheti ||
nahi parasparavirodhe kimapi siddhayatIti bhAvaH | tarhi prAmANyasya kA gatiriti chet.h | aprAmANye.api dIyatAM dR^iShyiH | dvitIye doShamAha- nacheti || j~nAnaM hi yathAvasthitamayathAvasthitaM vA.arthaM viShayIkuryAt.h | tR^itIyaprakArAnirUpaNAt.h | tathAcha prAmANyAprAmANyavikalaM j~nAnam.h ayaHshalAkAvadaviShayameva syAt.h | evaMcha na sAN^khayavachanAtkiJNchitprasiddhayatIti | tR^itIye tu jagadAndhyameva syAdityAha- nacheti ||
syAdetat.h yadA j~nAnakAraNaM guNopetaM tadA tadIyAyAmaprAmANyajananashaktau guNena pratibaddhAyAM pramANaj~nAnamevotpadyate | yadA tu doShopetaM tadA doSheNa prAmANyajananashaktau pratibaddhAyAM apramANaj~nAnamevotpadyate | nahi kimapi karaNaM yugapadubhayopetamubhayavikalaM vA sambhavati | yenoktadoShaH syAditi | uchyate | kimarthamitthaM kalpyate | j~nAnasyobhayAkAratvaprasakteriti chet.h | tatprasaktirapi kuto nAbhyupagantavyA | virodhabhayAditi chet.h | karaNe.apyubhayashaktivirodhAtkuto na bibheShi | 
yadapi viruddhakAryadvayajanakaM karaNaM tatsahakArisAhityAhitashaktikameva | prakR^ite cha tathA.abhyupagame dvayorapi paratastvApattiH | 
kiJNcha vachane kau guNadoShau | AptAnAptatvapraNItatve iti chet.h | tarhyubhayAbhAvAdvedavAkyenobhayAtmakamanubhayAtmakaM vA j~nAnamutpadyeta | notpadyeta vA | anAptapraNItatvaM guNa iti chet.h | tarhyAptApraNItatvaM doSho.api kinna syAditi sa eva prasaN^gaH | 
etena sAN^khayAchAryavachanaM svata eva pramANaM kimAptinishchayenetyapi nirastam.h | aprAmANyasyApi svatastvenoktasakaladoShApatteH | atha mahAjanaparigrahAttatprAmANyanishchaya iti chenna | pUjyArthatve.asiddheH | bahvarthatve savyabhichAratvAtsandigdhAsiddheshcheti | 
mA bhUtprakR^itikAraNatve prapaJNchasya pratyakShaM pramANam.h | mA cha bhUdAgamaH | anumAnaM tu bhaviShyati | yathoktam.h | "bhedAnAM parimANAtsamanvayAchChaktitaH pravR^itteshcha | kAraNakAryAvibhAgAdavibhAgAdvaishvarUpasya' iti |
ayamarthaH | kAraNakAryavibhAgAdavibhAgAdvaishvarUpyasya mUlakAraNamastyavyaktam.h | yathA kUrmasharIre santyevAN^gAni tato vibhajyante | tasminnevAvyaktIbhavanti | evaM kAraNAnmR^itpiNDAddhemapiNDAdvA kAryANi ghaTamukuTAdIni vibhajyante | santyeva cha pR^ithivyAdIni kAraNAttanmAtrAt.h | santyeva cha tanmAtrANyahaN^kArAt.h | sanneva chAhaN^kAro mahataH | sadeva cha mahatparamAvyaktAditi | so.ayaM kAraNAtparamAvyaktAtpAramparyeNa vishvasya kAryasya vibhAgaH pratisarge | mR^itpiNDaM hemapiNDaM vA ghaTamukuTAdayo vishanto.avyaktIbhavantIti tatkAraNarUpamevAnabhivyaktaghaTamukuTAdikAryamapekShyAvyaktaM bhavati | evaM pR^ithivyAdayastanmAtrANi vishantaH svApekShayA tanmAtramavyaktayanti | evaM tanmAtrANyahaN^kAraM vishantyahaN^kAramavyaktayanti | evamahaN^kAro mahAntamAvishanmahAntamavyaktayati | mahAnprakR^itiM svakAraNaM vishati | prakR^itestu na kvachinnivesha iti sA sarvakAryANAmavyaktameva | so.ayamavibhAgaH prakR^itau vaishvarUpyasya nAnArUpasya kAryasya | tasmAtkAraNe kAryasya sata eva vibhAgAvibhAgAbhyAmavyaktaM kAraNamastIti | 
itashcha, shaktitaH pravR^itteH | kAraNashaktito hi kAryaM pravartate | ashaktAtkAraNAtkAryasyAnutpatteH | shaktishcha kAraNagatA na kAryasyAvyaktatvAdanyA | astu tarhi mahata eva paramAvyaktatvamityata uktaM bhedAnAM parimANAditi | mahadAdInAmavyApakatvAdavyaktakAraNakatvaM ghaTAdivadityarthaH | itashcha, samanvayAt.h | sukhaduHkhabhogasamanvitAni hi kAryANi | yAni cha yadUpamanugatAni tAni tatsvabhAvAvyaktakAni | yathA mR^iddhemarUpamanugatA ghaTamukuTAdayo mR^iddhemapiNDAvyaktakAH | tasmAdasti sukhaduHkhamahohAtmakAnAM sattvarajastamasAM sAmyAvasthA.avyaktaM bhedAnAmiti |
yadyapyetAnyanumAnAnyavyaktasvarUpaM sAdhayanti | tathA.api mahadAdikAraNatayaiva tadetaiH siddhayatIti | atra vaktavyam.h | kimetairanumAnairjagadupAdAnatAmAtreNAvyaktaM siddhayati, uta svAtanteNA(pIti)pi | Adye siddhasAdhanam.h | asmAbhirapi vishvopAdAnasya pradhAnasyAbhyupagatatvAt.h | "sharIrarUpakaH' iti hyuktam.h | dvitIyaM nirAkartuM sUtram.h | rachanAnupapatteshcha nAnumAnamiti | tadvayAchaShye- idamiti ||
mahAdAdikAryamityarthaH | achetanavashaM svatantrAchetanAdhInotpattikam.h | pratipannavat.h | pradhAnavat.h | AstAM tAvaddUShaNAntaram.h iti pratyanumAnenaiva pratiShiddhasya pradhAnasvAtantyasya mUlAnumA sAdhikAnumA kena sAmarthyena bhavet.h pramANamiti sheShaH | mUlAnumeti vA.a.avartanIyam.h | kim.h AkShepe | akAryatvamatropAdhiriti chenna | paTAdau sAdhyAvyApteH | paTAdeH kuvindAdyadhiShThitatantvAdikAyartvasyAnvayavyatirekAbhyAmupalambhAt.h | 
evaM pradhAnasya rachanAyAH svatantrapravR^itteranumAnavirodhenAnupapatternAnumAnaM tatra pramANamiti sUtrAkSharayojanAM manasi nidhAya sUtratAtparyamuktam.h | idAnIM tAmeva vivR^iNvanpratipakShAntaramAha- svatantreti || 
chashabdo.anumAnAntarasamuchchaye | kuta evetyanvayaH | ayamatra prayogaH | pradhAnaM svatantrapravR^ittirahitam.h achetanatvAt.h | tantvAdivaditi |
nanvachetanatve.api pradhAnasya svAtanteNa pravR^ittirastu ko virodhaH | tathAcha vipakShe bAdhakAbhAvAdaprayojako.ayaM heturityata Aha- achetanatvamiti ||
tAvadeva hyanenAshaN^kanIyaM yasminnAshaN^kayamAne svavachanasvakriyAsvanyAyapramANAntaravirodho na prAduShyAt.h | nahi kashchidevaM 
shaN^kate | mUko.api vaktA kinna syAt.h | shabdo.apratipAdakaH kinna bhavet.h | anumAnatvAt.h anumAnamAtramapramANaM kuto na syAt.h | agniranuShNaH kuto na bhavediti | na hyeShA shaN^kApishAchI kadAchichChAntimupAgachChati | tasmAdevAmAshaN^kamAno na laukiko nApi parIkShaka ityunmattavadupekShaNIyaH | prakR^ite chAchetanatvaM svAtantyaM chAtmapramAhatam.h | svavyAhataM pramANaviruddhaM cha | tasmAdachetanatve.api svatantrapravR^ittirastu pradhAnasyeti shaN^kaiva notpattumarhatIti kimatra bAdhakopanyAseneti |
nanvachetanasya svAtantyashaN^kAyAM kathaM svavyAhatiH | nahi svAtantyaM nAma chaitanyam.h | nApyachetanatvaM nAmAsvAtantyam.h | kathaMcha pramANavirodhaH, ityata svavyAghAtaM tAvadupapAdayituM svAtantyaM vyAkhyAti- svechCheti ||
pravR^ittAviti sheShaH | vido vidurityanena sakalavidvatsammatametadityAha | ata eva hi svAtantAbhAvAd.hvR^ikShastiShThatItyAdikartR^itvavyavahAro gauNa iti sarve pratipannAH | 
tathA.api kathaM svavyAhatiH | nahyachetanatvaM nAmechChAvirahaH | kinnAma chaitanyaviraha ityata Aha- kuta iti ||
achetanasyechChA kutaH kAraNAjjAyate | na kutashchit.h | j~nAnameva hIchChAyA janakamityarthaH | tathA.api kimityata Aha- sechChaM chediti ||
sechChaM chedaN^gIkR^itaM tadA tadachetanaM kiM chetanamevetyarthaH | 
etaduktaM bhavati | achetanamapi pradhAnaM svAtanteNa pravR^ittimadastviti vadatA.achetanamichChAvadastvityuktaM syAt.h | svechChAnusAritvasya svAtantyashabdArthatayA sarvasammatatvAt.h | achetanasyechChAvattvamaN^gIkurvANena chetanatvamapyaN^gIkartavyaM syAt.h | anvayavyatirekAbhyAmichChAyAH svasamAnAshrayachaitanyakAryatvAvadhAraNAt.h | kAryAN^gIkAre kAraNAnaN^gIkArasyAnuchitatvAt.h | achetanaM chetanamiti cha sphuTA vyAhatiriti | 
etenaitadapi nirastam.h | achetanatvaM svAtantyaM cha yadi parasparavyAhataM tarhyachetanatvena svatantrapravR^ittirAhityasAdhane sAdhyAvishiShyatAdoShaH syAditi | nahyasmAbhirachetanatvasvAtantyayoH vandhyA apatyavatItivatsAkShAdvirodho.abhihitaH | kintu svAtantyabalena chaitanyaM pareNAN^gI(kArya)kArayitvA anenaiva svAtantAN^gIkAre.achetanatvAnupapattiriti bAdhakaM choktaM bhavati |
evamachetanasya svAtantAN^gIkAre svavyAhatimupapAdya pramANavirodhamapyupapAdayati- ichChAmIti ||
hishabdenAsyAnumAnasya vishvajanaprasiddhatvaM sUchayati | evashabdasyApagataivaityanvayaH | nijAnubhavaH sAkShyanubhavaH | ahamichChAmIti tAvadichChA AtmasambandhinI sAkShiNAnubhUyate | nacha sA dvikartR^ikA sambhavati | kvApyekasya vyApArasya dvikartR^ikatvAnupalambhAt.h | tatashchAchetanasyechChAN^gIkR^itA(vaitada)che(tta)danubhavavirodhAdachetanasyechChApagatA nAstIti yAvat.h | ichChAbhAve cha svechChAnusAritvalakShaNaM svAtantyaM dUrotsAritamiti bhAvaH | 
nanu navamastyanubhavaH kintvahamichChA(mIchChA)mIti vyavahAramAtram.h | tasyApi nimittaM bhedAgrahaH | AtmA hi nityo nirvikArashchaitanyamAtravapurna tasyechChAdikartR^itvamAgantukaM sambhavati | kintvantaHkaraNasyaiva prasavadharmatvAt.h | tayoshchAtmAntaHkaraNayorbhedAgrahAditaretaradharmavyavahAraH pravartate | bhedAgrahe cha nimittaM sannidhAnam.h | yathoktam.h | "tasmAttatsaMyogAdachetanaM chetanAvadiva liN^gam.h | guNakartR^itve cha tathA karteva bhavatyudAsInaH' iti | ato.anubhavabalAchchetanasyaivechChAvattvaM nAchetanasyetyayuktamityata Aha- yadIti ||
yadi evamanubhava eva nAsti kintu vyavahAramAtram.h, atra cha vyavahAre bhedAgraha eva nimittamuchyate, tadA sa bhedAgraho ghaTasya kiM (kathaM) na syAt.h | vyavahAraheturiti sheShaH | idamuktaM bhavati | svaprakAshAnubhavApalApadoShastAvat.h | vyavahAre cha nimittaM nAsti | nacha bhedAgrahaH | vishiShyavyavahArasya tAdR^ishaj~nAnakAryatAniyamAt.h | anyathA ghaTapaTAvapItaretarabhedaM na gR^ihNIta itItaretaradharmasaMsargavyavahAraH syAditi |
nanu gR^ihyamANayorbhedagraho vyavahAraheturna tu bhedAgrahamAtram.h | nacha ghaTapaTau svarUpaM gR^ihNItastatkathamatiprasaN^ga iti chet.h | kimayaM vishiShyo bhedAgraho.antaHkaraNasya, utAtmanaH | nAdyaH | tasyAchetanatvena svarUpagrahAnupapatteH | upapattau vA sa kathaM vishiShyo bhedAgraho ghaTasya na syAt.h | tathAcha vyavahAro.api syAt.h | nanvantaHkaraNe.asti chaitanyAropo na ghaTe, ato nAtiprasaN^ga iti chet.h | kiM tasya nimittam.h | sannidhAnamiti chet.h | tarhi sarvagatAtmasannidhAnaM ghaTe.apyastIti kathaM sa na ghaTasya syAt.h | nanu na saMyogamAtraM nimittam.h | kintUpakAryopakArakabhAve sati | sa chAstyAtmAntaHkaraNayoH | puruShasya darshanArthamityuktatvAt.h iti chet.h | tarhi ghaTo.api puruShasyopakAraka iti kathaM sa na ghaTasya syAt.h |
dvitIye vyavahAro.api kimAtmana utAntaHkaraNasya | nAdyaH | tasya nirvikArasya vyavahArakriyAnupapatteH | upapattau vA 
kimichChayA.aparAddham.h | dvitIye.anyagatena bhedAgraheNAnya(tra)sya vyavahArashchetkathaM sa na ghaTasya syAt.h | 
kiJNcha yadi bhedAgrahAdantaHkaraNadharma evechChA.a.atmani vyavahriyata ityaN^gIkriyate tadA ghaTasyApyAtmanA bhedAgrahAtpR^ithubudhnodarAkAro.ahamiti vyavahAraH kathaM na syAditi gUDhAbhisandheruttaram.h |
yadvA.atra chAtmAntaHkaraNayoshcha sphuTaM pratibhAsamAnabhedayorapIti hR^idayam.h | yadi bhedAgrahaH syAttadA kathaM sa bhedAgraho ghaTasyAtmanashcha na syAditi yojanA | 
athavaivaM vadanpraShyavyaH | bhedAgrahaH kiM bhedagrahasya virodhI na veti | neti pakShe kathaM sa ghaTasyAtmanA paTAdinA vA na syAdityuttaram.h |
nanu bhedagraho bhedAgrahavirodhI | sa chAsti ghaTa iti kutastatra bhedAgrahastatprayukto vyavahAro veti gUDhAbhisandhimajAnato dvitIyapakShamAshaN^kayAha- mana iti ||
bhedata iti tR^itIyArtho tasiH | yadi bhedagraho bhedAgrahavirodhIti bhedena gR^ihyamANe ghaTe na bhedAgraha ityuchyate, tadA me mana iti manaso.api bhedena gR^ihItatvAnnAtmanA bhedAgrahaH syAt.h | tathAcha bhedAgrahanimitto.ahamichChAmIti vyavahAra ityasat.h | kintvanubhavanimitta eva | ata eva nAntaHkaraNadharmasyAtmanyAropa ityapi yuktam.h | bhedagrahasadbhAvena AropahetorbhedAgrahasyAyogAt.h | nahyaviditabhedaM sambandhitayA gR^ihyate | Atmanyapi prasaN^gAt.h | kena punaH pramANena mano gR^ihyate | sAkShiNeti vadAmaH | tathAhi | natAvachchakShurAdinA tadavagamaH | arUpidravyatvAt.h | chakShurAdyavyApAre.apyupalabdheH | nachAnumAnena | liN^gAbhAvAt.h | nanvasti yugapajj~nAnAnutpattirmanaso liN^gam.h | tathAhi | bAhyendriyeShu svaiH svairviShayaiyarugapatsannikR^iShyeShvAtmanA.adhiShThiteShvapi na yugapajj~nAnAni jAyante | tena j~nAyate.astyetebhyo.anyatsahakAri | yatsaMyogakramavashAjj~nAnakramaH prakramata iti ||
atra kashchidAha | Atmana evaivaMvidhasAmarthyakalpanopapattAvanyathAsiddhamanumAnam.h | manasaH pratIndriyasaMyogavyavahAre kramavati kAraNAntarashUnye.anaikAntikaM cha | phalasya cha vR^ikShashatpatataH kramavartinyAkAshasaMyoge kuThArAdivyApAre cha | indriyANAM prativiShayasaMyogavyApAre cheti | tadayuktam.h | dR^iShyAnusAriNI hi kalpanA | kartA hyanekakaraNAdhiShThAnena yugapannAnAkAryANi kurvANo dR^iShyaH | tathAhi | yugapanmANavako gachChati paThati panthAnamIkShate vahati cha kamaNDalum.h | tasmAnnaiva kartR^idharmo yuktaH kalpayitum.h | kintu dR^iShyatvAd.h dravyAntaramevAvyApakam.h | anaikAntyaM tu nAstyeva | tatrApi kriyAkramAdernimittasya vidyamAnatvAditi | 
atrochyate | asti tAvadavivekinAmapi manaHpratItiH | mama mano.anyatra gatamityAdivyavahArAt.h | nacha te yugapajj~nAnAnutpattiM jAnanti | pratyuta yugapadeva j~nAnotpattiM manyante | anyathA vyAsaN^ge kramadarshanenAnyatrApi kramAnumAnaM parasya vyarthaM syAt.h | tasmAlliN^gadarshanAtprAgeva bhavadidaM manoj~nAnaM na tannimittakamiti | astu tarhi buddhayAdInAmasamavAyikAraNasya saMyogasyAshrayatayA manaHsiddhiH | maivam.h | pratyakShaj~nAne tAvadindriyAtmasaMyogasyaivAsamavAyikAraNatvasyopapatteH | anumityAdau liN^gaj~nAnAdeH | smR^itau bhAvanAyAH, sukhAdAviShyArthopalabdhAderiti | nityavisheShaguNAnAM saMyogAsamavAyikAraNatvaniyamAnnaivamiti chenna | vibhAga(ja)shabdajashabde vyabhichArAt.h | ashrAvaNattvena hetuvisheShaNAnneti chet.h | yathA tarhi vibhAgAdishabde kAraNAntaradarshanAttannirAsArthaM vyAptigrahaNavelAyAM prayatyate tathA sukhAdinirAsAya prayatanIyam.h | asamavAyikAraNAntaradarshanasya tulyatvAt.h | nimittaM taditi chenna | asamavAyikAraNalakShaNasyAtivyAptiprApteriti | nacha sukhAdyupalabdhikaraNatvena manassiddhiH | sAkShisiddhatayA.anyathAsiddheH | 
evamanumAnAntaramapi nirasanIyam.h | nachAgamo manasi pramANam.h | jAtibadhirANAmapi tatpratyayAt.h | tasmAtsiddhaM sAkShigrAhyatvaM manasaH | tasya cha tenaivAtmano bhinnatayA grahaNAdbhedAgrahAsambhavenechChAmyahamIti na bhedAgrahanibandhano vyavahAra iti |
nanu cha "kAmaHsaN^kalpo vichikitsA shraddhA.ashraddhA dhR^itiradhR^itirbhIrhIrityetatsarvaM mana eva' iti shrutau kAmasyAntaHkaraNarUpatvaM tAvatpratIyate | nacha shrautenArthenAnyathA bhavituM yuktam.h | ato balavadbAdhakopanipAtAdichChAmyahamiti bhedAgrahanimittaM vyavahAramAtrametaN^gIkaraNIyam.h | na tvAtmana ichChAsambandhAnubhavaH | nacha me mana iti bhedagrahAttadagrahAsambhavaH | me chaitanyamitivadvayavahAramAtratvAt.h | nachoktAnupapattiH | sattvarajastamasAmAdikAryaM hi buddhirityuchyate | sA chAMshatrayavatI | puruShoparAgo viShayoparAgo vyApArAveshashchetyaMshAH | bhavati hyahamidaM karomIti | tatrAhamiti chetanoparAgo darpaNasyaiva mukhoparAgo bhedAgrahAdatAttvikaH | idamiti viShayoparAga indriyapranADikayA pariNatibhedo darparasyeva malasambandhaH pAramArthikaH, 
tathobhayAyatto vyApArAveshaH | eShaiva digahamichChAmItyatrApItyata Aha- ubhayeti ||
tushabdo.avadhAraNe | tata ityupaskartavyam.h | yataH kAraNAtkAmasyobhayAtmakatA.asti | AtmadharmatA manodharmatA cha | tata eva manaH kAma iti shrutirupapadyate | idamuktaM bhavati | bhavedidaM bhedAgrahakalpanam.h | yadyAtmanaH kAmavattvaM pAramArthikaM na syAt.h | nachaitadasti | bAdhakAbhAvAt.h | dvividho hi kAmo.asti | eka Atmadharmo.aparo.antaHkaraNadharmaH | tatrAntaHkaraNadharmaM kAmamabhipretya shrutiH pravR^ittA, nAtmanaH kAmavattvaM bAdhate | nahi devadatto gomAniti vAkyaM yaj~nadattasya gosambandhaM bAdhituM shaknotIti | 
syAdetadevam.h | yadi kAmadvaividhyaM pramitaM syAt.h, etadeva kuta iti chet.h | shrutyanubhavabalAttAvat.h | prakArasahasrAnusaraNe.apyaghaTanAyAM khalvanubhavApalApasAhasamabhyupeyam.h | pramANAntaraM chAha- priyeti || 
priyamityAtyantikeShyamuchyate.apriyamiti cha tAtkAlikeShyam.h | viShayeNa viShayiNa upalakShaNam.h | asya kAmasya | ayamarthaH | asti tAvadAstikakAmukasya puruShasya srakchandavanitAdau idaM me syAdityekataH kAmaH | anyatastyajeyamiti | nachaika evAyam.h | viruddharUpatvAt.h | nacha dvAvapi manodharmau, yaugapadyAt.h | yugapatsajAtIyadharmajananAyogAt.h | nacha yaugapadyaM nAsti | anubhavasiddhatvAt.h | bAdhakAbhAvAchcha | tatra yo.apriyaviShayaH saH antaHkaraNadharmaH yastu priyaviShayaH sa Atmadharma iti |
yadvA priyApi्rayashabdAbhyAM muktisaMsArAvuchyete | tatsambandhivibhedena kAmadvaividhyaM dR^ishyata iti | asti tAvatsaMsAre prachuro.ayamantaHkaraNavR^ittirUpaH kAmaH | asti chAsau muktau | "sa yadi pitR^ilokakAmo bhavati' ityAdishruteH | nachaika evAyam.h | muktAvantaHkaraNavilayAt.h | tathAchAsAvAtmadharmo.abhyupeyaH | nachAgantukadharmasambandho muktAviti prAgapi kAmadvaividhyaM siddhayatIti |
shrutibAdhaparihArasya prayojanamAha- tasmAditi ||
shrutivirodhasya parihR^itatvAdbhedAgrahaH kutaH pramANAtkalpanIyaH | kutashchAnubhavApalApena vyavahArasya tannimittatvam.h | na kuto.apItyarthaH | anenAchetanasya pradhAnasya svAtanteNa jagatkAraNatvaM sAdhayatAmanumAnamapi svavachanavirodhaH pramANavirodhashchoktau bhavataH | dR^iShyAntashcha sAdhyavikalaH | achetanasvAtantyasya kvApyasammateriti |
sUtrArthamupasaMharannAnumAnamityetatprakArAntareNa vyAchaShye- rachaneti || 
tattasmAt.h | sarvaj~nAnumAgatamanumAnaM prakR^ityAdikaM, kasyachitpratyakShaM, prameyatvAditi sarvamasAdhakAnumayA.avagatam.h | etadanumAnasiddhasarvaj~navAkyAvagatamiti yAvat.h | 
yadvA.anumAnasiddhaprAmANyakatvenAnumAnapradhAnatvena cha sarvaj~nAbhimatasya vAkyameva sarvaj~nAnumochyate | vyAkhyAnAntarasya chedaM prayojanam.h | yatprAguktaM na yogipratyakSheNa sAN^khayAchAryavachanena vA.ayamarthaH siddhayatIti tadapi sUtrasUchitameveti j~nApanam.h | yadA tu sarvaj~nAbhimatotprekShitayA bhedAnAM parimANAdityAdikayA.anumayA.avagatamAnumAnamiti yojanA | tadA vaichi(tya)trIpradarshanaM vyAkhyAnAntaraprayojanam.h | jagatkartR^i svAtanteNa jagatkAraNam.h | 
syAdetat.h | parimANAdihetubhistAvanmahadAdikAryANAM kimapi mUlakAraNamastItyavagamyate | tasyApi kAraNAntarakalpane pramANAbhAvAdanavasthAnAchcha | tasya cha svAtantyaM kArakAntarAprayojyatvameva natu svechChAnusAritvam.h | yenoktadoShaH syAt.h | tachcha tatprayoktuH kArakAntarasyAprAmANikatvAdeva siddham.h | nachAchetanasya tadasambhAvitam.h | achetaneShvapi payo.ambuprabhR^itiShu darshanAt.h | achetanameva hi payo.anyAnadhiShThitamapi vatsavivR^iddhayarthaM pravartate | dadhibhAvaM chApadyate | ghanavinirmuktaM chAmbu jambIranArikelAdiShvanekavidhaM vikAraM prApnoti | nAdeyaM chApasarpati | tR^iNaM cha gavA jagdhaM kShIrIbhavati | ayashchAyaskAntamabhisarpati | nacha "idaM nAchetanavasham.h' ityAdipramANavirodhaH | tasyoktasthAneShvevAnaikAntyam.h | nachedaM brahmavAdinAM sammatam.h | yena siddhasAdhanaM syAdityAshaN^kAparihArArthaM sUtram.h- || OM payo.ambuvachchettatrApi OM || iti | tadvayAchaShye- payo.ambvAdi cheti || 
upamA svArthasambhAvanAyAmasmadIyahetuvyabhichAre cheti sheShaH | yathA.atra sAdhyaM vyabhicharati tathA pakShe.api vyabhicharatu heturityevamarthaM hi vyabhichArodbhAvanam.h | tadatra na yujyate | chetanAchetanasyaitatprashAstivachanAt.h | pArameshvarapreraNApratipAdakashruteH | Adyashchashabdo laukikAnAM svatantratayA pratIyamAnamapItyarthe | dvitIyastu na kevalamachetanasya | kintUbhayasyApIti | 
etaduktaM bhavati | kArakAntarAprayojyatvalakShaNamapi svAtantyaM na pradhAnasyopapadyate | asambhAvitatvAt.h | 
uktAnumAnaviruddhatvAchcha |
yaduktamatra payombvAdivaditi | tadasat.h | tatrApIshvarapreraNayA "etasya vA akSharasya' ityadishrutisiddhatvAt.h | ata eva pradhAnasya paraprayojyatve pramANAbhAvo.api parAsta iti | sUtre payo.ambuvadityukte.api nodAharaNamAdaraNIyam.h | sthalAntare sambhAvanA vyabhichArashcha bhaviShyata ityAshaN^kAparihArArthasya "vyatirekAnavasthiteshchAnapekShatvAt.h' iti uttarasUtrasyApi vyAkhyAnAyAdipadaprayogaH | yadvA payo.ambugrahaNamupalakShaNamityabhipretyAdipadaM pratyuktam.h | uttarasUtraM tu kaimutyArtham.h | chetanapravR^itterapIshvaravyatirekeNAnavasthiterachetanapravR^ittestadadhInatvaM kimu vAchyamiti | tadvayAkhyAnAya chetanAchetanasya chetyuktam.h |   Vyasa-(22)

kiJNcha parimANAditi hetustAvadanaikAntikaH | sattvarajastamasAM sAmyAvasthA hi prakR^itiruchyate | sattvAdayashcha parimitA eva | yathoktam.h | abagnIranabho.ahaN^kR^inmahattattvaguNatrayaiH | kramAddashottaraiH' (Adi pu.veM.mAhA.2-46) iti | nacha prakR^itiravyaktAntaravatIti kathaM nAnaikAntyam.h | nacha parimitasyApi mUlaprakR^ititve bAdhakamasti | sArvatrikakAryAnutpattiparimitAnAmeva kAraNatvam.h | tantvAdiShu darshanAt.h | aparimitasya kR^itsnaikadeshavikalpAnupapatteshcha | asmAkaM tvIshvarashaktyaivopapadyate | 
samanvayAdityapyasat.h | yatkAryaM yadanugatimattattAdR^ikkAraNopetamityasyA vyApteravyaktAdvayaktajanmAN^gIkAreNaiva bhagnatvAt.h | shaktitaH pravR^itteshchetyetadapi na vivakShitArthasAdhakam.h | antarbhAvitakAryatvameva kAraNasya shaktirityasya siddhau hi tathA syAt.h | tachcha satkAryavAdanirvAhyamiti | ata eva vibhAgAvibhAgAvapi nirastau | vibhAgAvibhAgayoreva satkAryavAdasiddhayadhInayorasattvAt.h | svaprakriyAmAtreNArthasiddhau "sthUlakAyarsya loShThAdeH' ityAdinA tArkikaparikalpitAbhyAM vibhAgAvibhAgAbhyAM paramANukAraNatvamapi syAdityAstAM prapaJNchaH | 
nanvidaM ghaTTakuTTIprabhAtanyAyamanusarati | ichChAvattvamAtmana eva na tu jaDasyetyatra hi prathamamanubhavaH pramANIkR^itaH | tatra cha shrutivirodhe chodite.antaHkaraNadharma Atmadharmashcheti kAmasya dvaividhyAnna virodha ityuktam.h | evaJNchAtmana evechChAvattvaM na tvachetanasyeti tyaktamevetyAshaN^kAM siMhAvalokananyAyena pariharati- dvaividhye.apIti || 
kAmAderdvaividhye.api sAkShAdanubhavArUDhamAtmanaH kAmAdeH svAmitvaM tu kutaH pramANAdapodituM shakyate na kuto.apIti yojanA | shrutyapekShayA.a.adipadagrahaNam.h | apoditumiti samprasAraNaM ChAndasam.h | ayamatrottarakramaH | satyaM kAmo dvividha Atmadharmo manovR^ittishcheti | tatra manovR^ittimapi kAmaM pratyAtmana eva svAmitvaM na manasaH | ahaM kAmaya iti sAkShyanubhavasiddhatvAt.h | manasastu kAmaM pratyupAdAnatvameva | yathA hi | kShetropAdAnakAnAmapi sasyAnAM kR^iShIvala eva svAmI na kShetraM tathaiva | nacha vAchyaM manasa eva kAmasvAmitvamahaM kAmaya ityanubhavastu bhrAntirvyavahAramAtraM veti | bAdhakapramANAbhAvAt.h | nacha kauTasthyaM bAdhakam.h | antaHkaraNasyaiva kAmopAdAnatvenAN^gIkR^itatvAt.h | svAmitvamAtreNa cha kauTasthyAvighAtAt.h | anyathA kR^ipaNadhanasyevAtmano vaiyarthyApatteriti | tadidamuktaM kvachiditi | nanvastu kAmasvAmitvamAtmana eva mA bhUchcha manasaH | tathA.api pUrvottaravirodhastadavastha eva | ichChAsvAmitvAbhAve.api yAdR^ishatAdR^ishasyechChAvattvasya manasyaN^gIkR^itattvAdityata Aha- ichCheti ||
achetanechChApagatetyAdAvichChAsvAmitvamevechChAvattvamuktam.h | nachAparamichChopAdAnatvalakShaNam.h | etaduktaM bhavati | syAdatra pUrvAparavirodhaH | yadi yadevechChAvattvaM prAN^manaso niShiddhaM tadevAtra punaraN^gIkriyeta | na chaitadasti | pUrvaM hIchChAsvAmitvalakShaNamichChAvattvamAtmana eva na tvachetanasyetyuktam.h | tasyaiva kartR^itvopayogAt.h | shrutyarthatayA tvichChopAdAnatvalakShaNamichChAvatvamidAnIM manaso.abhyupagamyata iti kuto virodha iti |
yadvA kAmasya dvaividhyena manaso.api kAmavattvAtkatarR^itvamupapatsyata ityata Aha- dvaividhye.apIti || dvayoH kAmavattve.api kAmasvAmitvamAtmana eva na tu manasaH | nirapavAdasAkShyanubhavasiddhatvAt.h | manasastu kAmopAdAnatvameveti | tataH kimityata Aha- ichCheti || ichChAsvAmitvalakShaNamevechChAvattvaM prAk.h kartR^itvopayuktamuktam.h | na punarichChopAdAnatvalakShaNam.h | yo hIchChati sa prayatate na tu yadichChA bhavati taditi | tasmAdichChAsvAmitvAchchetanasyaiva kartR^itvaM nAchetanasya | tasyechChopAdAnatve.apIchChAsvAmitvAbhAvAditi |
syAdetat.h | svaM nAma tadbhavati, yadyatheShyaviniyogayogyam.h | yathA gavAdi | svAmI cha sa uchyate yo yatheShyaviniyoktA | nachechChAtmanoretadasti | yasmAdAstikakAmukasya niShiddhechChAM niyachChato.api (ichChA)sA.a.avirbhavati | prayatamAnasyApi 
vihitechChA nodeti | tatkathamichChAsvAmitvamAtmanaH syAditi chet.h | kimichChA.a.atmanaH sarvathApi vashA na bhavati ityuchyate | uta kiJNchidvashatvamaN^gIkriyate | nAdyaH | anubhavavirodhAt.h | ichChati devadatta ityAdivyavahAravirahaprasaN^gAchcha | dvitIye tu siddhaM svAmitvamityAha- kiJNchiditi ||
prabalavirodhivashAdatyantavashatvAbhAve.apIchChAyAH kiJNchidAtmavashatvamAtreNApi tAM pratyAtmanaH svAmitvaM bhavede(vatye)va | katham.h | yathA.atyantamavashAyAmapi gavi kiJNchidvashatvamAtreNa devadattasvAmitvaM loke dR^iShyaM tathaiva | anyathA tadapi na syAditi | 
nanvevaM satyekaM sandhi(di)tsato (paraM prachya)nyachchyavata ityApannam.h | achetanasya kartR^itvaM nirAkartumAtmana evechChAsvAmitvaM natu manasa iti samarthitam.h | tarhIshvarasyApi kulAlAdimanovR^ittIchChAM prati svAmitvaM nAstIti ghaTAdikartR^itvaM na syAt.h | tathAchetaravyapadeshAdityadhikaraNavirodhaityata Aha- sarvAtmeti ||
yadA jIvasyApi kAmAdisvAmyaM tadA sarvAtmanA tantramadhInaM kAmAdi yasyAsau tathoktaH | sarveShAmAtmanAM tantraM sAdhanaM yaH kAmastasyAdiH kAraNaM tasya pareshituH kAmasvAmitvaM kimutaiva vaktavyam.h | etaduktaM bhavati | jIveshvarau dvAvapi sharIramadhitiShThataH | tatreshvaro.antaHkaraNaM spaShyaM dR^iShTvA tatra j~nAnechChAprayatnarUpA vR^ittIH svechChAj~nAnaprayatnairutpAdya bAhyakaraNAni chAdhiShThAya ghaTAdyutpAdayati | jIvastu taddattasvAmyo.avatiShThate | yathoktaM "baddhirj~nAnam.h' ityAdi | tasmAdIshvarasyaiva mukhyaM svAmyaM kartR^itvaM cha | jIvasya tvamukhyameveti | tathA choktam.h "svasvAmibhAvo dhruva eSha yatra tarhyachyute.asAviti kR^ityayoge' iti | 
yaduktaM nirapavAdAnubhavabalAdAtmana evechChAsvAmitvamiti | tadayuktam.h | kAmaH saN^kalpa iti manasaH kAmasvAmitvAbhidhAtyA.apauruSheyatvena balavatyA vedavAchaivApoditatvAdityata Aha- nacheti ||
kAmasvAmitvamAtmana iti sheShaH | kAmAdyanuvAdena khalviyaM vedavAk.h AtmopAdAnatvaM vaisheShikAdimataprAptaM vArayituM teShAM manorUpatvamAchaShye | kAmAdisvarUpaM cha sAkShyanubhavenaiva siddhamiti tasyopajIvyatvam.h | sa cha tAnAtmasvAmikAneva viShayIkaroti | nachopajIvyakamupajIvyamapavadituM shaknoti | vedasyotsargato balavattve.apyupajIvyApekShayA daurbalyameva | yathA AhuH | "prAbalyamAgamasyaiva jAtyA teShu triShu smR^itam.h | upajIvyavirodhe tu na prAmANyamamuShya cha' iti | ato na shruteranubhavApavAdakatvaM yuktamiti |
tarhi shruteH kA gatirityata Aha- tasmAditi |
upajIvyatvena balavatA.anubhavena bAdhitatvAdityarthaH | tadanyAbhidhAyinI svAmitvAdanyasyopAdAnatvasyAbhidhAyinI | 
na kevalamupajIvyabAdhAt.h | kintUpapattivirodhAchchetyAha- mokShakAma iti ||
yadi kAmo.antaHkaraNakartR^ikaH syAttadA mokShakAmo.apyantaHkaraNasyaiva syAt.h | mokShastu Atmana iti cha prasiddham.h | tathAcha yo mukto bhaviShyati tasmAdanya eva mokShakAma itayuktaM syAt.h | kAmasyAnyagatatve sAdhanAnuShThAtA.apyanya evetyaN^gIkartavyam.h | phalakAmanAsAdhanAnuShThAnayorekaniShThatvadR^iShyeH | tathAchAkR^itAbhyAgamakR^itavipraNashaprasaN^gaH | 
nanu nAyaM doShaH | puruShavimokShArthaM prakR^itipravR^ittyabhyupagamAt.h | dR^ishyate hi paraprayojanArthaM janAnAM pravR^ittiriti | atredamupatiShThate- mokShakAmasyeti ||
upalakShaNametat.h | sAdhanAnuShThAtetyapi draShyavyam.h | paraprayojanArtaM pravatarmAnAH khalu loke dR^iShyamadR^iShyaM vA kimapi prayojanamanusandadhAnAH prAyeNopalabdhAH | tathA.atrApi prakR^iteH prayojanena bhAvyam.h | nacha tadastItyarthaH | 
syAdetat.h | svaprayojanamananusandhAyaiva jIvamokShArthaM prakR^iteH pravR^ittiH, yatA kR^ipAlutvena bhavatAmIshvarasyetyata Aha- svanAshArthaM cheti ||
na kevalaM paraprayojanArthA prakR^iteH pravR^ittiryujyate | prakR^itilayo hi mokSho nAma | na hi ko.api kR^ipAlurAtmanAshArthaM yatamAno dR^iShya iti | yadyapyatrAnAdheyAtishayasya niShkriyasyopakAryatvamapi kvachinna dR^iShyamityeva vaktavyam.h | tathA.api tachChiShyairevohyatAmiti tadabhyupagamena dUShaNAntaramidamuktam.h |
nanvidamayuktam.h | chetano hi svaprayojanamanusandadhyAt.h | svanAshAchcha bibhyat.h parAvarteta | prakR^itistvachetanA kathamevaM paryanuyogamarhatIti | evaM tarhi kathamAtmamokShamapyanusandhAya pravarteta | svabhAvo.ayaM pradhAnasyeti chet.h | tarhi kadA.api saMsAro.asya na syAt.h | bhogArthA pravR^ittiH prakR^iteH svabhAva iti chet.h | tarhi mokShAbhAvaH | ubhayasvabhAvatve tUbhayaM na syAt.h | virodhAt.h | avirodhe vA yugapadubhayaM syAt.h | vyavasthApakAbhAvAt.h | bhogeShUpabhukteShu mokShArtheti chenna | 
bhogAnAmAnantyenAparisamApteriti |
ayaM prasaN^gAtharH | yadyAtmA na kAmakartA syAttadA mumukShurapi na syAt.h | tatashcha na tadarthaM prayateta | tathAcha na muchyeta | parapravR^itteH svaprayojanabhAvAbhAvayorayuktatvAditi | bahulametannidarshanamiti smaraNAdyatediti parasmaipadam.h | tathAchAha "chandrAdayastu manyante sarvasmAdubhayaM padam.h' iti |
evamanIshvarasAN^khayamataM sAdhAraNadUShaNairapAkR^itya ye kartR^itvaM prakR^itereva bhoktR^itvaM tvAtmana iti manyante tanmataM dUShayati- kartR^itvamiti ||
yadvaivamAtmanaH kartR^itvamupapAdya bhoktR^itvamapyanenaivopapAdayati | yena mayedaM kR^itaM sa evAhaM tatphalaM bhuJNja iti kartR^itvabhoktR^itvayoH sAmAnAdhikaraNyAnubhavAttayadvaiyadhikaraNyAN^gIkAre.anubhavavirodha ityarthaH | 
bhrAnto.ayamanubhava iti chenna | bAdhakAbhAvAdityAha- vibhAge cheti ||
yaduktamAtmano mokSho na syAditi | tadiShyApAdanam.h | prakR^itereva mokShAbhyupagamAt.h | nacha bandhamokShayorvaiyadhikaraNyAnupapattiH | bandhasyApi prakR^itigatatvAditi chenna | sakalashrutismR^itIhAsapurANAnubhavairbandhamokShayerAtmagatatvAvagamena tadvirodhAdityAshayavAnupasaMharati- sarveti ||
sarvamAnavirodha eva yA pradhAnadurdIkShA duShyo.anuShThAnasaN^kalpaH | tayA dIkShito.ayaM tu sAN^khayo mAyAvAdinAmupamAtvaM prApnuyAt.h | te.api hi kartR^itvabhoktR^itvAdisakaladharmavikalamasatkalpaM chaitanyamAtramaN^gIkR^ityAvidyAyA evAchetanAyAH sarvakAraNatvaM bandhamokShAdhikaraNatvaM chAbhyupagachChanti | tadeteShAM sarvapramANaviruddhArthAN^gIkAritve sAN^khayo.ayaM dR^iShyAntabhAvamApadyata iti | 
yatpuruShabahutvaM sAN^khayenAN^gIkR^itaM tadapi mAyAvAdibhirabhyupagatameva | jananAdiprakR^itidharmaireva hi tadbahutvam.h | natu svarUpe kashchidasti parasparato visheShaH | mAyAvAdino.api upAdhinibandhanaM bhedamaN^gIkurvantyeva | nacha prapaJNchasatyatvaM visheShaH | kAraNamAtratvAbhyupagamena kAyarprapaJNchasya sAN^khayena nirastatvAditi |
yA.api sAN^khayaparikalpitA sR^iShyipralayabandhamokShatatsAdhanaprakriyA sA.api sarvapramANaviruddhetyuktaM bhavati |
na kevalaM sAN^khayasya mAyAvAdisadR^ishatvamasmAbhirevochyate, kintu sUtrakR^itA.api sUchitamityAha- taditi ||
tasmAnmAyAvAdisadR^ishatvAdeva hi sAN^khayo bhoktrApatteravibhAgashchetsyAllokavaditi prAk.h parAkR^itena mAyAvAdinA rachanAnupapatteshcha nAnumAnamiti chashabdena samuchchitya nirAkR^itaH | yadvA pramANavirodho.api notsUtrita ityanenAha | tasmAtsarvamAnavirodhitvAdeva | chashabdAtsarvamAnavirodhasamuchchayAtharM chashabdaM prakShipyetyarthaH | 
|| iti shrImannyAyasudhAyAM rachanAnupapattyadhikaraNam.h || 
|| atha shrImannyAyasudhAyAM anyatrAbhAvAdhikaraNam.h || 
|| OM anyatrAbhAvAchcha na tR^iNAdivat.h OM || idaM sUtraM kechiditthaM vyAchakShate | yathA tR^iNapallavAdikaM gavAdinopabhuktaM svayameva kShIrIbhavati | evaM pradhAnaM svayameva mahadAdirUpeNa pariNamata ityAshaN^kA kilAtra nirasyate | na tR^iNAdivatsvayameva pradhAnasya pariNAmo vaktavyaH | yatastR^iNAdInAmapi svayameva pariNAmo nAsti | kutaH | anyatrAnaDuhopabhukte tadabhAvAditi | atrAshaN^kaiva tAvadanupapannA | payo.ambuvachchettatrApItyanenaiva parihR^itatvAt.h | pratyudAharaNaM cha sUtrapraNayanAyogAt.h | parihAro.apyayamanupapannaH | gavAdyupabhuktasyaiva kShIratvaM nAnyatreti hi vadatA prakR^iteH sahakArisadbhAvamAtramupapAditaM syAt.h | na punarIshvarApekShatvam.h | ato nAyaM sUtrArthaH | kintu pAtaJNjalamatamatrAdhikaraNe nirAkriyata ityAshayavAMstadupanyasyati- sAN^khayAnAmiti ||
sAN^khayamatasya nirastatvAtkiM punarupanyAsenetyato.asya matasya tato visheShaM tushabdena sUchayati | tameva visheShaM vyanakti- seshvara iti || seshvarashchenna nirAkAryo virodhAbhAvAdityata uktam.h- kShetreti || tushabdo.avadhAraNArtho.atrApyanvIyate | yadyapi seshvara ityanenaiveshvaro.astIti brUta iti siddham.h | tathA.api tadanuvAdena visheShaNavidhAnamevaitat.h | ya Ishvaro.asti sa kShetrAnugrahashaktimAneveti brUta iti | kShiyantyasminkAyarANyavyaktatayeti kShetramupAdAnaM prakR^itiH | tadanugrahashaktireveshvarasya tenAbhyupagamyate | ato nirAkaraNIya evAsAviti | sarvashaktitvAbhAve kiM tasyeshvaratvamityata uktam.h- svayambhAta iti || svayamindriyAdyanapekShameva bhAtaH | kartari ktaH | tatashcha sarvaj~na iti labhyate | IshvaratvopapAdakaM visheShaNAntaramAha- klesheti || kleshakarmavipAkAshayavarjita ityarthaH | tathAchAha pataJNjaliH | "kleshakarmavipAkashayairaparAmR^iShyaH puruShavisheSha IshvaraH' iti | tathA "nirmANakAyamadhiShThAya sampradAyapravartako.anugrAhakashcha' iti | tatrAvidyA.asmitArAgadveShAbhiniveshAH paJNcha kleshAH | 
anAtmanyAtmabuddhiravidyA | idaM madIyamityabhimAno.asmitA | viShayeShvAsaktI rAgaH | kopo dveShaH | bhayamabhiniveshaH | eta eva paJNcha kleshAstantrAntare tamo moho mahAmohAH tAmisro.andhatAmisra iti vyavahriyante | vArShagaNyastvenAnavidyetyevAha | karmeti vidhiniShedhAvuchyete | Ashayashabdena dharmAdharmau | vipAka iti tatphalaM sukhaduHkhe tadupAyashcheti | itishabdasya AgAminaH prativAkyaM sambandhaH | 
vedavAdavirodhaM sphuTIkartumavadhAraNavyAvartyamAha- kShetreti ||
yA jagadupAdAnaM sA prakR^itirevopAdAnatvashaktimatI brUte | na punarvedavAdina iva tAmapi shaktimIshvarAyattAm.h | vyAvartyAntaramAha- bIjeti || 
atrApyeveti sambaddhayate | sharIrendriyAdisambandhenotpattau yA shaktiH sA bIjashaktiH | jIva eva tadvAniti brUte | natu tadIyAM bIjashaktiM tattva(vAdina)vida iva bhagavadadhInAm.h | yadyupAdAnatvotpattishaktimattvaM prakR^itipuruShayoreva tadA kimIshvareNAnugrAhakeNetyata Aha- parjanyavaditi || yathA hi pR^ithivyAH kalamAdibIjAnAM chopAdAnatvabIjatvashaktI yadyapi svAyatte | tathA.apyaN^kurotpattau parjanyasyAsti pR^ithivyanu(grahakAraka)grAhakatvam.h | tathA prakR^itipuruShayoH svAyattashaktitve.apIshvaraH prakR^ityanugrahashaktimAnaN^gIkaraNIyaH | 
tatkiM parjanyavadanvayavyatirekAbhyAmIshvarasya prakR^ityanugrAhakatvamavaseyaM netyAha- daiveti || 
daivashabdo.adR^iShyasvarUpatvamAha | tenAnvayavyatirekAviShayatvaM lakShayati | tatkiM niShpramANaka eveshvaraH prakR^ityanugrAhako.aN^gIkaraNIya ityata uktam.h- smR^ita iti || "mAyA.adhyakSheNa prakR^itiH sUyate sacharAcharam.h' ityAdAviti sheShaH | smR^ita ityupalakShaNam.h | shruta ityapi grAhyam.h | 
prakR^itipuruShayoH svAyattashaktitvaM kuta ityata Aha- pR^ithivIvaditi ||
yathA pR^ithivyAH svAyattopAdanatvashaktiH tathA tat.h tasmAdupAdAnatvAtpradhAnamapi svAyattopAdAnatvashaktimadanumeyamityarthaH | upalakShaNaM chaitat.h | kalamAdibIjavadbIjatvAjjIvo.api svAyattabIjashaktimAnanumAtavya ityapi draShyavyam.h | 
nanu yathA loke kalamAdibIjAnAM kashchidAvapanakartAsti | tathA.atrApi tatsthAnIyena kenApi bhAvyam.h | nachAsAvanyo.asti parameshvarAt.h | tatkathaM kShetrAnugrahashaktimAneveshvara ityata Aha- jIva iti ||
dR^ishyate khalvapatyajIvo bIjabhUtaH | pitR^ijIvashchAvapanakartR^isthAnIyaH | tasmAtkimIshvarasya tachChaktikalpanayA | viShayotpattau tu tadapekShaiva nAstIti bhAvaH | nanvevaM pitR^ijIvasyApatyotpAdakatvAN^gIkAre.apasiddhAntaH syAt.h | sAN^khayairjIvasya kartR^itvAnabhyupagamAdityata uktam.h- sannidhimAtrata iti || sharIrAdirUpA prakR^itirevApatyo(tpatti)tpAdakatrI | tatsannidhinimittAdvivekAgrahAjjIve tatkartR^itvavyavahAra eveti brUta iti | 
evamupyastamatanirAsArthaM sUtramavatArayati- atreti ||
atraitanmataviShaye dUShaNaM prAhetyatharH | svayaM sAkShAnnopachAreNa | prabhuriti sUtrakR^ito dUShaNasAmarthyamAchaShye | sUtraM vyAchaShye- anyatreti ||
anyatra prakR^itau puruShe | tathA pR^ithivyAM kalamAdibIje cha | kA.apIti kShetrashaktirbIjashaktirbIjAvapanashaktishchetyarthaH | kathaM tarhyupAdAnatvAdikamityata uktam.h- svAtanteNeti || kuto nAstItyata Aha- Isheti ||
yasmAdIsha eva tAH pradhAnAdishaktIH prerayatIti shrutyAdiprasiddham.h | tasmAdanyatra kA.api shaktiH svAtantyeNa nAstIti | nacha pradhAnAdivadIshvarasyApi preraNAshaktiH parAyattetyuktam.h- aJNja iti || kriyAvisheShaNametat.h | tadanena parakIyAnumAnasya bAdhitaviShayatvaM dR^iShyAntasya cha sAdhyavikalatvamuktaM bhavati | 
na kevalaM prakR^itipuruShayoH svAtanteNa shaktyabhAvaH parameshvarAyattashaktitvaM cha | kiM tarhItyatashchashabdasamuchchitamarthamAha- tadadhInAshcheti || 
AdyashchashabdaH shaktiprerakatvasya sattAdipradatvena saha samuchchayArthaH | uttarAvanyonyasamuchchaye | pradhAnapuruShayostadIyAnAM shaktInAM cha, sattA svarUpaM, pratItayashcha pramAviShayatvaM cheti yAvat.h, tAstAH sarvAH pravR^ittayashcha sarvadA tadadhInA iti yojanA | kechinmanyante svarUpameva vastunaH sattvamiti, apare tu pramANayogyatvam.h, anye punararthakriyAvattvam.h | tadidaM trayamapi prakR^ityAdInAM bhagavadadhInameveti |
nanvetadayuktam.h | pradhAnAdisattAdenirtyatvAt.h | nityasya parAdhInatA.asambhavAdityata Aha- nityamiti ||
yathA.anityaM ghaTAdikamanityatayA niyamyate, tathA nityamapi nityAtmanA nityaM cha sarvadaiveshvaro niyAmayati | yata evaM tasmAduktamupapannamiti yojanA | 
etaduktaM bhavati | yathA hi ghaTAdayo.anitya(ttva)svabhAvA api nAkasmAdanityA bhavanti | ko doShaH | na chAnityatA parAdhIneti kadAchidghaTAdenirtyatA prAptA | vinAshakAraNopanipAtaghrauvyAt.h | tathA nityasya nityatAyAH parAdhInatve.atrapa na jAtvanityatAprasaktiH | tanniyamananiyamAditi | tadidamuktam.h- nityaM cheti || na chaitadalaukikam.h | nityakarmabhirduritaprAgabhAvAnuvR^itteH sAdhyatvena vAdibhirabhyupagatatvAt.h | anuvR^itternityatApAdanAnatirekAt.h | bhavedetade(vama)svarasanityasya | na svarasanityasyeti chenna | IshvarAtiriktasya tadbhAvAsammateH | iyAMstu visheShaH | kiJNchidasmadAyattanityatvam.h | kiJNchichcheshvarAyattanityatvamiti | tadapyasmAsu kasmAnnAyatate tathAbhUtaM cha kathamIshvarAdhInamityata uktam.h- nityashaktyeti || pradhAnAdishakteH prakR^itatvAt.h tadgrahaNamidamiti mandAshaN^kAM vArayituM svayetyuktam.h | 
yaduktaM pradhAnAderupAdAnatvAdishaktirna svAdhInA kintvIshvarapreritaiveti | tatkuta ityata Aha- neti ||
"na R^ite tvatkriyate kiJNchanAre' iti shruteH | prAguktaM pratipattavyamiti sheShaH | shaktireva hi kriyochyate | 
yatpradhAnAdisattAderbhagavadadhInatvamuktaM tasya sambhAvanaivoktA | pramANaM tu tatra kimityata Aha- svabhAveti || 
karmashabdena dharmAdhamarvyaktayo gR^ihyante | kriyAH parispandAH | shrutiH vedaH | santIti trividhamapi sattvaM vivakShitam.h | sattAdyAH pradhAnAdeH | nArAyaNaM vinA tatpreraNAM vinA | 
tasmAdanyatropAdAnatvAdishakterabhAvAt.h, tatsattAderapIshvarAyattatvAchcha, na, tR^iNAdInAmutpattau parjanyasyeva pR^ithivyanugrAhakatvaM, Ishvarasya mahadAdyutpattau kShetrAnugrAhakatvamAtram.h, kintu sarvasvAtantyameva, iti, yadanyadabhyupagataM pAtaJNjalairvaidikamataviruddhaM, tatsarvaM prathamAdhikaraNa eva nirastam.h | kiM punaH prayatnenetyAshayavAnpUvarmatena sahaitasya hetAmupasaMharati- taditi ||
vindhyo.anIshvaraH sAN^khayaH | Adipadena tadekadeshinAM paJNchashikheshvarakR^iShNAdInAM grahaNam.h | tadavAntaramatayorapi nirastatvAt.h | yadvA pataJNjalivindhyAvAdI yasya tattathoktam.h | pataJNjalinA.aN^gIkR^ito.apIshvaro anI(nirI)shvarakalpa eva | ataH pUrvasyAsya cha sAmyAbhiprAyeNa vA sahopasaMhAra iti |
|| iti shrImannyAyasudhAyAM anyatrAbhAvAdhikaraNam.h ||
|| atha shrImannyAyasudhAyAM abhyupagamAdhikaraNam.h ||
|| OM abhyupagame.apyarthAbhAvAt.h OM || kechididaM satramevaM vyAchakShate | prAk.h pradhAnasya pravR^ittirnopapadyata ityuktam.h | athedAnIM pravR^itterabhyupagame.api tasyAH prayejanAbhAvAditi | tadayuktam.h | abhyupagame.apItyetAvato vaiyarthyAt.h | arthAbhAvAchchetyetAvataiva pUrNatvAt.h | kiJNcha arthAbhAvena kiM sAdhyam.h | sAN^khayamatasyAsAmaJNjasyaM vA prakR^iteH pravR^ittyanupapattirvA | nAdyaH | vyadhikaraNatvAt.h | kathaJNchidekAdhikaraNatApAdane.api svamatenAnaikAntyAt.h | na dvitIyaH | abhyupagama(vAda)virodhAt.h | na hyabhyupagamavAde.api yadevAbhyupagamyate tadeva nirAkriyate | anAsthAM khalu tAtkAlikImabhyupagamena dyotayanti | yathA.astu shabdo nityo.anityo vA, anushAsanaM tAvatkartavyamiti | tasmAnnAyaM sUtrArthaH | 
kinnAma mA bhUdachetanasya kartR^itvaM, sharIrasyaiva chetanAvattvena katarR^itvopapatteH | kimIshvarAdinetyadhikAshaN^kayA pratyavatiShThamAnasya chArvAkasya matamatrAdhikaraNe nirasyata iti bhAvena tanmatamupanyasyati- chArvAkairiti ||
chArvI buddhistatsambandhAdAchAryo.api chArvI | tasyeme ChAtrAshchArvAkAH | tairakShajaM mAnamuchyate | nanvetadasmAkamapi sammatamityataH sAvadhAraNamidamuktamityAshayenoktaM vivR^iNoti- nAparamiti || anumAnamAgamashcha mAnaM nochyata ityarthaH | etadapyasmAkamanumatameva | prameyavisheShe pratyakShasyaiva mAnatA.abhyupagamAdityata Aha- kvachiditi ||
etaduktaM bhavati | pramANAdhInA hi prameyasiddhiH | pramANaM cha pratyakShameva | nAto.anyadasti | nacha pratyakSheNeshvaraM pratImaH | tasmAtpramANAbhAvAnnAstIshvara iti |
nanu yadi pratyakShAtiriktaM na pramANaM tadA dharmamokShayostatsAdhanAnAM cha pratyakShAviShayANAmasiddhiH syAdityata Aha- deha iti ||
j~nAnavAnkhalvAtmanA | j~nAnaM cha dehadharmaH | yathoktam.h- "pR^ithivyApastejovAyuriti tattvAni | tatsamudAye sharIrendriyaviShayasaMj~nA | tebhyashchaitanyaM madashaktivadvij~nAnam.h' iti | tasmAddeha evAtmA | sa cha vinAshItyataH kAlAntarabhAvinaH puMsa evAbhAvAddharmamokShAkhyapuruShArthAbhAvo nAniShyaH | puruShArthau tu kAmArthAveva | puruShAnvayasambhavAditi | tatrApi kAma eva 
mukhyo.arthastu tatsAdhanatayaiva pumartha iti j~nApayituM kAmasyAdau saN^kIrtanam.h | iti chochyata iti sambandhaH | 
etanmatanirAsArthaM sUtraM vyAkhyAtumupodghAtaM tAvadAha- yadevamiti ||
yadyevamatIndriyaM vastu na syAt.h tadA tadIyaM shAstraM viShayaprayojanashUnyamApadyeteti sheShaH | tatkathamiti chet.h | kimanena shAstreNa tatpraNetA viShayaM pratipadyate prayojanaM cha labhate | uta vineyA narAH | 
AdyaM dUShayati- darshaneneti ||
kimAkShepe | artho viShayaH prayojanaM cha | labdha upalabdhaH prAptashcha | pratyakShagocharo hIti | tatra hetuH | tatashchAyamarthaH | na tAvadanena shAstreNa shAstrapraNetrA.astIndriyo.arthaH upalabhyate | tadabhAvAt.h | nApyaindriyakaH | tasya pratyakShagocharatvena viShayatvAnupapatteH | "aprApte hi shAstramarthavat.h' | kiJNcha pratyakSheNa tamarthamupalabhya khalvasau shAstre pravINavAn.h | anyathA (tatpra)praNayanAnupapatteH | tathAcha taM prati tamevArthamupadarshayatkathaM saviShayaM syAt.h | evaM prayojanamapi na tAvadatIndriyam.h | tadabhAvAt.h | nApyaindriyakam.h | tasya yogyAnupala(bdhi)mbhabAdhitatvAt.h | nanu hitopadeShyari jano.anurajyate | "janAnurAgaprabhavAshcha sampadaH' iti chet.h | kR^itaghnatAnimittapratyavAyAnusandhAne satyevametat.h | tattu pareNa tyAjitamiti | 
dvitIyaM dUShayati- narairiti ||
labdhamityanuvartate | atrApi pUrvavaduttaram.h | syAdetat.h | dharmAdyatIndriyAbhimatArthAbhAvaH shAstrasya viShayaH | tasya pratyakShatve.api vaidikavAsanAnimittashaN^kAkalaN^kitatvena viShayatvamupapadyate | prayojanaM cha dharmAdharmashaN^koparuddhArthakAmopabhogaH | tatkathaM naraiH shAstrAtkiM labdhamityuchyate | maivam.h | viShayapratipattau hi prayojanAvAptiH | viShayaM cha kiM shAstramAptavAkyatayA pratipAdayet.h utopapattivyutpAdanena | nAdyaH | AgamaprAmANyAbhyupagamaprasaN^gAt.h | nAsti atIndriyaM kimapItyetAvataiva pUrNatve(naiva)na vAkyavistaravaiyarthyAchcha | na dvitIyaH | upapattiprAmANyAbhyupagamaprasaN^gAt.h | shAstraM shaN^kAmeva nivArayati | viShayapratipattistu pratyakSheNaiveti chenna | svayaM vopapattivyutpAdanena vA kamapyarthamanupadarshayataH shaN^kAnivAraNAsAmarthyAt.h | shaN^kA hi saMshayo vA syAdviparyayo vA | dvAvapi viparItArthagocharabalavatpratyayanirasanIyau | nAj~nAmAtreNa | tarkavyutpAdanaM shAstreNa kriyata iti chet.h(na) | tasyApi pramANatvAt.h | tadidaM "darshanena' iti prakR^itAnuvR^ittau satyAM "shAstrAtkim.h' itrata vadatA sUchitam.h | anyathA naraishchetyavakShyat.h | mohanaM vinetyubhayavAkyasheShaH parihAsaH | shAstrapraNetrA suraguruNA.ayogyajanavyAmohanaM prayojanaM labdham.h | anyaishcha mithyAj~nAnam.h | nAto.adhikamiti |
kimato yadyevamityata Aha- sveti ||
niShphalaM shAstramiti vakShyamANaM siMhAvalo(kananyAye)kitenAnuvartate | tachchopalakShaNam.h | nirviShayaM chetyapi draShyavyam.h | viShayaprayojanavattvaM hi svaparaviShayaprayojanavattayA vyAptam.h | tR^itIyaprakArAbhAvAt.h | sarvaprakAraparityAgena sAmAnyAnavasthAnAt.h | tatashcha vyApikAyAH svaparaviShayaprayojanavattAyA abhAvAttadvayAptaM viShayaprayojanavattvamapi nAstItyarthaH | 
astvevaM viShayaprayojanashUnyamasmadIyaM shAstram.h | tataH kimityataH sUtraM vyAkhyAti- svamatenaiveti || 
yata evaM svamatenaiva niShphalaM nirviShayaM cha na kevalaM paropapAdanameva | tasmAd.h vR^ithA viShayaprayojanashUnyam.h | yasmAdvAdinA chArvAkeNa prativAdibhishcha taditaraiH sarvairviShayaprayojanashUnyatayA.abhyupagatam.h | tasmAdviShayaprayojanashUnya(meve)tyarthaH | yasmAdvR^ithA tasmAttachChAstraM kimiti svayaM prekShAvAnpralapati | prekShAvatA nArambhaNIyamiti yAvat.h | viShayaprayojanashUnyaM chArabhamANo na laukiko nApi parIkShaka ityunmattavadupekShaNIyaH syAditi | yadvA niShphalamiti prayojanAbhAvAbhidhAnam.h | vR^itheti viShayAbhAvavachanam.h | tathAchaivaM sUtrayojanA | na kevalaM paropapAdanena kintu svAbhyupagame.apyarthAbhAvAdanArambhaNIyaM shAstramiti sheSha iti | arthAbhAvahetorasiddhiparihArAyAbhyupagame.apItyuktam.h |  Vyasa-(23)
